Your Lord is All-Forgiving, full of mercy. Had He wished to take them to task for their doings, He would have hastened in sending His scourge upon them. But He has set for them a time-limit which they cannot evade.

# 2199

All the townships afflicted with scourge are before your eyes. When they committed wrong, We destroyed them. For the destruction of each We had set a definite term.

# 2200

(And recount to them the story of Moses) when Moses said to his servant: "I will journey on until I reach the point where the two rivers meet, though I may march on for ages."

# 2201

But when they reached the point where the two rivers meet, they forgot their fish, and it took its way into the sea, as if through a tunnel.

# 2202

When they had journeyed further on, Moses said to his servant: "Bring us our repast. We are surely fatigued by today's journey."

# 2203

The servant said: "Did you see what happened? When we betook ourselves to the rock to take rest, I forgot the fish - and it is only Satan who caused me to forget to mention it to you - so that it made its way into the sea in a strange manner."

# 2204

Moses said: "That is what we were looking for." So the two turned back, retracing their footsteps,

# 2205

and there they found one of Our servants upon whom We had bestowed Our mercy, and to whom We had imparted a special knowledge from Ourselves.

# 2206

Moses said to him: "May l follow you that you may teach me something of the wisdom which you have been taught?"

# 2207

He answered: "You will surely not be able to bear with me.

# 2208

For how can you patiently bear with something you cannot encompass in your knowledge?"

# 2209

Moses replied: "You shall find me, if Allah wills, patient; and I shall not disobey you in anything."

# 2210

He said: "Well, if you follow me, do not ask me concerning anything until I myself mention it to you."

# 2211

Then the two went forth until, when they embarked on the boat, he made a hole in it, whereupon Moses exclaimed: "Have you made a hole in it so as to drown the people in the boat? You have certainly done an awful thing."

# 2212

He replied: "Did I not tell you that you will not be able to patiently bear with me?"

# 2213

Moses said: "Do not take me to task at my forgetfulness, and do not be hard on me."

# 2214

Then the two went forth until they met a lad whom he slew, whereupon Moses exclaimed: "What! Have you slain an innocent person without his having slain anyone? Surely you have done a horrible thing."

# 2215

He said: "Did I not tell you that you will not be able to patiently bear with me?"

# 2216

Moses said: "Keep me no more in your company if I question you concerning anything after this. You will then be fully justified."

# 2217

Then the two went forth until when they came to a town, they asked its people for food, but they refused to play host to them. They found in that town a wall that was on the verge of tumbling down, and he buttressed it, whereupon Moses said: "If you had wished, you could have received payment for it."

# 2218

He said: "This brings me and you to a parting of ways. Now I shall explain to you the true meaning of things about which you could not remain patient.

# 2219

As for the boat it belonged to some poor people who worked on the river, and I desired to damage it for beyond them lay the dominion of a king who was wont to seize every boat by force.

# 2220

As for the lad, his parents were people of faith, and we feared lest he should plague them with transgression and disbelief,

# 2221

and we desired that their Lord should grant them another in his place, a son more upright and more tender hearted.

# 2222

As for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the city, and under it there was a treasure that belonged to them. Their father was a righteous man and your Lord intended that they should come of age and then bring forth their treasure as a mercy from your Lord; I did not do this of my own bidding. This is the true meaning of things with which you could not keep your patience."

# 2223

(O Muhammad), they ask you about Dhu al-Qarnayn. Say: "I will give you an account of him."

# 2224

We granted him power in the land and endowed him with all kinds of resources.

# 2225

He set out (westwards) on an expedition,

# 2226

until when he reached the very limits where the sun sets, he saw it setting in dark turbid waters; and nearby he met a people. We said: "O Dhu al-Qarnayn, you have the power to punish or to treat them with kindness."

# 2227

He said: "We will chastise him who does wrong, whereafter he will be returned to his Lord and He will chastise him grievously.

# 2228

But as for him who believes and acts righteously, his will be a goodly reward and we shall enjoin upon him only mild commands."

# 2229

Then he set out on another expedition

# 2230

until he reached the limit where the sun rises and he found it rising on a people whom We had provided no shelter from it.

# 2231

Thus was the state of those people, and We encompassed in knowledge all concerning Dhu al- Qarnayn.

# 2232

Then he set out on another expedition

# 2233

until when he reached a place between the two mountains, he found beside the mountains a people who scarcely understood anything.

# 2234

They said: "O Dhu al-Qarnayn, Gog and Magog are spreading corruption in this land. So shall we pay you taxes on the understanding that you will set up a barrier between us and them?"

# 2235

He answered: "Whatever my Lord has granted me is good enough. But help me with your labour and I will erect a rampart between you and them.

# 2236

Bring me ingots of iron." Then after he had filled up the space between the two mountain-sides, he said: "(Light a fire) and ply bellows." When he had made it (red like) fire, he said: "Bring me molten copper which I may pour on it."

# 2237

Such was the rampart that Gog and Magog could not scale, nor could they pierce it.

# 2238

Dhu al-Qarnayn said: "This is a mercy from my Lord: but when the time of my Lord's promise shall come, He will level the rampart with the ground. My Lord's promise always comes true."

# 2239

And on that Day We shall let some of them surge like waves against others, and the Trumpet shall be blown. Then We shall gather them all together.

# 2240

That will be the Day We shall place Hell before the unbelievers

# 2241

whose eyes had become blind against My admonition and who were utterly disinclined to hear it.

# 2242

Do the unbelievers, then, believe that they can take any of My creatures as their guardians beside Me? Verily We have prepared Hell to welcome the unbelievers.

# 2243

Say, (O Muhammad): "Shall We tell you who will be the greatest losers in respect of their works?

# 2244

It will be those whose effort went astray in the life of the world and who believe nevertheless that they are doing good.

# 2245

Those are the ones who refused to believe in the revelations of their Lord and that they are bound to meet Him. Hence, all their deeds have come to naught, and We shall assign no weight to them on the Day of Resurrection.

# 2246

Hell is their recompense for disbelieving and their taking My revelations and My Messengers as objects of jest.

# 2247

As for those who believe and do good works, the Gardens of Paradise shall be there to welcome them;

# 2248

there they will abide for ever, with no desire to be removed from there."

# 2249

Say: "If the sea were to become ink to record the Words of my Lord, indeed the sea would be all used up before the Words of my Lord are exhausted, and it would be the same even if We were to bring an equal amount of ink."

# 2250

Say (O Muhammad): "I am no more than a human being like you; one to whom revelation is made: 'Your Lord is the One and Only God.' Hence, whoever looks forward to meet his Lord, let him do righteous works, and let him associate none with the worship of his Lord."

# 2251

Kaf. Ha'. Ya'. Ayn. Sad.

# 2252

This is an account of the mercy of your Lord to His servant Zechariah

# 2253

when he cried to his Lord in secret.

# 2254

He said: "Lord! My bones have grown feeble and my head is glistening with age; yet, never have my prayers to You, my Lord, been unfruitful.

# 2255

I fear evil from my kinsmen after I am gone; and my wife is barren, so grant me an heir out of Your special grace,

# 2256

one that might be my heir and the heir of the house of Jacob; and make him, Lord, one that will be pleasing to You.

# 2257

(He was told): "Zechariah, We bring you the good news of the birth of a son whose name shall be Yahya (John), one whose namesake We never created before."

# 2258

He said: "My Lord! How can I have a boy when my wife is barren and I have reached an extremely old age?"

# 2259

He answered: "So shall it be." Your Lord says: "It is easy for Me," and then added: "For beyond doubt, I created you earlier when you were nothing."

# 2260

Zechariah said: "Lord, grant me a Sign." Said He: "Your Sign is that you shall not be able to speak to people for three nights, though you will be otherwise sound."

# 2261

Thereupon Zechariah came out from the sanctuary and directed his people by gestures to extol His glory by day and by night.

# 2262

"O John! Hold the Book with all your strength." We had bestowed wisdom upon him while he was still a child;

# 2263

and We also endowed him with tenderness and purity, and he was exceedingly pious

# 2264

and cherishing to his parents. Never was he insolent or rebellious.

# 2265

Peace be upon him the day he was born, and the day he will die, and the day he will be raised up alive.

# 2266

(O Muhammad), recite in the Book the account of Mary, when she withdrew from her people to a place towards the east;

# 2267

and drew a curtain, screening herself from people whereupon We sent to her Our spirit and he appeared to her as a well-shaped man.

# 2268

Mary exclaimed: "I surely take refuge from you with the Most Compassionate Lord, if you are at all God-fearing."

# 2269

He said: "I am just a message-bearer of your Lord, I have come to grant you a most pure boy."

# 2270

Mary said: "How can a boy be born to me when no man has even touched me, nor have I ever been unchaste?"

# 2271

The angel said: "Thus shall it be. Your Lord says: 'It is easy for Me; and We shall do so in order to make him a Sign for mankind and a mercy from Us. This has been decreed.' "

# 2272

Then she conceived him and withdrew with him to a far-off place.

# 2273

Then the birth pangs drove her to the trunk of a palm-tree and she said: "Oh, would that I had died before this and had been all forgotten."

# 2274

Thereupon the angel below her cried out: "Grieve not, for your Lord has caused a stream of water to flow beneath you.

# 2275

Shake the trunk of the palm-tree towards yourself and fresh and ripe dates shall fall upon you.

# 2276

So eat and drink and cool your eyes; and if you see any person say to him: 'Verily I have vowed a fast to the Most Compassionate Lord, and so I shall not speak to anyone today.' "

# 2277

Then she came to her people, carrying her baby. They said: "O Mary! You have committed a monstrous thing.

# 2278

O sister of Aaron! Your father was not an evil man, nor was your mother an unchaste woman."

# 2279

Thereupon Mary pointed to the child. They exclaimed: "How can we speak to one who is in the cradle, a mere child?"

# 2280

The child cried out: "Verily I am Allah's servant. He has granted me the Book and has made me a Prophet

# 2281

and has blessed me wherever I might be and has enjoined upon me Prayer and Zakah (purifying alms) as long as I live;

# 2282

and has made me dutiful to my mother. He has not made me oppressive, nor bereft of God's blessings.

# 2283

Peace be upon me the day I was born and the day I will die, and the day I will be raised up alive."

# 2284

This is Jesus, the son of Mary; and this is the truth about him concerning which they are in doubt.

# 2285

It does not befit Allah to take for Himself a son. Glory be to Him! When He decrees a thing He only says: "Be" and it is.

# 2286

(Jesus had said): "Indeed Allah is my Lord and your Lord, so serve Him alone. This is the Straight Way."

# 2287

But different parties began to dispute with one another. A dreadful woe awaits on that great Day for those that reject the Truth.

# 2288

How well shall they hear and how well shall they see on the Day they come to Us! But today the evil-doers are in manifest error.

# 2289

(O Muhammad), warn those who are steeped in heedlessness and are obstinately rejecting the truth that the Day shall come when things will be finally decided and they shall be left with utter remorse.

# 2290

Ultimately, We shall inherit the earth and whatever is on it; to Us shall they be returned.

# 2291

(O Muhammad), recite in the Book the account of Abraham. Most surely he was a man of truth, a Prophet.

# 2292

(And remind people) when he said to his father: "Father! Why do you worship that which neither sees nor hears, and which can be of no avail to you?

# 2293

Father, a knowledge that has not reached you has come to me. So follow me that I may guide you to a Straight Way.

# 2294

Father, do not serve Satan, for Satan has indeed been a persistent rebel against the Most Compassionate Lord.

# 2295

Father, I fear that a punishment from the Most Compassionate Lord might strike you and you may end up as one of Satan's companions?"

# 2296

The father said: "Abraham, have you turned away from my gods? If you do not give this up, I shall stone you to death. Now begone from me forever."

# 2297

Abraham answered: "Peace be upon you. I shall seek pardon for you from my Lord. My Lord has always been kind to Me.

# 2298

I shall withdraw from you and all that you call upon beside Allah. I shall only call upon my Lord. I trust the prayer to my Lord will not go unanswered."

# 2299

Thereupon Abraham dissociated himself from his people and the deities they worshipped instead of Allah, and We bestowed upon him Isaac and Jacob and made each of them a Prophet;

# 2300

and We bestowed on them Our mercy, and granted them a truly lofty renown.

# 2301

And recite in the Book the account of Moses. He was a chosen one, a Messenger, a Prophet.

# 2302

We called out to him from the right side of the Mount, and We drew him near to Us by communing to him in secret,

# 2303

and out of Our mercy We appointed his brother Aaron, a Prophet (that he may assist him).

# 2304

And recite in the Book the account of Ishmael. He was ever true to his promise, and was a Messenger, a Prophet.

# 2305

He enjoined his household to observe Prayer and to give Zakah (purifying alms); and his Lord was well pleased with him.

# 2306

And recite in the Book the account of Idris. He was a man of truth, a Prophet;

# 2307

and We exalted him to a lofty position.

# 2308

These are the Prophets upon whom Allah bestowed His favour from the seed of Adam, and from the seed of those whom We carried (in the Ark) with Noah, and from the seed of Abraham and Israel. They were those whom We guided and chose (for an exalted position). They were such that when the words of the Most Compassionate Lord were recited to them, they fell down in prostration, weeping.

# 2309

They were succeeded by a people who neglected the Prayers and pursued their lusts. They shall presently meet with their doom,

# 2310

except those who repent and believe and act righteously. Such shall enter Paradise and shall not be wronged at all.

# 2311

Theirs shall be everlasting Gardens which the Most Compassionate Lord has promised His servants in a realm which is beyond the ken of perception. Surely His promise shall he fulfilled.

# 2312

They shall not hear in it anything vain; they shall hear only what is good; and they shall have their provision in it, morning and evening.

# 2313

Such is the Paradise which We shall cause those of Our servants who have been God-fearing to inherit.

# 2314

(The angels will say): "(O Muhammad!) We descend not except by the command of your Lord. To Him belongs all that is before us and all that is behind us, and all that is in between. Your Lord is not forgetful in the least.

# 2315

He is the Lord of the heavens and the earth and all that is in between. Serve Him, then, and be constant in serving Him. Do you know anyone that might be His compeer?"

# 2316

Man is prone to say: "Shall I be raised to life after I die?"

# 2317

Does man not remember that We created him before when he was nothing?

# 2318

By your Lord, We will surely muster them and the devils together. Then We will surely bring them all, on their knees, around Hell,

# 2319

and then We will draw aside from each party those who were most rebellious against the Most Compassionate Lord,

# 2320

and then We shall know well all those most worthy to be cast in Hell.

# 2321

There is not one of you but shall pass by Hell. This is a decree which your Lord will fulfil.

# 2322

Then We shall deliver those that feared Allah and leave the wrong-doers there on their knees.

# 2323

When Our clear revelations are recited to those who deny the Truth they are wont to say to those who have faith: "Which of the two groups has a better status and whose assemblies are grander?"

# 2324

How numerous are the peoples We destroyed before them - those that were more resourceful and grander in outward appearance!

# 2325

Say: "The Most Compassionate Lord grants respite to those who stray into error, until they behold what they had been threatened with, either God's chastisement (in the world) or the Hour (of Resurrection)" - then they fully know whose station is worse, and who is weaker in hosts!

# 2326

(On the contrary), Allah increases in guidance those who follow the Right Way. Lasting acts of righteousness are better in the sight of your Lord as reward and conducive to a better end.

# 2327

Have you seen him who rejected Our signs and said: "Surely I shall continue to be favoured with riches and children."

# 2328

Has he obtained knowledge of the Unseen, or has he taken a covenant with the Most Compassionate Lord?

# 2329

By no means! We shall write down all what he says; and We shall greatly prolong his chastisement,

# 2330

and We shall inherit all the resources and hosts of which he boasts, and he will come to Us all alone.

# 2331

They have taken other gods instead of Allah that they may be a source of strength for them.

# 2332

By no means! They shall soon deny their worship and shall become their adversaries instead.

# 2333

Do you not see that We have sent devils upon the unbelievers who greatly incite them (to oppose the Truth)?

# 2334

Therefore, do not hasten (in seeking a scourge against them). We are counting their days.

# 2335

The Day shall soon come when We shall bring together the God-fearing to the Most Compassionate Lord, as honoured guests;

# 2336

and We shall drive the guilty ones to Hell as a thirsty herd.

# 2337

On that Day none will have the power to intercede for them except those who received a sanction from the Most Compassionate Lord.

# 2338

They claim: "The Most Compassionate Lord has taken a son to Himself."

# 2339

Surely you have made a monstrous statement.

# 2340

It is such a monstrosity that heavens might well-nigh burst forth at it, the earth might be cleaved, and the mountains fall

# 2341

at their ascribing a son to the Most Compassionate Lord.

# 2342

It does not befit the Most Compassionate Lord that He should take a son.

# 2343

There is no one in the heavens and the earth but he shall come to the Most Compassionate Lord as His servant.

# 2344

Verily He encompasses them and has counted them all.

# 2345

On the Day of Resurrection each one of these will come to Him singly.

# 2346

Indeed, the Most Compassionate Lord will soon create enduring love for those who believe and do righteous works.

# 2347

Therefore, We have revealed the Qur'an in your tongue and made it easy to understand that you may give glad tidings to the God-fearing and warn a contentious people.

# 2348

How numerous are the peoples that We destroyed before them! Do you now perceive any one of them, or hear even their whisper?

# 2349

Ta' Ha'

# 2350

We did not reveal the Qur'an to you to cause you distress;

# 2351

it is only a reminder for him who fears Allah;

# 2352

a revelation from Him Who created the earth and the high heavens.

# 2353

The Most Compassionate Lord is settled on the Throne (of the Universe).

# 2354

To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth, and all that is in between, and all that is beneath the soil.

# 2355

Whether you speak out aloud (or in a low voice), He knows what is said secretly, and even that which is most hidden.

# 2356

Allah - there is no god but He. His are the most excellent names.

# 2357

Has the story of Moses reached you?

# 2358

When he saw a fire and said to his family: "Hold on! I have just perceived a fire; perhaps I will bring a brand from it for you, or I will find some guidance at the fire about the way to follow."

# 2359

When he came to it, a voice called out: "Moses!

# 2360

Verily I am your Lord! Take off your shoes. You are in the sacred valley, Tuwa!

# 2361

I Myself have chosen you; therefore, give ear to what is revealed.

# 2362

Verily I am Allah. There is no god beside Me. So serve Me and establish Prayers to remember Me.

# 2363

The Hour of Resurrection is coming. I have willed to keep the time of its coming hidden so that everyone may be recompensed in accordance with his effort.

# 2364

Let him who does not believe in it and follows his lust not turn your thought away from it, lest you are ruined.

# 2365

And what is in your right hand, O Moses?"

# 2366

Moses answered: "This is my staff. I lean on it (when I walk), and with it I beat down leaves for my flock, and I have many other uses for it."

# 2367

He said: "Moses, throw it down."

# 2368

So he threw it down, and lo! it was a rapidly moving snake.

# 2369

Then He said: "Seize it and have no fear. We shall restore it to its former state.

# 2370

And place your hand in your armpit, it will come forth shining white, without blemish. This is another Sign of Allah,

# 2371

for We shall show you some of Our greatest Signs.

# 2372

And go to Pharaoh now for he has transgressed all bounds."

# 2373

Moses said: "Lord! Open my breast for me;

# 2374

and ease my task for me,

# 2375

and loosen the knot from my tongue

# 2376

so that they may understand my speech;

# 2377

and appoint for me, from my household, someone who will help me bear my burden -

# 2378

Aaron, my brother.

# 2379

Strengthen me through him

# 2380

and let him share my task

# 2381

that we may abundantly extol Your glory;

# 2382

and may remember You much.

# 2383

Verily, You have always watched over us."

# 2384

He said: "Moses, your petition is granted.

# 2385

We have again bestowed Our favour upon you.

# 2386

Recall, when We indicated to your mother through inspiration:

# 2387

'Put the baby into a chest and then throw him in the river. The river will throw him up on the shore, and then an enemy of Mine and an enemy of his will take him.' And I spread My love over you in order that you might be reared in My sight.

# 2388

Recall, when your sister went along, saying: 'Shall I direct you to one who will take charge of him?' Thus We brought you back to your mother so that her heart might be gladdened and she might not grieve. Moses, recall when you slew a person. We delivered you from distress and made you go through several trials. Then you stayed for several years among the people of Midian, and now you have come at the right moment as ordained.

# 2389

I have chosen you for My service.

# 2390

So go forth, both you and your brother, with My Signs, and do not slacken in remembering Me.

# 2391

Go both of you to Pharaoh, for he has transgressed all bounds,

# 2392

and speak to him gently, perhaps he may take heed or fear (Allah)."

# 2393

The two said:" Lord! We fear he may commit excesses against us, or transgress all bounds."

# 2394

He said: "Have no fear. I am with you, hearing and seeing all.

# 2395

So, go to him, and say: 'Behold, both of us are the Messengers of your Lord. Let the Children of Israel go with us, and do not chastise them. We have come to you with a sign from your Lord; and peace shall be for him who follows the true guidance.

# 2396

It has been revealed to us that chastisement awaits those who called the lie to the truth and turned away from it.' "

# 2397

Pharaoh said:" Moses! Who is the Lord of the two of you?"

# 2398

He said: "Our Lord is He Who gave everything its form and then guided it."

# 2399

Pharaoh asked: "Then, what is the state of the former generations?"

# 2400

Moses said: "Its knowledge is with my Lord, recorded in the Book. My Lord does not err, nor does He forget."

# 2401

He it is Who spread the earth for you; and made in it paths for you, and sent down water from the sky, and then through it We brought forth many species of diverse plants.

# 2402

So eat yourself and pasture your cattle. Surely there are many Signs in this for people of understanding.

# 2403

From this very earth We created you and to the same earth We shall cause you to return, and from it We shall bring you forth to life again.

# 2404

Indeed We showed Pharaoh Our Signs, all of them, but he declared them to be false and rejected them.

# 2405

He said: "Have you come to us to drive us out of our land by your sorcery?

# 2406

We shall confront you with a sorcery like your own. So appoint a day when both of us might meet face to face in an open space; an appointment which neither we nor you shall fail to keep."

# 2407

Moses said: "The appointment to meet you is on the Day of the Feast and let all people come together before noon."

# 2408

Pharaoh went back and concerted all his stratagem and returned for the encounter.

# 2409

(At the time of the encounter) Moses said to them: "Woe to you! Do not invent falsehoods against Allah lest He destroy you with a scourge. Surely those who invent lies shall come to grief."

# 2410

Thereupon they wrangled among themselves about the matter and conferred in secret.

# 2411

Some of them said: "These two are magicians, who want to drive you out of your land with their magic and to destroy your excellent way of life.

# 2412

So muster all your stratagem and come forth in a row. Whoever prevails today shall triumph."

# 2413

The magicians said: "Moses, will you throw down or shall we be the first to throw?"

# 2414

Moses replied: "No, let it be you to throw first." Then suddenly it appeared to Moses, owing to their magic, as if their ropes and staffs were running.

# 2415

So Moses' heart was filled with fear.

# 2416

We said to him: "Have no fear; for it is you who will prevail.

# 2417

And throw down what is in your right hand; it will swallow up all that they have wrought. They have wrought only a magician's stratagem. A magician cannot come to any good, come whence he may."

# 2418

Eventually the magicians were impelled to fall down prostrate and said: "We believe in the Lord of Moses and Aaron."

# 2419

Pharaoh said: "What! Did you believe in Him even before I permitted you to do so? Surely, he must be your chief who taught you magic. Now I will certainly cut off your hands and your feet on opposite sides, and will crucify you on the trunks of palm-trees, and then you will come to know which of us can inflict sterner and more lasting torment."

# 2420

The magicians answered: "By Him Who has created us, we shall never prefer you to the Truth after manifest Signs have come to us. So decree whatever you will. Your decree will pertain, at the most, to the present life of the world.

# 2421

We believe in our Lord that He may forgive us our sins and also forgive us the practice of magic to which you had compelled us. Allah is the Best and He alone will abide."

# 2422

The truth is that Hell awaits him who comes to his Lord laden with sin; he shall neither die in it nor live.

# 2423

But he who comes to Him with faith and righteous works shall be exalted to high ranks,

# 2424

and shall live for ever in everlasting Gardens beneath which rivers flow. Such will be the reward of those who purify themselves.

# 2425

Most certainly We revealed to Moses: "Proceed with My servants in the night and strike for them a dry path in the sea. Have no fear of being overtaken, nor be afraid of treading through the sea."

# 2426

Pharaoh pursued them with his hosts, but they were fully overwhelmed by the sea.

# 2427

Pharaoh led his people astray; he did not guide them aright.

# 2428

Children of Israel! We saved you from your enemy and made a covenant with you on the right side of the Mount and sent down on you manna and quails,

# 2429

saying: "Partake of the good things that We have provided for you, but do not transgress lest My wrath fall upon you; for he upon whom My wrath falls is ruined.

# 2430

But I am indeed Most Forgiving to him who repents and believes and does righteous works and keeps to the Right Way."

# 2431

"But, O Moses, what has made you come in haste from your people?"

# 2432

He said: "They are close behind me, and I hastened to You, Lord, that You may be pleased with me."

# 2433

Said He: "Verily We tested your people in your absence and the Samiri led them astray."

# 2434

Moses returned to his people full of wrath and grief, and said: "My people! Has your Lord not made good an excellent promise He made to you? And has a long time passed since those promises were fulfilled? Or was it to incur the wrath of your Lord that you broke your promise with me?"

# 2435

They answered: "We did not break our promise with you out of our own volition; but we were laden with the load of people's ornaments, and we simply threw them down(into the fire), and the Samiri also threw down something,

# 2436

and brought out of there (from the molten gold) the effigy of a calf that lowed." The people cried out: "This is your deity and the deity of Moses, whom Moses has forgotten."

# 2437

Did they not see that it did not return a word to them, and had no power either to hurt them or to cause them any benefit?

# 2438

Certainly Aaron had said to them even before (the return of Moses): "My people, you were fallen into error because of the calf. Surely your Lord is Most Compassionate; so follow me and obey my command."

# 2439

But they answered: "By no means shall we cease to worship it until Moses returns to us."

# 2440

(After rebuking his people) Moses turned to Aaron and said: "Aaron! What prevented you, when you saw them going astray,

# 2441

from following my way? Have you disobeyed my command?"

# 2442

Aaron answered: "Son of my mother! Do not seize me with my beard, nor by (the hair of) my head. I feared that on returning you might say: 'You sowed discord among the Children of Israel, and did not pay heed to my words.'"

# 2443

Moses said: "What, then, is your case, O Samiri?"

# 2444

He answered: "I saw what the people did not see. So I took a handful of dust from the trail of the Messenger, and I flung it (into the fire). Thus did my mind prompt me."

# 2445

Moses said: "Be gone, then. All your life you shall cry: 'Untouchable.' There awaits a term for your reckoning that you cannot fail to keep. Now look at your god that you devotedly adored: We shall burn it and scatter its remains in the sea.

# 2446

Your God is none else than Allah, beside Whom there is no god. His knowledge embraces everything."

# 2447

(O Muhammad), thus do We recount to you the events of the past, and We have bestowed upon you from Ourself an admonition.

# 2448

He who turns away from it will surely bear a heavy burden on the Day of Resurrection,

# 2449

and will abide under this burden for ever. Grievous shall be the burden on the Day of Resurrection,

# 2450

the Day when the Trumpet shall be sounded and We shall muster the sinners, their eyes turned blue with terror.

# 2451

They shall whisper among themselves: "You stayed on the earth barely ten days."

# 2452

We know well what they will say to one another: We also know that even the most cautious in his estimate will say: "You lived in the world no more than a day."

# 2453

They ask you concerning the mountains: "Where will they go?" Say: "My Lord will scatter them like dust,

# 2454

and leave the earth a levelled plain

# 2455

in which you shall find no crookedness or curvature.

# 2456

On that Day people shall follow straight on to the call of the summoner, no one daring to show any haughtiness. Their voices shall be hushed before the Most Compassionate Lord, so that you will hear nothing but a whispering murmur.

# 2457

On that Day intercession shall not avail save of him whom the Most Compassionate Lord permits, and whose word of intercession is pleasing to Him.

# 2458

He knows all that is ahead of them and all that is behind them, while the others do not know.

# 2459

All faces shall be humbled before the Ever-Living, the Self-Subsisting Lord, and he who bears the burden of iniquity will have failed;

# 2460

but whosoever does righteous works, being a believer, shall have no fear of suffering wrong or loss."

# 2461

(O Muhammad), thus have We revealed this as an Arabic Qur'an and have expounded in it warning in diverse ways so that they may avoid evil or become heedful.

# 2462

Exalted is Allah, the True King! Hasten not with reciting the Qur'an before its revelation to you is finished, and pray: "Lord! Increase me in knowledge."

# 2463

Most certainly We had given Adam a command before, but he forgot. We found him lacking in firmness of resolution.

# 2464

Recall when We said to the angels: "Prostrate yourselves before Adam"; all prostrated themselves save Iblis. He refused.

# 2465

Then We said: "Adam! He is an enemy to you and to your wife. So let him not drive both of you out of Paradise and plunge you into affliction,

# 2466

(for in Paradise) neither are you hungry nor naked,

# 2467

nor face thirst or scorching heat."

# 2468

But Satan seduced him, saying: "Adam! Shall I direct you to a tree of eternal life and an abiding kingdom?"

# 2469

Then the two of them ate the fruit of that tree and their shameful parts became revealed to each other, and they began to cover themselves with the leaves from the Garden. Thus Adam disobeyed his Lord and strayed into error.

# 2470

Thereafter his Lord exalted him, accepted his repentance, and bestowed guidance upon him,

# 2471

and said: "Get down, both of you, (that is, man and Satan), and be out of it; each of you shall be an enemy to the other. Henceforth if there comes to you a guidance from Me, then whosoever follows My guidance shall neither go astray nor suffer misery.

# 2472

But whosoever turns away from this Admonition from Me shall have a straitened life; We shall raise him blind on the Day of Resurrection,"

# 2473

where-upon he will say: "Lord! Why have You raised me blind when I had sight in the world?"

# 2474

He will say: "Even so it is. Our Signs came to you and you ignored them. So shall you be ignored this Day."

# 2475

Thus do We requite him who transgresses and does not believe in the signs of your Lord (during the life of the world); and surely the punishment of the Hereafter is even more terrible and more enduring.

# 2476

Did they not find any guidance in the fact that We destroyed many nations in whose ruined dwelling-places they now walk about? Surely there are many Signs in them for people endowed with wisdom.

# 2477

Were it not for a word already gone from your Lord, the decree (of their destruction) would have come to pass.

# 2478

So bear patiently with what they say. Glorify your Lord, praising Him before sunrise and before sunset, and in the watches of the night, and glorify Him and at the ends of the day that you may attain to happiness.

# 2479

Do not turn your eyes covetously towards the embellishments of worldly life that We have bestowed upon various kinds of people to test them. But the clean provision bestowed upon you by your Lord is better and more enduring.

# 2480

Enjoin Prayer on your household, and do keep observing it. We do not ask you for any worldly provision; rather, it is We Who provide you, and ultimately the pious will end up the best.

# 2481

They ask: "Why does he not bring us a (miraculous) sign from his Lord?" Has there not come to them a Book containing the teachings of the previous scriptures?

# 2482

Had We destroyed them through some calamity before his coming, they would have said: "Our Lord! Why did You not send any Messenger to us that we might have followed Your signs before being humbled and disgraced?"

# 2483

Tell them, (O Muhammad): "Everyone is waiting for his end. Wait, then, and you will soon know who are the people of the Right Way, and are rightly-guided."

# 2484

The time of people's reckoning has drawn near, and yet they turn aside in heedlessness.

# 2485

Whenever any fresh admonition comes to them from their Lord they barely heed it and remain immersed in play,

# 2486

their hearts being set on other concerns. The wrong-doers whisper to one another: "This person is no more than a mortal like yourselves. Will you, then, be enchanted by sorcery while you see?"

# 2487

He said: "My Lord knows well all that is spoken in the heavens and the earth. He is All-Hearing, All- Knowing."

# 2488

They say: "Nay, these are confused dreams; nay, he has forged it; nay, he is a poet. So let him bring us a sign, even as the Messengers of the past were sent with signs."

# 2489

Not one township that We destroyed before them believed. Would they, then, believe?

# 2490

(O Muhammad), even before you We never sent any other than human beings as Messengers, and to them We sent revelation. Ask the People of the Book if you do not know.

# 2491

We did not endow the Messengers with bodies that would need no food; nor were they immortals.

# 2492

Then We fulfilled the promise We had made to them: We rescued them and those whom We wished, and We destroyed those who exceeded all bounds.

# 2493

We have bestowed upon you a Book that mentions you. Do you not understand?

# 2494

How many a wrong-doing town did We shatter and then raise up another people.

# 2495

Then, when they perceived Our chastisement they took to their heels and fled.

# 2496

(They were told): "Flee not, but return to your comforts and to your dwellings. You are likely to be questioned."

# 2497

They said: "Woe to us; surely we were wrong-doers."

# 2498

They did not cease to cry this until We reduced them to stubble, still and silent.

# 2499

We did not create in sport the heavens and the earth and all that lies between the two.

# 2500

Had it been Our will to find a pastime, We would have found one near at hand; if at all We were inclined to do so.

# 2501

Nay, We hurl the Truth at falsehood so that the Truth crushes falsehood, and lo! it vanishes. Woe to you for what you utter!

# 2502

To Him belongs whosoever dwells in the heavens and on earth. Those (angels) that are with Him neither disdain to serve Him out of pride, nor do they weary of it.

# 2503

They glorify Him night and day, without flagging.

# 2504

Have they taken earthly gods who are such that they raise up the dead to life?

# 2505

Had there been any gods in the heavens and the earth apart from Allah, the order of both the heavens and the earth would have gone to ruins. Glory be to Allah, the Lord of the Throne, Who is far above their false descriptions of Him.

# 2506

None shall question Him about what He does, but they shall be questioned.

# 2507

Have they taken gods other than Him? Say, (O Muhammad): "Bring forth your proof! Here is the Book with admonition for those of my time and there are also scriptures with admonition for people before me." But most people do not know the Truth, and have, therefore, turned away from it.

# 2508

Never did We send any Messenger before you to whom We did not reveal: "There is no god but Me. So serve Me alone."

# 2509

They say: "The Most Compassionate Lord has taken to Himself a son." Glory be to Him! Those whom they so designate are only His honoured servants.

# 2510

They do not outstrip Him in speech and only act as He commands.

# 2511

He knows whatever is before them and whatsoever is remote from them and they do not intercede except for him, intercession on whose behalf pleases Him, and they stand constantly in awe of Him.

# 2512

And if anyone of them were to claim: "Indeed I am a god apart from Him," We shall recompense both with Hell. Thus do We recompense the wrong-doers.

# 2513

Did the unbelievers (who do not accept the teaching of the Prophet) not realize that the heavens and the earth were one solid mass, then We tore them apart, and We made every living being out of water? Will they, then, not believe (that We created all this)?

# 2514

And We placed firm mountains on earth lest it should sway with them, and We made wide paths in them that they may find their way;

# 2515

and We made the sky a secure canopy; and yet they turn away from these Signs.

# 2516

It is He Who created the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Each of them is floating in its orbit.

# 2517

(O Muhammad), We did not grant everlasting life to any human being even before you. If you were to die, will they live for ever?

# 2518

Every living being shall taste death and We shall subject you to ill and good by way of trial, and to Us shall all of you be eventually sent back.

# 2519

When the unbelievers see you they make you an object of fun, saying: "Is he the one who mentions your gods?" They say so, and yet they reject with disdain the very mention of the Most Compassionate Lord.

# 2520

Man is hasty by nature. I shall certainly show you My Signs. Do not ask Me to be hasty.

# 2521

They say: "(Tell us) when will the threat of punishment come to pass if you are truthful?"

# 2522

If only the unbelievers knew of the Hour when they shall not be able to keep off the Fire from their faces, nor from their backs; nor shall they be helped.

# 2523

That will suddenly come upon them and stupefy them. They shall not be able to ward it off, nor shall they be granted any respite.

# 2524

Other Messengers before you were also mocked, but those who scoffed at the Messengers were overtaken by the same scourge that they had scoffed at.

# 2525

Tell them, (O Muhammad): "Who protects you, during the night or the day from the Most Compassionate Lord?" And yet they turn away from the Admonition of their Lord.

# 2526

Do they have any gods who would protect them against Us? They have no power even to help themselves; nor do they enjoy Our support.

# 2527

Nay, We generously provided them and their fathers, and they enjoyed Our provision for long. Do they not see that We are now advancing into their territory, diminishing it from different sides? Is it they, then, who will triumph?"

# 2528

Tell them: "I only warn you by the Revelation." But the deaf do not hear the cry when they are warned.

# 2529

Were only the slightest whiff from your Lord's punishment to touch them, they would cry out: "Woe to us; we were indeed wrong-doers."

# 2530

We shall set up just scales on the Day of Resurrection so that none will be wronged in the least. (We shall bring forth the acts of everyone), even if it be the weight of a grain of mustard seed. We shall suffice as Reckoners.

# 2531

Surely We had granted to Moses and Aaron the Criterion (between right and wrong), and Light and Admonition for the good of the God-fearing,

# 2532

for those who fear their Lord without seeing Him and dread the Hour (of Reckoning).

# 2533

This is a Blessed Admonition that We have revealed. Are you, then, going to reject it?

# 2534

Surely We had bestowed wisdom upon Abraham even earlier, and We knew him well.

# 2535

Recall, when he said to his father and his people: "What are these images to which you are devoutly clinging?"

# 2536

They answered: "We found our fathers worshipping them."

# 2537

He said: "Certainly you and your fathers have all been in manifest error."

# 2538

They said: "Are you expressing your true ideas before us or are you jesting?"

# 2539

He said: "Nay, but your Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth which He created and to that I bear witness before you.

# 2540

By Allah, I shall certainly carry out my plan against your gods after you are gone."

# 2541

Then he broke them all into pieces, sparing only the supreme one among them that they may possibly return to him.

# 2542

(When they saw the idols in this state) they said: "Who has done this to our gods? Surely he is one of the wrong-doers."

# 2543

Some of them said: "We heard a youth called Abraham speak (ill) of them."

# 2544

The others said: "Bring him, then, before the eyes of the people that they may see (what will be done to him)."

# 2545

(On Abraham's arrival) they said: "Abraham, are you he who has done this to our gods?"

# 2546

He answered: "Rather it was this supreme one who has done it. So ask them, if they can speak."

# 2547

Thereupon they turned to their (inner) selves and said (to themselves): "Surely it is you who are the wrong-doers."

# 2548

Then their minds were turned upside down, and they said: "You know well that they do not speak."

# 2549

Abraham said: "Do you, then, worship beside Allah a thing that can neither benefit you nor hurt you?

# 2550

Fie upon you and upon all that you worship beside Allah. Do you have no sense?"

# 2551

They said: "Burn him, and come to the support of your gods, if you are going to do anything."

# 2552

We said: "O fire, become coolness and safety for Abraham."

# 2553

They had sought to do evil to him, but We caused them to be the worst losers,

# 2554

and We saved him and Lot and brought him to the land upon which We had bestowed Our blessings for all the people of the world.

# 2555

And We bestowed upon him Isaac and Jacob as an additional gift, making each of them righteous.

# 2556

And We made them into leaders to guide people in accordance with Our command, and We inspired them to good works, and to establish Prayers and to give Zakah. They worshipped Us alone.

# 2557

We bestowed upon Lot sound judgement and knowledge, and We delivered him from the city that was immersed in foul deeds. They were indeed a wicked people, exceedingly disobedient.

# 2558

And We admitted him into Our mercy. Verily he was of the righteous.

# 2559

We bestowed the same favour upon Noah. Recall, when he cried to Us before; We accepted his prayer and delivered him and his household from the great distress

# 2560

and We helped him against a people who rejected Our signs as false. They were indeed an evil people and so We drowned them all.

# 2561

We bestowed the same favour upon David and Solomon. Recall, when they gave judgement regarding a tillage into which the sheep of some people had strayed at night, and We were witnesses to their judgement.

# 2562

We guided Solomon to the right verdict, and We had granted each of them judgement and knowledge. We made the mountains and the birds celebrate the praise of Allah with David. It was We Who did all this.

# 2563

It was We Who taught him the art of making coats of mail for your benefit so that it may protect you from each other's violence. Do you, then, give thanks?

# 2564

And We subdued the strongly raging wind to Solomon which blew at his bidding towards the land We blessed. We know everything.

# 2565

And We subdued many devils who dived (into the sea) for him and carried out other jobs besides that. We kept watch over all of them.

# 2566

We bestowed (the same wisdom, judgement and knowledge) upon Job. Recall, when he cried to his Lord: "Behold, disease has struck me and You are the Most Merciful of those that are merciful."

# 2567

We accepted his prayer and removed the affliction from him, and We not only restored to him his family but as many more with them as a mercy from Us and as a lesson to the worshippers.

# 2568

And (We bestowed the same favour) upon Ishmael, Idris and Dhu al-Kifl, for they were all steadfast.

# 2569

And We admitted them into Our mercy, for they were of the righteous.

# 2570

And We bestowed Our favour upon Dhu al-Nun. Recall, when he went forth enraged, thinking We have no power to take him to task. Eventually he cried out in the darkness:" There is no god but You. Glory be to You! I have done wrong."

# 2571

Thereupon We accepted his prayer, and rescued him from grief. Thus do We rescue the believers.

# 2572

And We bestowed favour upon Zechariah, when he cried to his Lord: "Lord! Leave me not solitary (without any issue). You are the Best Inheritor."

# 2573

So We accepted his prayer and bestowed upon him John, and We made his wife fit (to bear a child). Verily they hastened in doing good works and called upon Us with longing and fear, and humbled themselves to Us.

# 2574

And also recall the woman who guarded her chastity: We breathed into her of Our spirit, and made her and her son a Sign to the whole world.

# 2575

Verily this community of yours is a single community, and I am your Lord; so worship Me.

# 2576

But they tore asunder their faith into many parts. But to Us they are bound to return.

# 2577

Then whosoever does righteous works, while believing, his striving will not go unappreciated. We record them all for him.

# 2578

It has been ordained against every town that We ever destroyed that they shall not return (to enjoy a new lease of life)

# 2579

until Gog and Magog are let loose, and begin swooping from every mound,

# 2580

and the time for the fulfilment of the true promise of Allah draws near, whereupon the eyes of those who disbelieved will stare in fear, and they will say: "Woe to us, we were indeed heedless of this; nay, we were wrongdoers."

# 2581

(They will be told): "Verily you and the gods you worshipped beside Allah are the fuel of Hell. All of you are bound to arrive there.

# 2582

Had these indeed been gods they would not have gone there. But (as it is), all of you shall ever abide in it."

# 2583

There they shall groan with anguish and the din and noise in Hell will not let them hear anything.

# 2584

But for those whom We had decided to favour with good reward, they shall be kept far removed from Hell.

# 2585

They shall not hear even a whisper of it, and they shall live for ever in the delights which they had desired.

# 2586

The Hour of the Great Terror shall not grieve them, and the angels shall receive them saying: "This is your Day which you had been promised."

# 2587

On that Day We shall roll up the heavens like a scroll for writing. Even as We originated the creation first so We shall repeat it. This is a promise binding on Us; and so We shall do.

# 2588

Surely We wrote in the Psalms, after the exhortation, that the earth shall be inherited by My righteous servants.

# 2589

Herein, surely, is a message for those devoted to worship.

# 2590

We have sent you forth as nothing but mercy to people of the whole world.

# 2591

Say: "It is revealed to me that your God is only One God. Will you, then, submit to Him?"

# 2592

If they turn away, say to them: "I have warned you all alike; and I cannot say whether what you have been promised is near or distant.

# 2593

Indeed He knows what you say loudly and what you hide.

# 2594

I think that this \[reprieve\] is possibly a trial for you, an opportunity to enjoy yourselves until an appointed time."

# 2595

The Messenger said: "My Lord! Judge with truth. Our Compassionate Lord alone is our support against your (blasphemous) utterances."

# 2596

O mankind, fear the (wrath of) your Lord! Indeed, the earthquake of the Hour (of Judgement) will be an awesome thing.

# 2597

On the Day when you witness it, the suckling woman shall utterly neglect the infant she suckles, and every pregnant woman shall cast her burden, and you will see people as though they are drunk, when they are not drunk; but dreadful shall be Allah's chastisement.

# 2598

Among people there are some who wrangle about Allah without knowledge and follow every rebellious devil,

# 2599

although it is decreed about him that he shall lead into error whosoever takes him for a friend, and will direct him to the torment of the Fire.

# 2600

O mankind! If you have any doubt concerning Resurrection, then know that it is surely We Who created you from dust, then from a drop of sperm, then from a clot of blood, then from a little lump of flesh, some of it shapely and other shapeless. (We are rehearsing this) that We may make the reality clear to you. We cause (the drop of sperm) that We please to remain in the wombs till an appointed time. We bring you forth as infants (and nurture you) that you may come of age. Among you is he that dies (at a young age) and he who is kept back to the most abject age so that after once having known, he reaches a stage when he knows nothing. You see the earth dry and barren and then no sooner than We send down water upon it, it begins to quiver and swell and brings forth every kind of beauteous vegetation.

# 2601

All this is because Allah, He is the Truth, and because He resurrects the dead, and because He has power over everything,

# 2602

(all of which shows that) the Hour shall surely come to pass - in this there is no doubt - and Allah shall surely resurrect those that are in graves.

# 2603

And among people are those that wrangle about Allah without knowledge, without any true guidance, and without any scripture to enlighten them.

# 2604

They wrangle arrogantly, intent on leading people astray from the Way of Allah. Such shall suffer disgrace in this world and We shall cause them to taste the chastisement of burning (in the Next).

# 2605

That is the outcome of what your own hands have wrought, for Allah never wrongs His creatures.

# 2606

And among people is he who worships Allah on the borderline; if any good befalls him, he is satisfied; but if a trial afflicts him, he utterly turns away. He will incur the loss of this world and the Hereafter. That indeed is a clear loss.

# 2607

He invokes, instead of Allah, those who can neither harm nor benefit him. That indeed is straying far away.

# 2608

He invokes those that are more likely to cause him harm than benefit. Such is surely an evil patron, and an evil associate.

# 2609

(In contrast) Allah will assuredly cause those who believe and act righteously to enter Gardens beneath which rivers flow. For, most certainly, Allah does whatever He pleases.

# 2610

Anyone who fancies that Allah will not support him in this world and in the Hereafter, let him reach out to heaven through a rope, and then make a hole in the sky and see whether his device can avert that which enrages him.

# 2611

Even so We have revealed the Qur'an with Clear Signs. Verily Allah guides whomsoever He wills.

# 2612

On the Day of Resurrection Allah will most certainly judge among those who believe, and those who became Jews, and Sabaeans, and Christians, and Magians, and those who associate others with Allah in His Divinity. Surely Allah watches over everything.

# 2613

Have you not seen that all those who are in the heavens and all those who are in the earth prostrate themselves before Allah; and so do the sun and the moon, and the stars and the mountains, and the trees, and the beasts, and so do many human beings, and even many of those who are condemned to chastisement? And he whom Allah humiliates, none can give him honour. Allah does whatever He wills.

# 2614

These two groups (the believers and unbelievers) are in dispute about their Lord. As for those that disbelieve, garments of fire have been cut out for them; boiling water shall be poured down over their heads,

# 2615

causing (not only) their skins but all that is in their bellies as well to melt away.

# 2616

There shall be maces of iron to lash them.

# 2617

Whenever they try, in their anguish, to escape from Hell, they will be driven back into it, (and shall be told): "Now taste the torment of burning."

# 2618

(On the other hand), Allah will cause those who believed and acted righteously to enter the Gardens beneath which rivers flow. They shall be decked in them with bracelets of gold and pearls and their raiment shall be of silk.

# 2619

They were guided (to accept) the pure word; they were guided to the Way of the Praiseworthy (Lord).

# 2620

Indeed those who disbelieve and who (now) hinder people from the Way of Allah and hinder them from the Holy Mosque which We have set up (as a place of worship) for all people, equally for those who dwell therein and for those who come from outside, (they surely deserve punishment). Whosoever deviates therein from the Right Way and acts with iniquity, We shall cause him to taste a painful chastisement.

# 2621

Call to mind when We assigned to Abraham the site of the House (Kabah), directing him: "Do not associate aught with Me" and "Keep My House pure for those who walk around it, and for those who stand and who bow down and who prostrate themselves (in worship),

# 2622

and publicly proclaim Pilgrimage for all mankind so that they come to you on foot and mounted on lean camels from every distant point

# 2623

to witness the benefits in store for them, and pronounce the name of Allah during the appointed days over the cattle that He has provided them. So eat of it and feed the distressed and the needy.

# 2624

Thereafter, let them tidy up and fulfil their vows and circumambulate the Ancient House."

# 2625

Such (was the purpose of building the Kabah). Whosoever, then, venerates Allah's sanctities will find it to be good for him in the sight of his Lord. Cattle have been made lawful for you except those mentioned to you (as unlawful). So shun the abomination of idols and shun all words of falsehood.

# 2626

Become exclusively devoted to Allah, ascribing Divinity to none other than Him. Whoso ascribes Divinity to aught beside Allah, it is as though he fell down from the sky whereafter either the birds will snatch him away, or the wind will sweep him to a distant place (causing him to be shattered to pieces).

# 2627

Such is the fact. And whoso venerates the sanctity of all that have been ordained as symbols of Allah surely does so because it is part of the true piety of the hearts.

# 2628

You may derive benefit (from sacrificial animals) until an appointed time. Thereafter their place (of sacrifice) is near the Ancient House.

# 2629

For every people We have laid down a ritual of sacrifice(- although the purpose of the ritual is the same -)that they pronounce the name of Allah over the cattle He has provided them. Your Lord is One God; so submit yourselves to Him alone. And give, (O Prophet), glad tidings to those that humble themselves (before Allah),

# 2630

whose hearts shiver whenever Allah is mentioned, who patiently bear whatever affliction comes to them, who establish Prayer, and who spend (for good purposes) out of what We have provided them.

# 2631

We have appointed sacrificial camels among the symbols of (devotion to) Allah. There is much good in them for you. So make them stand (at the time of sacrifice) and pronounce the name of Allah over them, and when they fall down on their sides (after they are slaughtered), eat and also feed them who do not ask and those who ask. Thus have We subjected these animals that you may give thanks.

# 2632

Neither their flesh reaches Allah nor their blood; it is your piety that reaches Him. He has subjected these animals (to you) that you may magnify Allah for the guidance He has bestowed upon you. Give glad tidings, (O Prophet), to those who do good.

# 2633

Surely Allah defends those who believe. Certainly Allah has no love for the perfidious, the thankless.

# 2634

Permission (to fight) has been granted to those for they have been wronged. Verily Allah has the power to help them:

# 2635

those who were unjustly expelled from their homes for no other reason than their saying: "Allah is Our Lord." If Allah were not to repel some through others, monasteries and churches and synagogues and mosques wherein the name of Allah is much mentioned, would certainly have been pulled down. Allah will most certainly help those who will help Him. Verily Allah is Immensely Strong, Overwhelmingly Mighty.

# 2636

(Allah will certainly help) those who, were We to bestow authority on them in the land, will establish Prayers, render Zakah, enjoin good, and forbid evil. The end of all matters rests with Allah.

# 2637

(O Prophet), if they give the lie to you, then before them the people of 'Ad and Thamud, also gave the lie (to the Prophets),

# 2638

and so too did the people of Abraham and the people of Lot;

# 2639

and so did the dwellers of Midian, and Moses too was branded a liar. Initially I granted respite to the unbelievers for a while and then seized them. How dreadful was My punishment!

# 2640

How many towns have We destroyed because their people were steeped in iniquity: so they lie fallen down upon their turrets! How many wells lie deserted; and how many towering palaces lie in ruins!

# 2641

Have they not journeyed in the land that their hearts might understand and their ears might listen? For indeed it is not the eyes that are blinded; it is rather the hearts in the breasts that are rendered blind.

# 2642

They ask you to hasten the punishment. Allah shall most certainly not fail His promise; but a Day with your Lord is as a thousand years of your reckoning.

# 2643

How many towns did I respite at first though they were steeped in iniquity, and then I seized them! To Me are all destined to return.

# 2644

Say (O Muhammad): "O people! I have been sent to you only as a plain warner (before the Doom strikes you)."

# 2645

So those who believe and act righteously shall be granted forgiveness and an honourable sustenance,

# 2646

whereas those who strive against Our Signs, seeking to profane them, they are the friends of the Fire!

# 2647

Never did We send a Messenger or a Prophet before you (O Muhammad), but that whenever he had a desire, Satan interfered with that desire. Allah eradicates the interference of Satan and strengthens His Signs. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.

# 2648

(He does this) in order that He may make the evil caused by Satan a trial for those in whose hearts there is sickness (of hypocrisy), whose hearts are hard (and vitiated). Surely these wrong-doers have gone too far in their dissension.

# 2649

(He also does this) in order that those endowed with knowledge may know that it is the Truth from your Lord and that they may have faith in it and their hearts may humble themselves before Him. Verily Allah always directs those that believe to the Right Way.

# 2650

The unbelievers will not cease to be in doubt about it until the Hour suddenly comes upon them, or the chastisement of an ominous day overtakes them.

# 2651

On that Day all sovereignty shall be Allah's and He will judge among them. Then those who believed and acted righteously shall be in Gardens of Bliss.

# 2652

A humiliating chastisement awaits those who disbelieved and denied Our Signs.

# 2653

As for those who migrated in the way of Allah, whereafter they were slain, or died, Allah will certainly grant them a goodly provision. Indeed, Allah is the Best of all those who provide.

# 2654

He will surely admit them to a resort which will please them. Most certainly Allah is All-Knowing, Most Forbearing.

# 2655

That indeed is so, as for him who retaliates in proportion to the excess committed against him, and is thereafter again subjected to transgression, Allah will surely aid him. Verily Allah is All-Pardoning, All-Forgiving.

# 2656

So shall it be because it is Allah Who causes the night to emerge out of the day and causes the day to emerge out of the night and Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing.

# 2657

So shall it be because Allah, He is the Truth, and all whom they invoke instead of Him are false. Allah is Most High, All-Great.

# 2658

Do you not see that Allah sends down water from the sky whereby the earth turns green? Verily Allah is Subtle, All-Aware.

# 2659

To Him belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth. Surely Allah - He alone is Self- Sufficient, Praiseworthy.

# 2660

Have you not seen how Allah has subjected to you all that is in the earth, and the vessels that sail in the sea by His command, and it is He Who holds back the sky that it may not fall on earth except by His leave? Surely Allah is Most Gentle, Ever Compassionate to people.

# 2661

And it is He Who has endowed you with life and it is He who causes you to die, and it is He Who will then resurrect you. Man is indeed extremely prone to denying the Truth.

# 2662

For every people We have prescribed a way of worship which they follow. So, (O Muhammad), let them not dispute with you concerning this, and call them to Your Lord. You are certainly on the Straight Way.

# 2663

And if they dispute with you, say: "Allah knows well what you do.

# 2664

Allah will judge among you on the Day of Resurrection concerning matters about which you disagreed."

# 2665

Are you not aware that Allah knows all that is in the heaven and the earth? Surely it is all preserved in a Book. Indeed that is easy with Allah.

# 2666

Instead of Allah they worship those concerning whom He has revealed no sanction and concerning whom they have no true knowledge. None shall be able to help such evil-doers.

# 2667

When Our Signs are plainly recited to them, you will perceive utter repugnance on their faces and it all but seems as if they will soon pounce upon those who recite Our Signs to them. Say: "Shall I tell you what is worse than that? The Fire with which Allah has threatened those who disbelieve. That is truly an evil end."

# 2668

O people, a parable is set forth: pay heed to it. Those who call upon aught other than Allah shall never be able to create even a fly, even if all of them were to come together to do that. And if the fly were to snatch away anything from them, they would not be able to recover that from it. Powerless is the supplicant; and powerless is he to whom he supplicates.

# 2669

They have not formed a true estimate of Allah. Indeed, Allah is All-Powerful, All-Mighty.

# 2670

Allah chooses Messengers from among angels and from among human beings (to convey His command). Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing.

# 2671

He knows all that is before them and that which is hidden from them. And it is to Allah that all affairs are returned.

# 2672

Believers, bow down and prostrate yourselves before Your Lord and serve Your Lord and do good that you may prosper.

# 2673

Strive in the cause of Allah in a manner worthy of that striving. He has chosen you (for His task), and He has not laid upon you any hardship in religion. Keep to the faith of your father Abraham. Allah named you Muslims earlier and even in this (Book), that the Messenger may be a witness over you, and that you may be witnesses over all mankind. So establish Prayer, and pay Zakah, and hold fast to Allah. He is your Protector. What an excellent Protector; what an excellent Helper!

# 2674

The believers have indeed attained true success:

# 2675

those who, in their Prayers, humble themselves;

# 2676

who avoid whatever is vain and frivolous;

# 2677

who observe Zakah;

# 2678

who strictly guard their private parts

# 2679

save from their wives, or those whom their right hands possess; for with regard to them they are free from blame "

# 2680

As for those who seek beyond that, they are transgressors"

# 2681

who are true to their trusts and their covenants,

# 2682

and who guard their Prayers.

# 2683

Such are the inheritors

# 2684

that shall inherit Paradise; and in it they shall abide for ever.

# 2685

We created man out of the extract of clay,

# 2686

then We made him into a drop of life-germ, then We placed it in a safe depository,

# 2687

then We made this drop into a clot, then We made the clot into a lump, then We made the lump into bones, then We clothed the bones with flesh, and then We caused it to grow into another creation. Thus Most Blessed is Allah, the Best of all those that create.

# 2688

Thereafter you are destined to die,

# 2689

and then on the Day of Resurrection you shall certainly be raised up.

# 2690

We have indeed fashioned above you seven paths. Never were We unaware of the task of creation.

# 2691

We sent down water from the sky in right measure, and caused it to stay in the earth, and We have the power to cause it to vanish (in the manner We please).

# 2692

Then through water We caused gardens of date-palms and vines to grow for you wherein you have an abundance of delicious fruits and from them you derive your livelihood.

# 2693

And We also produced the tree which springs forth from Mount Sinai, containing oil and sauce for those that eat.

# 2694

And indeed there is also a lesson for you in cattle. We provide you with drink out of what they have in their bellies; and you have many other benefits in them: you eat of them,

# 2695

and are carried on them and also on ships.

# 2696

We sent Noah to his people, and he said: "My people! Serve Allah; you have no deity other than He. Do you have no fear?"

# 2697

But the notables among his people had refused to believe, and said: "This is none other than a mortal like yourselves who desires to attain superiority over you. Had Allah wanted (to send any Messengers) He would have sent down angels. We have heard nothing like this in the time of our forebears of old (that humans were sent as Messengers).

# 2698

He is a person who has been seized with a little madness; so wait for a while (perhaps he will improve)."

# 2699

Noah said: "My Lord! Come to my help at their accusation that I am lying."

# 2700

Thereupon We revealed to him, saying: "Build the Ark under Our eyes and according to Our revelation. And when Our command comes to pass and the oven boils over, take on board a pair each from every species, and also take your household except those of them against whom sentence has already been passed and do not plead to Me on behalf of the wrong-doers. They are doomed to be drowned.

# 2701

And then when you and those accompanying you are firmly seated in the Ark, say: "Thanks be to Allah Who has delivered us from the wrong-doing people."

# 2702

And say: "My Lord! Make my landing a blessed landing, for You are the Best of those Who can cause people to land in safety."

# 2703

There are great Signs in this story; and surely We do put people to test.

# 2704

Then, after them, We brought forth another generation;

# 2705

and We sent among them a Messenger from among themselves, saying: "Serve Allah; you have no god other than He. Do you have no fear?"

# 2706

The notables among his people who had refused to believe and who denied the meeting of the Hereafter, and those whom We had endowed with ease and comfort in this life, cried out: "This is no other than a mortal like yourselves who eats what you eat and drinks what you drink.

# 2707

If you were to obey a human being like yourselves, you will certainly be losers.

# 2708

Does he promise you that when you are dead and are reduced to dust and bones, you will be brought forth to life?

# 2709

Far-fetched, utterly far-fetched is what you are being promised.

# 2710

There is no other life than the life of the world. We shall live here and here shall we die; and we are not going to be raised again.

# 2711

This man has forged a mere lie in the name of Allah and we shall never believe what he says."

# 2712

The Messenger said: "My Lord! Come to my help at their accusing me of lying."

# 2713

He answered: "A short while, and they shall be repenting."

# 2714

Then a mighty blast quite justly overtook them, and We reduced them to a rubble. So away with the wrong-doing folk!

# 2715

Then, after them, We brought forth other generations.

# 2716

No nation can outstrip its term, nor can it put it back.

# 2717

Then We sent Our Messengers in succession. Whenever a Messenger came to his people they rejected him, calling him a liar. Thereupon, We made each people to follow the other (to its doom), reducing them to mere tales (of the past). Scourged be the people who do not believe!

# 2718

Then We sent Moses and his brother Aaron with Our Signs and a clear authority

# 2719

to Pharaoh and to his chiefs, but they behaved superciliously and they were haughty.

# 2720

They said: "Shall we put faith in two mortals like ourselves when their people are slaves to us?"

# 2721

So they rejected them, calling them liars, and they too eventually became of those that were destroyed.

# 2722

And We gave Moses the Book that people might be guided by it.

# 2723

And We made Mary's son, and his mother, a Sign, and We gave them refuge on a lofty ground, a peaceful site with springs flowing in it.

# 2724

Messengers! Partake of the things that are clean, and act righteously. I know well all that you do.

# 2725

This community of yours is one community, and I am your Lord; so hold Me alone in fear.

# 2726

But people later cut up their religion into bits, each group rejoicing in what they have.

# 2727

So leave them immersed in their heedlessness till an appointed time.

# 2728

Do they fancy that Our continuing to give them wealth and children (means) that

# 2729

We are busy lavishing on them all kinds of good? Nay, they do not perceive the reality of the matter.

# 2730

Surely those who stand in awe for fear of their Lord,

# 2731

who have full faith in the Signs of their Lord;

# 2732

who associate none with their Lord in His Divinity,

# 2733

who give, whatever they give in charity, with their hearts trembling at the thought that they are destined to return to their Lord;

# 2734

it is these who hasten to do good works and vie in so doing with one another.

# 2735

We do not lay a burden on anyone beyond his capacity. We have a Book with Us that speaks the truth (about everyone); and they shall in no wise be wronged.

# 2736

Nay, their hearts are lost in ignorance of all this; and their deeds too vary from the way (mentioned above). They will persist in these deeds

# 2737

until We seize with Our chastisement those of them that are given to luxuriant ways. They will then begin to groan.

# 2738

"Put a stop to your groaning now! Surely no help shall be provided to you from Us.

# 2739

My Signs were rehearsed to you and you turned back on your heels and took to flight,

# 2740

behaving arrogantly, and making fun, and talking nonsense (about the Book in your nightly chats)."

# 2741

Did they never ponder over this Word (of God)? Or has he (to wit, the Messenger) brought something the like of which did not come to their forefathers of yore?

# 2742

Or is it that they were unaware of their Messenger and were therefore repelled by him for he was a stranger to them?

# 2743

Or do they say that there is madness in him? Nay, he has brought them the Truth and it is the Truth that most of them disdain.

# 2744

Were the Truth to follow their desires, the order of the heavens and the earth and those who dwell in them would have been ruined. Nay, the fact is that We have brought to them their own remembrance; and yet it is from their own remembrance that they are turning away.

# 2745

Are you asking them for something? What Allah has given you is the best. He is the Best of providers.

# 2746

You are calling them to a Straight Way,

# 2747

but those who do not believe in the Hereafter are ever prone to deviate from the Right Way.

# 2748

Were We to be merciful to them and remove from them their present afflictions, they would persist in their transgression, blindly wandering on.

# 2749

(They are such) that We seized them with chastisement (and yet) they did not humble themselves before their Lord, nor do they entreat

# 2750

until We opened upon them the door of a severe chastisement. Then lo, in this state they become utterly despaired of any good.

# 2751

It is He Who has endowed you with the faculties of hearing and sight and has given you hearts (to think). Scarcely do you give thanks.

# 2752

It is He Who has dispersed you all around the earth, and it is unto Him that you shall all be mustered.

# 2753

It is He Who gives life and causes death, and He holds mastery over the alternation of night and day. Do you not understand this?

# 2754

Nay, but they say the like of what their predecessors of yore had said.

# 2755

They say: "Is it that when we are dead and have been reduced to dust and bones, shall we then be raised up again?

# 2756

We were promised such things and so were our forefathers before us. All these are no more than tales of the past."

# 2757

Ask them: "Whose is the earth and those who are in it? Tell us if you know"

# 2758

They will surely say: "Allah's." Say: "Then why do you not take heed?"

# 2759

Ask them: "Who is the Lord of the seven heavens, the Lord of the Great Throne?"

# 2760

They will surely say: "Allah." Say: "Will you not, then, fear (Allah)?"

# 2761

Ask them: "Say, if you indeed know, to whom belongs the dominion over all things; (Who is it) that grants asylum, but against Whom no asylum is available?"

# 2762

They will surely say: "(The dominion over all things) belongs to Allah." Say: "Whence are you then deluded?"

# 2763

We have brought before them the Truth, and there is no doubt that they are lying.

# 2764

Never did Allah take unto Himself any son, nor is there any god other than He. (Had there been any other gods) each god would have taken his creatures away with him, and each would have rushed to overpower the other. Glory be to Allah from all that they characterize Him with!

# 2765

He knows both what is visible and what is not visible. Exalted is Allah above all that they associate with Him.

# 2766

Pray, (O Muhammad): "My Lord, if You should bring the scourge of which they had been warned in my presence,

# 2767

then do not include me, my Lord, among these wrong-doing people."

# 2768

Surely We are able to show you what We warn them against.

# 2769

(O Muhammad)! Repel evil in the best manner. We are well aware of all that they say about you.

# 2770

And pray: "My Lord! I seek Your refuge from the suggestions of the evil ones;

# 2771

I even seek Your refuge, my Lord, lest they should approach me."

# 2772

(They shall persist in their deeds) until when death comes to anyone of them he will say: "My Lord, send me back to the world

# 2773

that I have left behind. I am likely to do good." Nay, it is merely a word that he is uttering. There is a barrier behind all of them (who are dead) until the Day when they will be raised up.

# 2774

And then no sooner the Trumpet is blown than there will remain no kinship among them that Day, nor will they ask one another.

# 2775

It will be an Hour when those whose scales are heavy, they alone will attain success;

# 2776

and those whose scales are light, those will be the ones who will have courted loss. They will abide in Hell.

# 2777

The Fire shall scorch their faces, exposing their jaws.

# 2778

"Are you not those to whom My revelations were recited, and you dubbed them as lies?"

# 2779

They will say: "Our Lord! Our misfortune prevailed over us. We were indeed an erring people.

# 2780

Our Lord! Take us out of this. Then if we revert (to evil-doing) we shall indeed be wrongdoers."

# 2781

Allah will say: "Away from Me; stay where you are and do not address Me.

# 2782

You are those that when a party of My servants said: 'Our Lord, we believe, so forgive us, and have mercy on us, for You are the Best of those that are merciful,'
