All power belongs to Allah both before and after. On that day will the believers rejoice

# 3414

at the victory granted by Allah. He grants victory to whomsoever He pleases. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Compassionate.

# 3415

This is Allah's promise and He does not go back on His promise. But most people do not know.

# 3416

People simply know the outward aspect of the worldly life but are utterly heedless of the Hereafter.

# 3417

Do they not reflect on themselves? Allah created the heavens and the earth and whatever lies between them in Truth and for an appointed term. Yet many people deny that they will meet their Lord.

# 3418

Have they not travelled through the earth that they may observe what was the end of their predecessors who were far mightier and tilled the land and built upon it more than these have ever built? And Allah's Messengers came to them with Clear Signs. It was not Allah Who wronged them, but it is they who wronged themselves.

# 3419

Evil was the end of those evil-doers, for they gave the lie to Allah's Signs and scoffed at them.

# 3420

Allah creates in the first instance and will later repeat it. Thereafter it is to Him that you shall be sent back.

# 3421

On that Day when the Hour will come to pass, the criminals shall be dumbfounded.

# 3422

None whom they had associated with Allah in His Divinity will intercede on their behalf; rather, they will disown those whom they had set up as Allah's associates in His Divinity.

# 3423

On that Day when the Hour will come to pass, people will be split into groups.

# 3424

Then those who believed and acted righteously will be placed in a Garden and will be happy and jubilant.

# 3425

As for those who disbelieved and gave the lie to Our Signs and to the encounter of the Hereafter, they will be arraigned for chastisement.

# 3426

So glorify Allah in the evening and the morning.

# 3427

His is all praise in the heavens and in the earth; (and glorify Him) in the afternoon and when the sun begins to decline.

# 3428

He brings forth the living from the dead and brings forth the dead from the living, and revives the earth after it is dead. Likewise will you be raised to life (after you die).

# 3429

And of His Signs is that He created you from dust and behold, you became human beings, and are multiplying around (the earth).

# 3430

And of His Signs is that He has created mates for you from your own kind that you may find peace in them and He has set between you love and mercy. Surely there are Signs in this for those who reflect.

# 3431

And of His Signs is the creation of the heavens and the earth and the diversity of your tongues and colours. Indeed there are Signs in this for the wise.

# 3432

And of His Signs is your sleeping at night and your seeking His Bounty during the day. Indeed there are Signs in this for those who hearken.

# 3433

And of His Signs is that He shows you lightning, arousing both fear and hope, and sends down water from the sky and revives the earth after it is dead. Indeed there are Signs in this for those who use their reason.

# 3434

And of His Signs is that the sky and the earth stand firm by His command. Then no sooner than He summons you out of the earth you will come forth.

# 3435

To Him belong all who are in the heavens and all who are on the earth. All are in obedience to Him.

# 3436

It is He Who creates in the first instance and it is He Who will repeat the creation, and that is easier for Him. His is the loftiest attribute in the heavens and the earth. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 3437

He sets forth for you a parable from your own lives. Do you have among your slaves some who share with you the sustenance that We have bestowed on you so that you become equals in it, all being alike, and then you would hold them in fear as you fear each other? Thus do We make plain the Signs for those who use reason.

# 3438

But the wrong-doers follow their desires without any knowledge. Who, then, can show the way to him whom Allah lets go astray? Such shall have no helpers.

# 3439

(O Prophet and his followers), turn your face singlemindedly to the true Faith and adhere to the true nature on which Allah has created human beings. The mould fashioned by Allah cannot be altered. That is the True, Straight Faith, although most people do not know.

# 3440

(Adhere to the True Faith and) turn to Him, and hold Him in awe, and establish Prayer, and do not be of those who associate others with Allah in His Divinity,

# 3441

those who have split up their religion and have become divided into sects, each party exulting in what they have.

# 3442

(Such are human beings) that when any misfortune befalls them, they cry to their Lord, penitently turning to Him. But no sooner that He lets them have a taste of His Mercy than some of them begin associating others with their Lord in His Divinity

# 3443

so that they may show ingratitude to Us for the favours We had bestowed upon them. So, enjoy yourselves a while; but then you shall soon come to know.

# 3444

Have We sent down any sanction which provides support to their associating others with Allah in His Divinity?

# 3445

When We make people have a taste of Our Mercy, they exult in it; and when any misfortune befalls them in consequence of their deeds, then lo and behold, they despair.

# 3446

Do they not see that Allah enlarges and straitens the sustenance of those whom He pleases? There are Signs in this for those who believe.

# 3447

So give his due to the near of kin, and to the needy, and to the wayfarer. That is better for those who desire to please Allah. It is they who will prosper.

# 3448

Whatever you pay as interest so that it may increase the wealth of people does not increase in the sight of Allah. As for the Zakah that you give, seeking with it Allah's good pleasure, that is multiplied manifold.

# 3449

It is Allah Who created you, then bestowed upon you your sustenance, and He will cause you to die and then will bring you back to life. Can any of those whom you associate with Allah in His Divinity! do any such thing? Glory be to Him and exalted be He above whatever they associate with Allah in His Divinity.

# 3450

Evil has become rife on the land and at sea because of men's deeds; this in order that He may cause them to have a taste of some of their deeds; perhaps they will turn back (from evil).

# 3451

(O Prophet), say: Traverse in the earth and see what was the end of those who went before you: most of them associated others with Allah in His Divinity.

# 3452

So turn your face exclusively towards the True Faith before there comes the Day whose coming from Allah cannot be averted, the Day when people will split into groups.

# 3453

He who disbelieves will suffer the consequence of it and he who acts righteously, they will pave the way for their own good

# 3454

so that Allah may, out of His Bounty, reward those who believe and act righteously. Verily He does not love the unbelievers.

# 3455

And of His Signs is that He sends winds to herald good tidings and that He may give you a taste of His Mercy, and that ships may sail at His bidding, and you may seek His Bounty and give thanks to Him.

# 3456

We sent Messengers before you to their respective nations, and they brought Clear Signs to them. Then We took vengeance upon those who acted wickedly. It was incumbent on Us to come to the aid of the believers.

# 3457

Allah sends the winds that stir up clouds and then He spreads them in the sky as He pleases and splits them into different fragments, whereafter you see drops of rain pouring down from them. He then causes the rain to fall on whomsoever of His servants He pleases, and lo, they rejoice at it,

# 3458

although before that they were given to despair.

# 3459

See, then, the tokens of Allah's Mercy: how He revives the earth after it is dead. Verily He is the One Who will revive the dead. He has power over everything.

# 3460

But if We were to send a wind and then their tilth has become yellow, they would never cease to disbelieve.

# 3461

(O Prophet), you cannot make the dead hear, nor can you make the deaf hear your call when they turn back in retreat,

# 3462

nor can you guide the blind out of their error. You can make none hear (your call) except those who believe in Our Signs and have surrendered themselves (to Him).

# 3463

It is Allah Who created you in a state of weakness; then after weakness He gave you strength, then after strength He made you weak and old. He creates what He pleases. He is All-Knowing, All-Powerful.

# 3464

On that Day when the Hour will come to pass the wicked shall swear that they had stayed (in the world) no more than an hour. Thus they used to be deceived in the life of the world.

# 3465

But those who had been endowed with knowledge and faith shall say: According to Allah's Record you have stayed till the Day of Resurrection. Now, this is the Day of Resurrection. But you did not know.

# 3466

So that will be the Day when the excuses of the wrong-doers will not avail them, nor will they be asked to make amends.

# 3467

In the Qur'an We have explained things to people in myriad ways. But no matter what Sign you bring to them, those who are resolved upon denying the Truth will say: You are given to falsehood.

# 3468

Thus does Allah seal the hearts of those who have no knowledge.

# 3469

Therefore, (O Prophet), have patience. Surely Allah's promise is true. Let those who lack certainty not cause you to be unsteady.

# 3470

Alif. Lam. Mim.

# 3471

These are the verses of the Wise Book,

# 3472

a guidance and mercy for the doers of good,

# 3473

who establish Prayer and pay Zakah, and have firm faith in the Hereafter.

# 3474

It is they who are on true guidance from their Lord, and it is they who shall prosper.

# 3475

There are some human beings who purchase an enchanting diversion in order to lead people away from the way of Allah without having any knowledge, who hold the call to the Way of Allah to ridicule. A humiliating chastisement awaits them.

# 3476

When Our verses are recited to such a person, he arrogantly turns away, as though he had not heard them, or as though there was a deafness in his ears. So announce to him the tidings of a grievous chastisement.

# 3477

Surely those who believe and do good deeds shall have Gardens of Bliss.

# 3478

They shall abide in them forever. This is Allah's promise that shall come true. He is the Most Powerful, the Most Wise.

# 3479

He created the heavens without any pillars visible to you and He placed mountains in the earth as pegs lest it should turn topsy turvy with you, and He dispersed all kinds of animals over the earth, and sent down water from the sky causing all kinds of excellent plants to grow on it.

# 3480

Such is Allah's creation. Show me, then, what any others, apart from Allah, have created. Nay, the fact is that the wrong-doers are in manifest error.

# 3481

We bestowed wisdom upon Luqman, (enjoining): Give thanks to Allah. Whoso gives thanks to Allah, does so to his own good. And whoso disbelieves (let him know that) Allah is All-Sufficient, Immensely Praiseworthy.

# 3482

And call to mind when Luqman said to his son while exhorting him: My son, do not associate others with Allah in His Divinity. Surely, associating others with Allah in His Divinity is a mighty wrong.

# 3483

We enjoined upon man to be dutiful to his parents. His mother bore him in weakness upon weakness, and his weaning lasted two years. (We, therefore, enjoined upon him): Give thanks to Me and to your parents. To Me is your ultimate return.

# 3484

But if they press you to associate others with Me in My Divinity, (to associate) those regarding whom you have no knowledge (that they are My associates), do not obey them. And yet treat them well in this world, and follow the way of him who turns to Me in devotion. Eventually it is to Me that all of you shall return, and I shall then tell you all that you did.

# 3485

(Luqman said): Son, Allah will bring forth everything even if it be as small as the grain of a mustard seed even though it be hidden inside a rock or (anywhere) in the heavens or earth. Allah is Most Subtle, All-Aware.

# 3486

Son, establish Prayer, enjoin all that is good and forbid all that is evil, and endure with patience whatever affliction befalls you. Surely these have been emphatically enjoined.

# 3487

Do not (contemptuously) turn your face away from people, nor tread haughtily upon earth. Allah does not love the arrogant and the vainglorious.

# 3488

Be moderate in your stride and lower your voice. Verily the most disgusting of all voices is the braying of the donkey.

# 3489

Have you not seen that Allah has subjected to your service all that is in the heavens and on the earth and has abundantly bestowed upon you all His bounties, both visible and invisible? Yet some persons dispute regarding Allah without having any knowledge or guidance or any illuminating Book.

# 3490

When they are told: Follow what Allah has revealed, they say: We will rather follow that which we have found our forefathers following. (Will they follow that) even though Satan might invite them to the chastisement of the Blazing Fire?

# 3491

Whoever surrenders himself to Allah and lives righteously grasps the most firm handle. The ultimate decision of all matters rests with Allah.

# 3492

So let the unbelief of the unbeliever not grieve you. To Us is their return and then We shall inform them of all that they did. Surely Allah knows well even the secrets that are hidden in the breasts (of people).

# 3493

We allow them to enjoy themselves a while in the world and then We shall drive them in utter helplessness to a harsh chastisement.

# 3494

If you were to ask them: Who created the heavens and the earth? they will certainly reply: Allah. Say: All praise and thanks be to Allah. Yet most of them do not know.

# 3495

All that is in the heavens and the earth belongs to Allah. Verily He is All-Sufficient, Immensely Praiseworthy.

# 3496

If all the trees on earth become pens, and the sea replenished by seven more seas were to supply them with ink, the Words of Allah would not be exhausted. Verily Allah is Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 3497

To create all of you or to resurrect all of you is to Him like (creating or resurrecting) a single person. Verily Allah is All-Hearing, All-Seeing.

# 3498

Do you not see that Allah makes the night phase into the day and makes the day phase into the night and has subjected the sun and the moon to His will so that each of them is pursuing its course till an appointed time? (Do you not know that) Allah is well aware of all that you do?

# 3499

All this is because Allah, He alone, is the Truth and all that which they call upon beside Him is false. Surely Allah, He alone, is All-High, Incomparably Great.

# 3500

Do you not see that ships sail in the sea by Allah's Grace that He may show you some of His Signs? Surely there are Signs in this for everyone who is steadfast, thankful.

# 3501

When waves engulf them (in the sea) like canopies, they call upon Allah, consecrating their faith solely to Him. But when He delivers them safely to the land, some of them become lukewarm. None denies Our Signs except the perfidious, the ungrateful.

# 3502

O people, fear (the wrath) of your Lord, and dread the Day when no father will stand for his child, nor any child stand for his father. Surely Allah's promise is true. So let the life of this world not beguile you, nor let the Deluder delude you about Allah.

# 3503

Surely Allah alone has the knowledge of the Hour. It is He Who sends down the rain and knows what is in the wombs, although no person knows what he will earn tomorrow, nor does he know in which land he will die. Indeed, Allah is All-Knowing, All-Aware.

# 3504

Alif. Lam. Mim.

# 3505

This Book, beyond all doubt, was revealed by the Lord of the Universe.

# 3506

Or do they say: He has fabricated it? Nay, it is the Truth from your Lord so that you may warn a people to whom no warner came before you; perhaps they will be guided to the Right Way.

# 3507

It is Allah Who created the heavens and the earth and all that is between the two, in six days, and then He established Himself on the Throne. You have no guardian or intercessor other than He. Will you, then, not take heed?

# 3508

He governs from the heaven to the earth and then the record (of this governance) goes up to Him in a day whose measure is a thousand years in your reckoning.

# 3509

He knows all that is beyond as well as all that is within a creature's sense-perception. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Compassionate,

# 3510

He Who excelled in the creation of all that He created. He originated the creation of man from clay,

# 3511

then made his progeny from the extract of a mean fluid,

# 3512

then He duly proportioned him, and breathed into him of His spirit, and bestowed upon you ears and eyes and hearts. And yet, little thanks do you give.

# 3513

They say: Shall we be created afresh after we have become lost in the earth? Nay, the fact is that they deny that they will meet their Lord.

# 3514

Tell them: The angel of death who has been charged with your souls shall gather you, and then you shall be brought back to your Lord.

# 3515

Would that you could see the guilty standing before their Lord with their heads downcast, (saying to Him): Our Lord, we have now seen and heard, so send us back (to the world) that we might act righteously. For now we have come to have firm faith.

# 3516

(They will be told): If We had so willed, We could have bestowed guidance on every person. But the Word from Me that I will fill Hell with men and jinn, all together, has been fulfilled.

# 3517

So taste the chastisement on account of your forgetting the encounter of this Day. We, too, have forgotten you. Taste the eternal chastisement as a requital for your misdeeds.

# 3518

None believes in Our Signs except those who, when they are given good counsel through Our verses, fall down prostrate and celebrate the praise of their Lord and do not wax proud.

# 3519

Their sides forsake their beds, and they call upon their Lord in fear and hope, and expend (in charity) out of the sustenance We have granted them.

# 3520

No one knows what delights of the eyes are kept hidden for them as a reward for their deeds.

# 3521

Would a true believer be like him who was an evil-doer? Surely they are not equal.

# 3522

As for those who believe and act righteously, theirs shall be Gardens to dwell in, a hospitality to reward them for their deeds.

# 3523

As for the evil-doers, their refuge shall be the Fire. Every time they want to escape from it they shall be driven back and shall be told: Taste the chastisement of the Fire which you used to reject as a lie.

# 3524

We shall certainly have them taste some chastisement in this world in addition to the greater chastisement (of the Hereafter); perhaps they will retract (from their transgression).

# 3525

And who is more unjust than he who is given good counsel through the Signs of his Lord and yet he turns away from them? Surely We will exact full retribution from such criminals.

# 3526

Verily We bestowed the Book upon Moses. So entertain no doubt if (the Prophet Muhammad) received the same. We had made that Book a guidance for the Children of Israel,

# 3527

and when they remained steadfast and firmly believed in Our Signs, We created among them leaders who guided people by Our command.

# 3528

Surely your Lord will judge among them on the Day of Resurrection concerning the matters about which the Children of Israel used to differ.

# 3529

Did (these historical events) not make them realise that We destroyed many nations before them amidst whose dwellings they now move about? Surely there are many Signs in this. Are they unable to hear?

# 3530

Have they not seen that We drive water to the parched land, thereby bringing forth crops which they and their cattle eat? Are they unable to see?

# 3531

They say: If you are truthful, (tell us) when will the Judgement come?

# 3532

Tell them: If the unbelievers were to believe on the Day of Judgement that will not avail them. For then they will be granted no respite.

# 3533

So (leave them to themselves and) turn away from them and wait; they too are waiting.

# 3534

O Prophet, fear Allah and do not obey the unbelievers and the hypocrites. Verily Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.

# 3535

Follow that which is revealed to you from your Lord. Verily Allah is fully aware of all that you do.

# 3536

Put your trust in Allah: Allah is sufficient as Guardian.

# 3537

Allah has never put two hearts within one person's body; nor has He made your wives, whom you compare to your mothers' backs (to divorce them), your true mothers; nor has He made those whom you adopt as sons your own sons. These are only words that you utter with your mouths. But Allah proclaims the Truth and directs you to the Right Path.

# 3538

Call your adopted sons after their true fathers; that is more equitable in the sight of Allah. But if you do not know their true fathers, then regard them as your brethren in faith and as allies. You will not be taken to task for your mistaken utterances, but you will be taken to task for what you say deliberately. Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 3539

Surely the Prophet has a greater claim over the believers than they have over each other, and his wives are their mothers. According to the Book of Allah, blood relatives have greater claim over each other than the rest of the believers and the Emigrants (in the cause of Allah), except that you may do some good to your allies (if you so wish). This is inscribed in the Book of Allah.

# 3540

And call to mind, (O Prophet), when We took the covenant from all Prophets; and also from you and Noah and Abraham, Moses, and Jesus the son of Mary. We took from them a solemn covenant

# 3541

so that (their Lord) may question the truthful about their truthfulness. As for the unbelievers, He has kept a painful chastisement in store for them.

# 3542

Believers, call to mind Allah's favour to you when enemy hosts invaded you. Then We sent against them a wind and hosts that you did not see although Allah was observing all that you were then doing.

# 3543

When they came upon you from above you and from below you, when your eyes were stupefied with horror and your hearts leapt to your throats, and you began to entertain diverse thoughts about Allah.

# 3544

The believers were then put to a severe test and were most violently convulsed.

# 3545

And call to mind when the hypocrites and all those with diseased hearts said: All that Allah and His Messenger had promised us was nothing but deceit.

# 3546

And when a section of them said: (O people of Yathrib), now there is no place for you to stay, so turn back. (And call to mind) when a section of them was seeking permission from the Prophet to leave, saying: Our houses are exposed (to attack), although they were not exposed (to attack); they only wished to flee (from the battle-front).

# 3547

If the enemy were to enter the town from various directions, and they were summoned to act treacherously, they would have succumbed to it and would have shown little reluctance in doing so.

# 3548

They had earlier covenanted with Allah that they would not turn their backs in flight. And a covenant made with Allah must needs be answered for.

# 3549

(O Prophet), tell them: If you run away from death or slaying, this flight will not avail you. You will have little time after that to enjoy (the pleasures of life).

# 3550

Say (to them): Who can protect you from Allah if He desires an evil for you? And who can prevent Him if He desires to show mercy to you? They shall find none other than Allah to be their protector or helper.

# 3551

Allah knows well those of you who create obstructions (in war efforts) and say to their brethren: Come and join us. They hardly take any part in battle.

# 3552

They are utterly niggardly (in coming to your aid). Whenever there is danger, you will see them looking at you, their eyes rolling as though they were on the verge of fainting at the approach of death. But when the danger passes away, their greed for wealth prompts them to greet you with their sharp, scissor-like tongues. These are the ones who never truly believed, and so Allah has caused their deeds to be reduced to naught. That is easy enough for Allah.

# 3553

They think that the invading confederates have not yet gone. But if the confederates were to mount another assault, they would wish to be in the desert among the bedouins and keep themselves informed about you from there. But even if they remained in your midst, hardly would they fight.

# 3554

Surely there was a good example for you in the Messenger of Allah, for all those who look forward to Allah and the Last Day and remember Allah much.

# 3555

As for the true believers, when they saw the invading confederates, they cried out: This is what Allah and His Messenger had promised us, and what Allah and His Messenger said was absolutely true. This only increased their faith and submission.

# 3556

Among the believers there are those who have remained true to the covenant they made with Allah. Among those some of them have fulfilled their vow and others await the appointed time. They have not changed in the least.

# 3557

(All this is) in order that Allah may reward the truthful for their truthfulness, and either punish the hypocrites or, if He so wills, accept their repentance. Verily Allah is Most Pardoning, Most Compassionate.

# 3558

Allah sent back the unbelievers empty-handed, their hearts seething with rage. Allah sufficed the believers in their fight. Allah is Most Powerful, Most Mighty.

# 3559

Allah brought down from their fortresses those People of the Book who had supported the invading confederates and cast such terror into their hearts that some of them you kill and some of them you take captive.

# 3560

Allah made you inherit their land, their dwellings, and their goods, and a piece of land on which you had not yet trodden. Verily Allah has power over all things.

# 3561

O Prophet, tell your wives: If you seek the world and its embellishments, then come and I will make some provision for you and release you in an honourable way.

# 3562

But if you seek Allah and His Messenger and the Abode of the Hereafter, then surely Allah has prepared a great reward for those of you who do good.

# 3563

Wives of the Prophet, if any of you commit flagrant indecency, her chastisement shall be doubled. That is easy for Allah.

# 3564

But whoever of you is obedient to Allah and His Messenger and does good deeds, Allah will double her reward. We have prepared for her a generous provision.

# 3565

Wives of the Prophet, you are not like other women. If you fear Allah, do not be too complaisant in your speech lest those with diseased hearts should covet you; but speak in a straight forward manner.

# 3566

And stay in your homes and do not go about displaying your allurements as in the former Time of Ignorance. Establish Prayer, give Zakah, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah only wishes to remove uncleanness from you, O members of the (Prophet's) household, and to purify you completely.

# 3567

Remember the Signs of Allah and the words of wisdom which are rehearsed in your homes. Verily Allah is All-Subtle, All-Aware.

# 3568

Surely the men who submit (to Allah) and the women who submit (to Allah), the men who have faith and the women who have faith, the men who are obedient and the women who are obedient, the men who are truthful and the women who are truthful; the men who are steadfast and the women who are steadfast, the men who humble themselves (to Allah) and the women who humble themselves (to Allah), the men who give alms and the women who give alms, the men who fast and the women who fast, the men who guard their chastity and the women who guard their chastity, the men who remember Allah much and the women who remember Allah much: for them has Allah prepared forgiveness and a mighty reward.

# 3569

It does not behove a believer, male or female, that when Allah and His Messenger have decided an affair they should exercise their choice. And whoever disobeys Allah and His Messenger has strayed to manifest error.

# 3570

(O Prophet), call to mind when you said to him whom Allah had favoured and you had favoured: Cleave to your wife and fear Allah, and you concealed within yourself for fear of people what Allah was to reveal, although Allah has greater right that you fear Him. So when Zayd had accomplished what he would of her, We gave her in marriage to you so that there should not be any constraint for the believers regarding the wives of their adopted sons after they had accomplished whatever they would of them. And Allah's command was bound to be accomplished.

# 3571

There could be no hindrance to the Prophet regarding what Allah ordained for him. Such has been Allah's Way (with the Prophets) who went before. Allah's command is a decree firmly determined.

# 3572

(This is Allah's Way) regarding those who deliver the Messages of Allah and who fear Him, and fear no one else than Allah. Allah is Sufficient as a Reckoner.

# 3573

Muhammad is not the father of any of your men, but he is the Messenger of Allah and the seal of the Prophets. Allah has full knowledge of everything.

# 3574

Believers, remember Allah much

# 3575

and glorify Him morning and evening.

# 3576

It is He Who lavishes His blessings on you and His angels invoke blessings on you that He may lead you out of darkness into light. He is Most Compassionate to the believers.

# 3577

On the Day they meet Him they will be greeted with: Peace. He has prepared for them a generous reward.

# 3578

O Prophet, We have sent you forth as a witness, a bearer of good tidings, and a warner,

# 3579

as one who calls people to Allah by His leave, and as a bright, shining lamp.

# 3580

Announce to the believers the good tidings that Allah has kept bounteous blessings in store for them.

# 3581

Do not yield to the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and disregard the hurt that comes from them, and put your trust in Allah. Allah suffices as the Guardian to entrust one's affairs to.

# 3582

Believers, when you marry believing women and then divorce them before you have touched them, you may not require them to observe a waiting period that you might reckon against them. So make provision for them and release them in an honourable manner.

# 3583

O Prophet, We have made lawful for you your wives whose bridal dues you have paid, and the slave-girls you possess from among the prisoners of war, and the daughters of your paternal uncles and paternal aunts, and the daughters of your maternal uncles and maternal aunts who have migrated with you, and a believing woman who gives herself to the Prophet and whom he wants to take in marriage. (O Prophet), this privilege is yours alone to the exclusion of other believers. We know well what restrictions We have imposed upon them as regards their wives and those whom their right hands possess, (and have exempted you from those restrictions) that there may be no constraint upon you. Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3584

Of them you may put off any of them you wish, and you may take any of them whom you wish, and you may call back any of those whom you had (temporarily) set aside: there will be no blame on you (on this account). It is likelier that they will thus be comforted, and will not grieve, and every one of them will be well-pleased with what you give them. Allah knows what is in your hearts. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Forbearing.

# 3585

Thereafter women will not be lawful for you, and it will not be lawful for you to take other wives in place of them, even though their beauty might please you, unless they be those whom your right hand owns. Allah is watchful over everything.

# 3586

Believers, enter not the houses of the Prophet without his permission, nor wait for a meal to be prepared; instead enter when you are invited to eat, and when you have had the meal, disperse. Do not linger in idle talk. That is hurtful to the Prophet but he does not express it out of shyness; but Allah is not ashamed of speaking out the Truth. And if you were to ask the wives of the Prophet for something, ask from behind a curtain. That is more apt for the cleanness of your hearts and theirs. It is not lawful for you to cause hurt to Allah's Messenger, nor to ever marry his wives after him. Surely that would be an enormous sin in Allah's sight.

# 3587

(It does not matter) whether you disclose something or conceal it, for Allah certainly knows everything.

# 3588

It will not be blameworthy for the wives of the Prophet if their fathers, their sons, their brothers, their brothers' sons, their sisters' sons, and the women with whom they have social relations, and the persons whom their right hands possess enter their houses. (O women), shun disobeying Allah. Allah is watchful over everything.

# 3589

Allah and His angels bless the Prophet. Believers, invoke blessings and peace on him.

# 3590

Verily those who cause annoyance to Allah and His Messenger - Allah has cursed them in this world and in the Hereafter and has prepared for them a humiliating chastisement.

# 3591

Those who cause hurt to believing men and to believing women have invited upon themselves a calumny and a manifest sin.

# 3592

O Prophet, enjoin your wives and your daughters and the believing women, to draw a part of their outer coverings around them. It is likelier that they will be recognised and not molested. Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3593

If the hypocrites and those in whose hearts there is a sickness, and the scandal mongers in Madinah do not desist from their vile acts, We shall urge you to take action against them, and then they will hardly be able to stay in the city with you.

# 3594

They shall be cursed from all around and they shall be ruthlessly killed wherever they are seized.

# 3595

This has been Allah's Way with those who have gone before, and you shall find no change in Allah's Way.

# 3596

People ask you concerning the Hour (of Resurrection). Say: Allah alone has knowledge of it. What do you know? Perhaps the Hour is nigh.

# 3597

Allah has cursed the unbelievers and has prepared for them a Blazing Fire;

# 3598

therein they shall abide for ever. They shall find none to protect or help them.

# 3599

On that Day when their faces shall be turned around in the Fire, they will say: Would that we had obeyed Allah and obeyed the Messenger.

# 3600

They will say: Our Lord, we obeyed our chiefs and our great ones, and they turned us away from the Right Way.

# 3601

Our Lord, mete out to them a double chastisement and lay upon them a mighty curse.

# 3602

Believers, do not be like those who distressed Moses and then Allah declared him quit of the ill they spoke about him; and he had a high standing with Allah.

# 3603

Believers, fear Allah and speak the truth:

# 3604

Allah will set your deeds right for you and will forgive you your sins. Whoever obeys Allah and His Messenger has achieved a great triumph.

# 3605

We offered the trust to the heavens and the earth and the mountains, but they refused to carry it and were afraid of doing so; but man carried it. Surely he is wrong-doing, ignorant.

# 3606

(The consequence of man's carrying the trust is) that Allah may chastise hypocritical men and hypocritical women and accept the repentance of believing men and believing women. He is Most Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 3607

All praise be to Allah to Whom belongs all that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth, and all praise be to Him in the World to Come. He is Most Wise, All-Aware.

# 3608

He knows what penetrates into the earth and what goes forth from it, what descends from the heaven and what ascends to it. He is the Most Merciful, the Most Forgiving.

# 3609

The unbelievers say: How come the Hour is not coming upon us! Say to them: Yes indeed, by my Lord, by Him Who fully knows the realm beyond the ken of perception, that the Hour shall inevitably come upon you. Nothing escapes Him, not even the smallest particle in the heavens or the earth; nor is anything smaller or bigger than that but is in a Manifest Book.

# 3610

(The Hour shall come) that He may reward those who believe and do righteous deeds. Theirs shall be forgiveness and a generous provision.

# 3611

As for those who worked against Our Signs in order to frustrate them, they shall suffer a painful chastisement.

# 3612

(O Prophet), those who have knowledge see clearly that what has been revealed to you from your Lord is the Truth and directs to the Way of the Most Mighty, the Immensely Praiseworthy Lord.

# 3613

The unbelievers say: Shall we direct you to the man who tells you that when you have been utterly broken to pieces, you will be raised to life again?

# 3614

Has he forged a lie against Allah, or is he afflicted with madness? Nay, but those who do not believe in the Hereafter are doomed to be chastised and are far gone in error.

# 3615

Do they not see how the heavens and the earth encompass them from the front and the rear? We could, if We so wished, cause the earth to swallow them or let fragments of the sky fall upon them. Verily there is a Sign in this for every servant (of Allah) who penitently turns to Him.

# 3616

We bestowed Our favour upon David. (We commanded): O mountains, sing Allah's praises with him; (and so did We command) the birds. We softened the iron for him, (saying):

# 3617

Fashion coats of mail and measure their links with care and act righteously. I am watching over whatever you do.

# 3618

And We subdued the wind to Solomon: its morning course was a month's journey and its evening course was a month's journey. We gave him a spring flowing with molten brass, and We subdued for him jinn who, by his Lord's permission, worked before him. Such of them as swerved from Our commandment, We let them taste the chastisement of the Blazing Fire.

# 3619

They made for him whatever he would desire: stately buildings, images, basins like water-troughs and huge, built-in-cauldrons: Work, O house of David, in thankfulness (to your Lord). Few of My servants are truly thankful.

# 3620

When We executed Our decree of death on Solomon, nothing indicated to the jinn that he was dead except a worm eating away his staff. So when Solomon fell down, the jinn realised that had they known what lies in the realm beyond perception, they would not have continued to be in this humiliating chastisement.

# 3621

For Sheba there was also a Sign in their dwelling place: the two gardens to the right and to the left. Eat of your Lord's provision, and render thanks to Him. Most pleasant is your land and Most Forgiving is your Lord.

# 3622

But they turned away and so We let loose upon them a devastating flood that swept away the dams and replaced their gardens by two others bearing bitter fruits, tamarisks, and a few lote trees.

# 3623

Thus did We retribute them for their ingratitude. And none do We retribute in this manner except the utterly ungrateful.

# 3624

We placed other prominent towns between them, the towns that We had blessed and had set well-measured stages between them. Move back and forth between them, night and day, in perfect security.

# 3625

But they said: Lord, make the stages of our journeys longer. They wronged their own selves so We reduced them to bygone tales, and utterly tore them to pieces. Verily there are Signs in this for everyone who is steadfast and thankful.

# 3626

Iblis found his estimate of them to be true, and they followed him, except a party of the believers.

# 3627

Iblis had no authority over them and whatever happened was in order that We might know him who believes in the Hereafter as distinct from him who is in doubt about it. Your Lord is watchful over everything.

# 3628

(O Prophet), say to those who associate others with Allah in His Divinity: Call upon those whom you fancied to be deities beside Allah. They own not even the smallest particle, neither in the heavens nor on the earth; nor do they have any share in the ownership of either of them. Nor is any of them even a helper of Allah.

# 3629

No intercession can avail with Allah except for him whom Allah permits (to intercede). When their hearts are relieved of fright they will ask the intercessors: What did your Lord say? They will reply: (He said) what is right, and He is the High, the Great.

# 3630

Ask them, (O Prophet): Who provides you sustenance from the heavens and the earth? Say: Allah. Now, inevitably only one of us is rightly guided, either we or you; and the other is in manifest error.

# 3631

Tell them: You will not be called to account about the guilt we committed, nor will we be called to account for what you did.

# 3632

Say: Our Lord will bring us together and then He will rightly judge between us. He is the Great Judge, the All-Knowing.

# 3633

Say: Show me those whom you have attached to Him as His associates (in Divinity). Nay, Allah alone is Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 3634

(O Prophet), We have not sent you forth but as a herald of good news and a warner for all mankind. But most people do not know.

# 3635

They ask you: When will this promise (of Resurrection) be fulfilled, if what you say is true?

# 3636

Say: Your day is appointed, you can neither hold back its coming by an hour, nor hasten it by an hour.

# 3637

The unbelievers say: We shall never believe in this Qur'an, nor in any Scripture before it. If you could only see the wrong-doers arrayed before their Lord, each bandying charges against the other. Those who were suppressed will say to those who waxed arrogant: Had it not been for you, we would have been believers.

# 3638

The arrogant ones will retort to those who were suppressed: What! Did we bar you from the guidance after it came to you? Not at all; rather you yourselves were evil-doers.

# 3639

Those who were suppressed will say to those who waxed arrogant: By no means; it was your scheming, night and day, when you would enjoin us to disbelieve in Allah and set up others as equals to Him. When they are confronted with the chastisement, they will be remorseful in their hearts. We shall put fetters around the necks of the unbelievers. Can people be requited except for their deeds?

# 3640

We never sent a warner to any town but its wealthy ones said: We disbelieve in the Message you have brought.

# 3641

They always said: We have more wealth and children than you have, and we shall not be chastised.

# 3642

(O Prophet), say to them: My Lord grants provision abundantly to whomsoever He pleases and straitens it for whomsoever He pleases. But most people do not know this.

# 3643

It is not your riches nor your children that make you near-stationed to Us, except for him who has faith and acts righteously; it is they who will receive double the recompense for their deeds. They shall live in lofty mansions in perfect peace.

# 3644

As for those who work against Our Signs so as to frustrate them, they shall be arraigned into the chastisement.

# 3645

Say, (O Prophet): Verily, my Lord grants provision abundantly to whomsoever He pleases and straitens it for whomsoever He pleases. Whatever you spend, He will replace it. He is the Best of all Providers.

# 3646

And on the Day when He will muster them all and will ask the angels: Are they the ones who worshipped you?

# 3647

They will reply: Glory to You! You are our Protector, not they. Nay, they rather used to worship the jinn. Most of them believe in them.

# 3648

Today none of you has the power to benefit or harm another; and We shall say to the evil-doers: Taste now the chastisement of the Fire which you used to deny, calling it a lie.

# 3649

When Our Clear Signs are rehearsed to them they say: This is a person who wants to turn you away from the deities whom your ancestors worshipped. They say: This is nothing but an invented falsehood. And when the Truth came to the unbelievers they declared: This is nothing but plain sorcery,

# 3650

whereas We gave them no Books that they could study nor sent to them any warner before you.

# 3651

Those who went before them also denounced (Allah's Messengers) as liars. They have not attained even a tenth of what We had given them. But when they rejected My Messengers, calling them liars, how terrible was My chastisement!

# 3652

Say to them, (O Prophet): I give you but one counsel: stand up (for heaven's sake), singly and in pairs, and then think: what is it in your companion (to wit, Muhammad) that could be deemed as madness? He is nothing but a warner, warning you before the coming of a grevious chastisement.

# 3653

Say to them: Whatever recompense I might ask of you, it shall be yours. My recompense is with Allah, and He is witness over everything.

# 3654

Say to them: My Lord hurls down the Truth (upon me). He knows fully all that lies beyond the range of perception.

# 3655

Say: The Truth has come and falsehood can neither originate nor recreate anything.

# 3656

Say: If I go astray then the hurt of straying will come only upon me. But if I am rightly-guided, that is only because of the revelation that my Lord makes to me. He is All-Hearing, Ever Nigh.

# 3657

If you could only see when the unbelievers will go about in a state of terror. They will have no escape and will be seized from a place near at hand.

# 3658

They will then say: We believe in it; but whence can they attain it from so far-off a place?

# 3659

They disbelieved in it before and indulged in conjectures from far away.

# 3660

A barrier will be placed between them and what they desire, as was done with the likes of them before. Surely they were in a disquieting doubt.

# 3661

All praise be to Allah, the Fashioner of the heavens and earth, Who appointed angels as His message bearers, having two, three, four wings. He adds to His creation whatever He pleases. Verily Allah has power over everything.

# 3662

Whatever Mercy Allah accords to people, none can withhold; and whatever He withholds, no other will be able to release after Him. He is Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 3663

O people, remember Allah's favour upon you. Is there any creator, apart from Allah, who provides you your sustenance out of the heavens and earth? There is no god but He. Whither are you, then, being misdirected?

# 3664

(O Prophet), (there is nothing novel in it) if they cry lies to you; Messengers before you were also cried lies to. To Allah shall all matters be sent back.

# 3665

O people, assuredly Allah's promise is true. So let the life of the world not delude you, and let not the Deluder delude you concerning Allah.

# 3666

Surely Satan is an enemy to you. Therefore, do take him as an enemy. He calls his followers to his way so that they may be among the inmates of the Fire.

# 3667

A severe chastisement lies in store for those that disbelieve, but there is pardon and a great reward for those that believe and work righteous deeds.

# 3668

(How awful is the straying of the person) for whom his evil deed has been embellished so that it looks fair to him? The fact is that Allah causes whomsoever He will to fall into error and shows the Right Way to whomsoever He will. So, (O Prophet), let not your life go to waste sorrowing over them. Allah is well aware of all that they do.

# 3669

It is Allah Who sends forth winds which then set the clouds in motion, which We drive to some dead land giving a fresh life to earth after it had become dead. Such will be the resurrection of the dead.

# 3670

He who seeks glory, let him know that all glory belongs to Allah alone. To Him do good words go up, and righteous action uplifts them. But those who contrive evil deeds, a severe punishment lies in store for them, and their contriving will come to naught.

# 3671

Allah created you from dust, then from a drop of sperm, then He made you into pairs. No female conceives, nor delivers (a child) except with His knowledge. None is given a long life nor is any diminished in his life but it is written in a Book. Surely that is quite easy for Allah.

# 3672

The two masses of water are not alike. The one is sweet, sates thirst, and is pleasant to drink from, while the other is salt, bitter on the tongue. Yet from both you eat fresh meat, and extract from it ornaments that you wear; and you see ships cruising through it that you may seek of His Bounty and be thankful to Him.

# 3673

He causes the night to phase into the day and the day into the night, and He has subjected the sun and the moon, each running its course to an appointed term. That is Allah, your Lord; to Him belongs the Kingdom; but those whom you call upon, apart from Allah, possess not so much as the skin of a date-stone.

# 3674

If you call upon them, they cannot hear your prayer. And if they hear it, they cannot answer it. On the Day of Resurrection they will disown you for associating others with Allah in His Divinity. No one can inform you of the truth save the All-Aware.

# 3675

O people, it is you who stand in need of Allah; as for Allah, He is Self-Sufficient, Immensely Praiseworthy.

# 3676

If He wishes, He can remove you and put in your place a new creation.

# 3677

That surely is not difficult for Allah.

# 3678

No one can bear another's burden. If a heavily laden one should call another to carry his load, none of it shall be carried by the other, even though he be a near of kin. (O Prophet), you can warn only those who fear their Lord without seeing Him and establish Prayer. Whoever purifies himself does so to his own good. To Allah is the final return.

# 3679

The blind and the seeing are not alike,

# 3680

nor darkness and light;

# 3681

nor cool shade and torrid heat;

# 3682

nor are the living and the dead alike. Allah makes to hear whomsoever He wishes, but you, (O Prophet), cannot cause to hear those who are in their graves.

# 3683

You are no more than a warner.

# 3684

We have sent you with the Truth to proclaim good news and to warn. Never has there been a nation but a warner came to it.

# 3685

If they give the lie to you now, those that went before them also gave the lie to their Messengers when they came to them with Clear Proofs, with Scriptures, and with the Illuminating Book.

# 3686

Then I seized those who denied the Truth, and how terrible was My punishment!

# 3687

Do you not see that Allah sent down water from the sky with which We brought forth fruits of diverse hues? In the mountains there are white and red, of diverse hues, and pitchy black;

# 3688

and human beings too, and beasts, and cattle -- diverse are their hues. From among His servants, it is only those who know that fear Allah. Verily Allah is Most Mighty, Most Forgiving.

# 3689

Surely those who recite the Book of Allah and establish Prayer and spend, privately and publicly, out of what We have provided them, look forward to a trade that shall suffer no loss;

# 3690

(a trade in which they have invested their all) so that Allah may pay them their wages in full and may add to them out of His Bounty. He is Most Forgiving, Most Appreciative.

# 3691

(O Prophet), the Book We have revealed to you is the Truth, confirming the Books that came before it. Verily Allah is well aware of His servants and sees everything.

# 3692

Then We bequeathed the Book to those of Our servants that We chose. Now, some of them wrong themselves and some follow the medium course; and some, by Allah's leave, vie with each other in acts of goodness. That is the great bounty.

# 3693

They shall enter the everlasting Gardens, shall be adorned with bracelets of gold and with pearls, and their apparel therein shall be silk.

# 3694

They will say: All praise be to Allah Who has taken away all sorrow from us. Surely our Lord is Most Forgiving, Most Appreciative;

# 3695

(the Lord) Who, out of His Bounty, has made us dwell in an abode wherein no toil, nor fatigue affects us.

# 3696

As for those who disbelieved, the Fire of Hell awaits them. There they shall not be finished off and die; nor will the torment (of Hell) be lightened for them. Thus do We requite every thankless being.

# 3697

They will cry out in Hell and say: Our Lord, let us out so that we may act righteously, different from what we did before. (They will be told): Did we not grant you an age long enough for anyone to take heed if he had wanted to take heed? Besides, there came a warner to you. So have a taste of the torment now. None may come to the help of the wrong-doers.

# 3698

Surely Allah knows the Unseen in the heavens and the earth. He even knows the secrets hidden in people's breasts.

# 3699

It is He Who made you vicegerents in the earth. So whoever disbelieves will bear the burden of his unbelief. The unbelievers' unbelief adds nothing but Allah's wrath against them. The unbelievers' unbelief adds nothing but their own loss.

# 3700

Say to them (O Prophet): Have you ever seen those of your associates upon whom you call apart from Allah? Show me what have they created in the earth? Or do they have any partnership (with Allah) in the heavens? Or have We given them a Book so that they have a clear proof (for associating others with Allah in His Divinity)? Nay, what these wrong-doers promise each other is nothing but delusion.

# 3701

Surely Allah holds the heavens and the earth, lest they should be displaced there, for if they were displaced none would be able to hold them after Him. Surely He is Most Forbearing, Most Forgiving.

# 3702

Swearing by Allah their strongest oaths they claimed that if a warner came to them they would be better-guided than any other people. But when a warner did come to them, his coming only increased their aversion (to the Truth).

# 3703

They began to wax even more proud on earth and contrived evil designs although the contriving of evil designs only overtakes their authors. Are they waiting, then, for anything except what happened to the nations before them? You shall not find any change in the Way of Allah; and you shall not find anything that can ever alter the Way of Allah.

# 3704

Have they not journeyed in the earth to behold the end of those who went before them though they were stronger than them in might? Nothing in the heavens nor on earth can frustrate Him in the least. He is All-Knowing, All-Powerful.

# 3705

If Allah were to take people to task for their deeds, He would not leave any living creature on earth, but He grants them respite to an appointed time. When their appointed time comes to an end, surely Allah fully observes His servants.

# 3706

Ya'. Sin.

# 3707

By the Wise Qur'an,

# 3708

you are truly among the Messengers,

# 3709

on a Straight Way,

# 3710

(and this Qur'an) is a revelation from the Most Mighty, the Most Compassionate

# 3711

so that you may warn a people whose ancestors were not warned before wherefore they are heedless.

# 3712

Surely most of them merit the decree of chastisement; so they do not believe.

# 3713

We have put fetters around their necks which reach up to their chins so that they are standing with their heads upright,

# 3714

and We have put a barrier before them and a barrier behind them, and have covered them up, so they are unable to see.

# 3715

It is all the same for them whether you warn them or do not warn them for they shall not believe.

# 3716

You can warn only him who follows the Admonition and fears the Merciful Lord without seeing Him. Give such a one good tidings of forgiveness and a generous reward.

# 3717

We shall surely raise the dead to life and We record what they did and the traces of their deeds that they have left behind. We have encompassed that in a Clear Book.

# 3718

Recite to them, as a case in point, the story of the people of the town when the Messengers came to them.

# 3719

We sent to them two Messengers and they rejected both of them as liars. Then We strengthened them with a third (Messenger).

# 3720

They said: We have been sent to you as Messengers. The people of the town said: You are only human beings like ourselves, and the Merciful Lord has revealed nothing. You are simply lying.

# 3721

The Messengers said: Our Lord knows that we have indeed been sent to you

# 3722

and our duty is no more than to clearly convey the Message.

# 3723

The people of the town said: We believe you are an evil omen for us. If you do not desist, we will stone you or you will receive a grievous chastisement from us.

# 3724

The Messengers replied: Your evil omen is with you. (Are you saying this) because you were asked to take heed? The truth is that you are a people who have exceeded all bounds.

# 3725

In the meantime a man came running from the far end of the town, saying: My people, follow the Messengers;

# 3726

follow those who do not ask any recompense from you and are rightly-guided.

# 3727

Why should I not serve the One Who created me and to Whom all of you shall be sent back?

# 3728

What! Shall I take any deities apart from Him whose intercession will not avail me the least were the Merciful One to bring any adversity upon me, nor will they be able to rescue me?

# 3729

Surely in that case I should indeed be in evident error.

# 3730

I believe in your Lord; so listen to me.

# 3731

(Eventually they killed him and he was told): Enter Paradise. The man exclaimed: Would that my people knew

# 3732

for what reason Allah has forgiven me and placed me among the honoured ones.

# 3733

After him, We did not send down any hosts from the heaven; We stood in no need to send down any host.

# 3734

There was but a single Blast and suddenly they became silent and still.

# 3735

Alas for My servants! Never does a Messenger come to them but they mock him.

# 3736

Have they not seen how many nations before them did We destroy? Thereafter they never came back to them.

# 3737

All of them shall (one day) be gathered before Us.

# 3738

Let the dead earth be a Sign for them. We gave it life and produced from it grain whereof they eat.

# 3739

We made in it gardens of date-palms and vines, and We caused springs to gush forth

# 3740

that they might eat of its fruits. It was not their hands that made them. Will they not, then, give thanks?

# 3741

Holy is He Who created all things in pairs, whether it be of what the earth produces, and of themselves, and of what they do not know.

# 3742

And the night is another Sign for them. We strip the day from it and they become plunged in darkness.

# 3743

The sun is running its course to its appointed place. That is the ordaining of the All-Mighty, the All-Knowing.

# 3744

We have appointed stages for the moon till it returns in the shape of a dry old branch of palm-tree.

# 3745

Neither does it lie in the sun's power to overtake the moon nor can the night outstrip the day. All glide along, each in its own orbit.

# 3746

Another Sign for them is that We carried all their offspring in the laden vessel

# 3747

and then created for them other vessels like those on which they ride.

# 3748

Should We so wish, We can drown them, and there will be none to heed their cries of distress, nor will they be rescued.

# 3749

It is only Our Mercy (that rescues them) and enables enjoyment of life for a while.

# 3750

When it is said to such people: Guard yourselves against what is ahead of you and what has preceded you that mercy be shown to you (they pay scant heed to it).

# 3751

Never does any Sign of their Lord come to them, but they turn away from it.

# 3752

And when it is said to them: Spend (in the Way of Allah) out of the sustenance that Allah has provided you, the unbelievers say to the believers: Shall we feed him whom, Allah would have fed, had He so wished? Say: You are in evident error.

# 3753

They say: When will this threat (of Resurrection) come to pass? Tell us if indeed you are truthful.

# 3754

The Truth is that they are waiting for nothing but a mighty Blast to seize them the while they are disputing (in their worldly affairs),

# 3755

and they will not even be able to make a testament, nor to return to their households.

# 3756

Then the Trumpet shall be blown and lo! they will come out of their graves and be on the move towards their Lord,

# 3757

(nervously) exclaiming. Alas for us! Who roused us out of our sleeping-place? This is what the Merciful One had promised, and what (His) Messengers had said was true.

# 3758

Then there will simply be one single Blast, and all will have gathered before Us.

# 3759

Today no one shall suffer the least injustice, and you shall not be recompensed except according to your deeds.

# 3760

Indeed, the people of Paradise will be busy enjoying themselves:

# 3761

they and their spouses shall be reclining on their couches in shady groves;

# 3762

therein there will be all kinds of fruits to eat, and they shall have all that they desire.

# 3763

Peace shall be the word conveyed to them from their Merciful Lord.

# 3764

Criminals, separate yourselves from others today!

# 3765

Children of Adam, did I not command you not to serve Satan -- he is to you an open enemy

# 3766

and serve Me alone: this is the Straight Way?

# 3767

Still, he misguided a whole throng of you. Did you have no sense?

# 3768

Now this is the Hell of which you were warned.

# 3769

Burn in it on account of your disbelieving.

# 3770

Today We shall put a seal on their mouths, and their hands will speak to Us and their feet shall bear witness to what they had been doing.

# 3771

If We so willed, We would have put out their eyes, then they would rush to see the Way, but how would they be able to see?

# 3772

If We so willed, We would have transformed them where they were so that they would not go forward or backward.

# 3773

Whomsoever We grant a long life, We reverse him in his constitution. Do they still not understand?

# 3774

We did not teach him (to wit, the Messenger) poetry and it does not behove him. This is none but an Admonition, and a Clear Book

# 3775

that he may warn him who is alive and establish an argument against those that deny the Truth.

# 3776

Do they not see Our handiwork: We created for them cattle which they own?

# 3777

We have subjected the cattle to them so that some of them they ride and eat the flesh of others.

# 3778

They derive a variety of benefits and drinks from them. Will they, then, not give thanks?

# 3779

They set up deities apart from Allah, hoping that they will receive help from them.

# 3780

Those deities can render them no help. Yet these devotees act as though they were an army in waiting for them.

# 3781

Let not their words grieve you. Surely We know all things about them, what they conceal and what they reveal.

# 3782

Does man not see that We created him of a sperm drop, and lo! he is flagrantly contentious?

# 3783

He strikes for Us a similitude and forgot his own creation. He says: Who will quicken the bones when they have decayed?

# 3784

Say: He Who first brought them into being will quicken them; He knows well about every kind of creation;

# 3785

He Who created from a green tree a fire for you, a fire to light your stoves with.

# 3786

Has He Who created the heavens and the earth no power to create the likes of them? Yes, indeed, He is the Superb Creator.

# 3787

Whenever He wills a thing, He just commands it Be and it is.

# 3788

Holy is He Who has full control over everything, and to Him you shall all be recalled.

# 3789

By those who range themselves in rows;

# 3790

by those who reprove severely,

# 3791

and those who recite the Exhortation;

# 3792

surely your God is One,

# 3793

the Lord of the heavens and the earth and of whatever lies between the two, the Lord of the Easts.

# 3794

We have adorned the lower heaven with the adornment of the stars

# 3795

and have protected it from every rebellious satan.

# 3796

These satans cannot listen to what transpires in the High Council for they are pelted away from every side

# 3797

and are repelled. Theirs is an unceasing chastisement.

# 3798

And if any is able to snatch a fragment, he is pursued by a piercing flame.

# 3799

So ask them (that is, human beings): Were they harder to create than the objects We created? We created them from sticky clay.

# 3800

You marvel (at the wondrous creations of Allah) and they scoff at it,

# 3801

and when they are admonished, they pay no heed;

# 3802

and if they see any Sign, they laugh it away

# 3803

and say: This is nothing but plain sorcery.

# 3804

Is it ever possible that after we die and are reduced to dust and (a skeleton of) bones, we will be raised to life?

# 3805

And so also shall our forefathers of yore be raised to life?

# 3806

Tell them: Yes; and you are utterly helpless (against Allah).

# 3807

There will be a single stern rebuff and lo, they will be observing with their own eyes (all that they had been warned against).

# 3808

They will then say: Woe for us. This is the Day of Judgement.

# 3809

Yes, this is the Day of Final Decision that you used to deny as a lie.

# 3810

(Then will the command be given): Muster all the wrong-doers and their spouses and the deities whom they used to serve

# 3811

apart from Allah, and direct them to the path of Hell,

# 3812

and detain them there; they will be called to account.

# 3813

How is it that you are not helping one another?

# 3814

Indeed, today they are surrendering themselves completely.

# 3815

They will then turn towards each other (and start wrangling).

# 3816

(The followers will say to their leaders): You used to come to us from the right hand.

# 3817

They will say: Nay, you yourselves were not the ones who would believe.

# 3818

We had no power over you. You were a rebellious people,

# 3819

and so we became deserving of the Word of our Lord that we shall be made to suffer chastisement.

# 3820

So we led you astray; we ourselves were strayed.

# 3821

On that Day, they will all share the chastisement.

# 3822

Thus do We treat the culprits.

# 3823

Whenever it was said to them: There is no true deity apart from Allah, they waxed proud

# 3824

and said: Shall we forsake our deities for the sake of a distracted poet?

# 3825

(They say so although) he brought the Truth and confirmed the veracity of the Messengers.

# 3826

(They will be told): You shall taste the grievous chastisement.

# 3827

You will only be recompensed according to your deeds.

# 3828

But Allah's chosen servants (shall be spared this woeful end).

# 3829

For them awaits a known provision,

# 3830

a variety of delicious fruits; and they shall be honoured

# 3831

in the Gardens of Bliss.

# 3832

They will be seated upon couches set face to face;

# 3833

a cup filled with wine from its springs, will be passed around to them;

# 3834

white, sparkling (wine), a delight to the drinkers.

# 3835

There will neither be any harm in it for their body nor will it intoxicate their mind.

# 3836

Theirs shall be wide-eyed maidens with bashful, restrained glances,

# 3837

so delicate as the hidden peel under an egg's shell.

# 3838

Then some of them will turn to others, and will ask each other.

# 3839

One of them will say: I had a companion in the world

# 3840

who used to say: -- Are you also one of those who confirm the Truth (of life after death)?

# 3841

After we are dead and have become all dust and bones shall we still be requited?'

# 3842

He will say: -- Do you wish to know where he is now?'

# 3843

Then he will look downwards, and will see him in the depths of Hell.

# 3844

He will say to him: -- By Allah, you almost ruined me.

# 3845

But for Allah's favour, I should be one of those who have been mustered here.

# 3846

So, are we not going to die,

# 3847

except for our first death? And shall we suffer no chastisement?'

# 3848

Surely this is the supreme triumph.

# 3849

For the like of it should the workers work.

# 3850

Is this a better hospitality or the tree of al-Zaqqum?

# 3851

We have made this tree a trial for the wrong-doers.

# 3852

It is a tree that grows in the nethermost part of Hell.

# 3853

Its spathes are like the heads of satans.

# 3854

(The people of Hell) will surely eat of it, filling their bellies with it.

# 3855

Then on top of it they will have a brew of boiling water.

# 3856

Then their return will be to the same blazing Hell.

# 3857

These are the ones who found their fathers steeped in error,

# 3858

and they are running in their footsteps.

# 3859

Before them a multitude of people of olden times had erred,

# 3860

and We had sent among them Messengers to warn them.

# 3861

Observe, then, what was the end of those that had been warned,

# 3862

except for the chosen servants of Allah?

# 3863

Noah had called upon Us (earlier). See, how excellent We were in answering him!

# 3864

We delivered him and his household from the great calamity;

# 3865

and made his offspring the only ones to survive,

# 3866

and We established for him a good name among posterity.

# 3867

Peace be upon Noah among all the nations.

# 3868

Thus do We reward all those who do good.

# 3869

Surely he was one of Our truly believing servants.

# 3870

Thereafter We caused the others to be drowned.

# 3871

Abraham was on the self-same way (as Noah).

# 3872

When he came to his Lord with a pure heart,

# 3873

and said to his father and his people: Whom do you worship?

# 3874

Is it false deities that you want to serve rather than Allah?

# 3875

What do you think of the Lord of the whole Universe?

# 3876

Then he looked carefully at the stars

# 3877

and said: I am sick.

# 3878

So turning their backs, they went away from him.

# 3879

Then he went quietly to the (temple of the deities) and said: What is the matter with you, why do you not eat?

# 3880

What is the matter with you, why do you not speak?

# 3881

Then he turned upon them, striking them with his right hand,

# 3882

whereupon people came to him running.

# 3883

Abraham said to them: Do you worship what you yourselves have carved with your own hands

# 3884

while it is Allah Who has created you and all that you make?

# 3885

They spoke among themselves: Build him a pyre and then throw him into the furnace.

# 3886

They had contrived an evil plan against him, but We abased them all.

# 3887

Abraham said: I am going to my Lord; He will guide me.

# 3888

Lord, grant me a righteous son.

# 3889

(In response to this prayer) We gave him the good news of a prudent boy;

# 3890

and when he was old enough to go about and work with him, (one day) Abraham said to him: My son, I see in my dream that I am slaughtering you. So consider (and tell me) what you think. He said: Do as you are bidden. You will find me, if Allah so wills, among the steadfast.

# 3891

When both surrendered (to Allah's command) and Abraham flung the son down on his forehead,

# 3892

We cried out: O Abraham,

# 3893

you have indeed fulfilled your dream. Thus do We reward the good-doers.

# 3894

This was indeed a plain trial.

# 3895

And We ransomed him with a mighty sacrifice,

# 3896

and We preserved for him a good name among posterity.

# 3897

Peace be upon Abraham.

# 3898

Thus do We reward the good-doers.

# 3899

Surely he was one of Our believing servants.

# 3900

And We gave him the good news of Isaac, a Prophet and among the righteous ones.

# 3901

And We blessed him and Isaac. Among the offspring of the two some did good and some plainly wronged themselves.

# 3902

Verily We bestowed Our favours on Moses and Aaron

# 3903

and We delivered both of them and their people from the great calamity.

# 3904

We succoured them, and they gained the upper hand (against their enemies).

# 3905

We granted them a Clear Book,

# 3906

and showed them the Straight Way,

# 3907

and preserved for them a good name among posterity.

# 3908

Peace be upon Moses and Aaron.

# 3909

Thus do We reward the good-doers.

# 3910

Surely both of them were among Our believing servants.

# 3911

Surely, Elias too was among the Messengers.

# 3912

(Call to mind) when he said to his people: Will you not fear Allah?

# 3913

Do you call upon Baal and forsake the Best of the Creators?

# 3914

Allah is your Lord and the Lord of your ancestors of yore.

# 3915

But they denounced him as a liar, so they will surely be arraigned (for punishment),

# 3916

except Allah's chosen servants.

# 3917

We preserved a good name for him among posterity.

# 3918

Peace be upon Elias.

# 3919

Thus do We reward the good-doers.

# 3920

He was one of Our believing servants.

# 3921

And Lot too was one of the Messengers.

# 3922

(Call to mind) when We delivered him and all his kinsfolk,

# 3923

except for an old woman who was among those that stayed behind.

# 3924

Then We utterly destroyed the rest of them.

# 3925

You pass by their desolate habitations in the morning

# 3926

and at night. Do you still not understand?

# 3927

And Jonah too was one of the Messengers.

# 3928

Call to mind when he fled to the laden ship,

# 3929

cast lots, and was among the losers.

# 3930

Then a fish swallowed him, and he was blameworthy.

# 3931

Had he not been one of those who glorify Allah,

# 3932

he would certainly have remained in its belly till the Day of Resurrection.

# 3933

But We threw him on a wide bare tract of land while he was ill;

# 3934

and caused a gourd tree to grow over him,

# 3935

and We sent him forth to a nation of a hundred thousand or more,

# 3936

and they believed. So We let them enjoy life for a while.

# 3937

So ask their opinion: (Are you convinced) that your Lord should have daughters and you should have sons?

# 3938

Did We create the angels as females the while they witnessed?

# 3939

Behold, it is one of their fabrications that they say:

# 3940

Allah has begotten. They are liars!

# 3941

Did He choose daughters rather than sons?

# 3942

What is the matter with you that you make such strange judgements?

# 3943

Will you then not take heed?

# 3944

Do you have any clear authority for such claims?

# 3945

Bring your Book, if you are truthful.

# 3946

They have established a kinship between Allah and the angels; and the angels know well that these people will be arraigned (as culprits).

# 3947

(They say): Exalted be Allah above what they attribute to Him,

# 3948

all of them except the chosen servants of Allah.

# 3949

So you and your deities

# 3950

shall not be able to tempt anyone away from Allah

# 3951

except him who shall roast in the Blazing Fire.

# 3952

As for us, there is none but has an appointed station.

# 3953

Verily we range ourselves in rows (as humble servants)

# 3954

and we are of those who glorify Allah.

# 3955

They used to say before:

# 3956

If only we had the Reminder which had been granted to the people of yore

# 3957

we would surely have been Allah's chosen servants.

# 3958

But when it came to them, they rejected it. They shall soon come to know (the end of such an attitude).

# 3959

We have already given Our promise to Our Messengers

# 3960

that they shall certainly be succoured,

# 3961

and that Our hosts shall triumph.

# 3962

So, (O Prophet), leave them alone for a while,

# 3963

and see, and soon they too shall see.

# 3964

Do they seek to hasten Our chastisement?

# 3965

When that chastisement will descend upon their courtyard, evil shall that Day be for those who had been warned.

# 3966

Leave them alone for a while,

# 3967

and see; and they too shall soon see.

# 3968

Exalted be your Lord, the Lord of Glory, above what they attribute to Him,

# 3969

and peace be upon the Messengers,

# 3970

and all praise be to Allah, the Lord of the Universe.

# 3971

Sad, and by the Qur'an full of exhortation!

# 3972

Nay, but the unbelievers are steeped in arrogance and stubborn defiance.

# 3973

How many a nation did We destroy before them! (When they approached their doom) they cried out (for deliverance), but the time for deliverance was already past.

# 3974

They wondered that a warner had come to them from among themselves, and the deniers of the Truth said: This is a sorcerer, and a big liar.

# 3975

Has he made the gods one single God? This is truly astounding.

# 3976

And the elders among them went forth saying: Go ahead and be steadfast in adhering to your deities. What is being said is with a design.

# 3977

We have not heard this in the religious community close to our time. This is nothing but a fabrication.

# 3978

Has this Exhortation been sent down among us only to him, to the exclusion of all others? Nay, they are in doubt regarding My Exhortation, and are saying all this because they have not yet had any taste of My chastisement.

# 3979

Do they possess the treasures of your Lord, the Most Mighty, the Great Bestower?

# 3980

Or do they possess the dominion of the heavens and the earth and of all that is in between them? If so, let them ascend the heights of the realm of causation and see!

# 3981

This is only a small army out of the several armies that will suffer defeat here.

# 3982

Before them the people of Noah, Ad, and Pharaoh of the tent-pegs gave the lie (to the Messengers)

# 3983

and so did Thamud and the people of Lot and the people of Aykah. These were all leagued together.

# 3984

Each of them gave the lie to Messengers and My decree of chastisement came upon them.

# 3985

They are waiting for nothing except a single Cry, after which there will be no second Cry.

# 3986

They say: Our Lord, hasten to us our share (of chastisement) before the Day of Reckoning.

# 3987

(O Prophet), bear with patience what they say, and call to mind Our servant David, who was endowed with great strength and who constantly turned (to Allah).

# 3988

With him We had subjected the mountains that they join him in celebrating Allah's glory, evening and morning,

# 3989

and the birds, too, in their flocks, and turn again and again to celebrating Allah's glory.

# 3990

And We strengthened his kingdom and endowed him with wisdom and decisive judgement.

# 3991

Has the story of the litigants reached you -- of those who entered his private chambers by climbing over the wall?

# 3992

As they came upon David -- and he was frightened of them -- they said: Be not afraid. We are just two litigants: one of us has committed excess against the other. So judge rightly between us, and be not unjust; and guide us to the Right Way.

# 3993

Behold, this is my brother; he has ninety-nine ewes and I have only one ewe. And yet he said: Give her into my charge, and he got the better of me in argument.

# 3994

David said: He has certainly wronged you in seeking to add your ewe to his ewes; and indeed many who live together commit excesses, one to the other, except those that believe and act righteously; and they are but few. (While so saying) David realized that it is We Who have put him to test; therefore, he sought the forgiveness of his Lord, and fell down, bowing and penitently turning (to Him).

# 3995

Thereupon We forgave him his shortcoming and indeed (an exalted position of) nearness awaits him, and an excellent resort.

# 3996

(We said to him): O David, We have appointed you vicegerent on earth. Therefore, rule among people with justice and do not follow (your) desire lest it should lead you astray from Allah's Path. Allah's severe chastisement awaits those who stray away from Allah's Path, for they had forgotten the Day of Reckoning.

# 3997
