But he who says to his parents: Fie on you! Do you threaten me that I shall be resurrected, although myriad generations have passed away before me (and not one of them was resurrected)? The parents beseech Allah (and say to their child): Woe to you, have faith. Surely Allah's promise is true. But he says: All this is nothing but fables of olden times.

# 4528

It is against such that Allah's sentence (of punishment) has become due. They will join the communities of humans and jinn that have preceded them. Verily all of them will court utter loss.

# 4529

Of these all have ranks according to their deeds so that Allah may fully recompense them for their deeds. They shall not be wronged.

# 4530

And on the Day when the unbelievers will be exposed to the Fire, they will be told: You have exhausted your share of the bounties in the life of the world, and you took your fill of enjoyments. So, degrading chastisement shall be yours on this Day for you waxed arrogant in the earth without justification and acted iniquitously.

# 4531

Recount to them the story of (Hud), the brother of (the tribe of) 'Ad. Hud warned his people beside the sand-dunes -- and there have been other warners before him and since his time -- saying: Serve none but Allah. Verily I fear that the chastisement of an awesome day shall come upon you.

# 4532

They said: Have you come to us to turn us away from our gods? Then, bring upon us the scourge that you threaten us with. Do so if you are truthful.

# 4533

He replied: Allah alone knows about this. I only convey to you the Message that I have been sent with. But I see that you are an ignorant people.

# 4534

When they saw the scourge advancing towards their valleys, they said: This is a cloud that will bring much rain to us. By no means; it is what you had sought to hasten -- a wind-storm bearing a grievous chastisement

# 4535

that will destroy everything by the command of its Lord. Thereafter nothing was left to be seen except their dwellings. Thus do We requite the wrong-doers.

# 4536

We had established them firmly in a manner We have not established you. We had given them ears and eyes and hearts. But nothing availed them -- neither their ears, nor their eyes, nor their hearts, for they denied the Signs of Allah. Then what they had mocked at encompassed them.

# 4537

Surely We destroyed many a town around you. We sent Our Messages to them repeatedly and in diverse forms that they may eschew (their evil ways) and return (to Allah).

# 4538

So why did those whom they had set up as gods apart from Allah, hoping that they would bring them nearer to Him, not come to their aid? Instead, they failed them. This was the end of the lie they had fabricated and the false beliefs they had invented.

# 4539

And call to mind when We sent to you a party of the jinn that they may listen to the Qur'an. When they reached the place (where you were reciting the Qur'an), they said to one another: Be silent (and listen). And when the recitation ended, they went back to their people as warners.

# 4540

They said: Our people, We have heard a Scripture revealed after Moses, verifying the Scriptures revealed before it; it guides to the Truth and to the Straight Way.

# 4541

Our people, respond to the call of him who calls you to Allah and believe in him. Allah will forgive your sins and will protect you from a grievous chastisement.

# 4542

And he who does not respond to the one who calls to Allah will not be able to frustrate Him on earth, nor will they have anyone to protect them from Allah. Such people are in manifest error.

# 4543

Do they not see that Allah, Who created the heavens and the earth -- and creating them did not wear Him out -- has the power to bring the dead back to life? Why not! He certainly has the power over everything.

# 4544

On the Day when the unbelievers will be brought within sight of the Fire, they will be asked: Is this not the Truth? and they will answer Yes, by Our Lord (this is the Truth). Allah will say: Then suffer the chastisement as a requital for your disbelieving.

# 4545

So bear with patience, (O Prophet), even as the Messengers endowed with firmness of resolve (before you) bore with patience, and do not be hasty in their regard. The Day when they see what they had been warned against they will feel as though they had remained in the world no more than an hour of a day. (The Truth has been conveyed.) Will any, then, suffer perdition except those who disobey?

# 4546

Allah has caused the works of those who disbelieve and hinder people from the way of Allah to go to waste.

# 4547

As for those who attained to faith and did righteous works and believed in what was revealed to Muhammad -- which indeed is the Truth from their Lord -- Allah has remitted their evil deeds and has set their condition right.

# 4548

That is because those who disbelieved followed falsehood whereas those who believed followed the Truth that came to them from their Lord. Thus does Allah set forth to people parables showing their true state.

# 4549

When you meet the unbelievers (in battle), smite their necks until you have crushed them, then bind your captives firmly; thereafter (you are entitled to) set them free, either by an act of grace, or against ransom, until the war ends. That is for you to do. If Allah had so willed, He would have Himself exacted retribution from them. (But He did not do so) that He may test some of you by means of others. As for those who are slain in the way of Allah, He shall never let their works go to waste.

# 4550

He will guide them and set their condition right

# 4551

and will admit them to Paradise with which He has acquainted them.

# 4552

Believers, if you aid Allah, He will come to your aid and will plant your feet firmly.

# 4553

As to those who disbelieve, perdition lies in store for them and Allah has reduced their works to nought.

# 4554

That was because they were averse to what Allah had revealed; so He let their works go to waste.

# 4555

Have they not journeyed through the land to see the end of those who went before them? Allah utterly destroyed them. These unbelievers are doomed to the same end.

# 4556

That is because Allah is the Protector of the believers whereas the unbelievers have none to protect them.

# 4557

Allah shall admit those who believe and do righteous works to the Gardens beneath which rivers flow. As for the unbelievers, they enjoy the pleasures of this transient life and eat as cattle eat. The Fire shall be their resort.

# 4558

(O Prophet), how many are the cities that had greater power than your city that drove you out? We destroyed them and there was none to protect them.

# 4559

Then, can he, who is on a Clear Guidance from His Lord, be like him whose evil deeds have been embellished to him, and who pursued their lusts?

# 4560

Here is the parable of Paradise which the God-fearing have been promised: in it shall be rivers of incorruptible water, rivers of milk unchanging in taste, and rivers of wine, a delight to those that drink; and rivers of pure honey. In it they will have every kind of fruit as well as forgiveness from their Lord. Can such be like those who will abide in the Fire and will be given a boiling water to drink that will tear their bowels apart?

# 4561

Among them some give ear to you. But no sooner do they leave your presence than they ask those endowed with knowledge: What is it that he said just now? Such are those whose hearts Allah has sealed and who pursue their lusts.

# 4562

As for those who were led to the Guidance, Allah increases them in their guidance and causes them to grow in God-fearing.

# 4563

Are they waiting, then, for anything else than the Last Hour to suddenly come upon them? Already some of its tokens have come. But when it does actually come upon them, where will any time be left for them to take heed?

# 4564

Know, therefore, (O Prophet), that there is no god but Allah, and ask forgiveness for your shortcomings and also for (the shortcomings of) believing men and believing women. Allah knows the places where you move about and where you dwell.

# 4565

The believers used to say: Why is a surah (that would ordain fighting) not revealed? But when a definitive surah was revealed wherein fighting was mentioned, you saw that those in whose hearts there was a sickness looked at you as though they were about to faint at the approach of death. Pity on them!

# 4566

(They keep affirming their) obedience and saying good words. But when a course of action was clearly determined, it would have been better for them if they had proved true to Allah.

# 4567

Now, if you were to turn away, what else can be expected but that you will work corruption in the land and fly at each other's throats?

# 4568

It is these upon whom Allah has laid His curse: so He made them deaf and deprived them of their sight.

# 4569

Do they, then, not reflect on the Qur'an? Or are there locks on their hearts?

# 4570

Certainly those who have turned their backs on the True Guidance after it became manifest to them, Satan has embellished their ways for them and has buoyed them up with false hopes.

# 4571

This, because they said to those who are averse to the faith that Allah has revealed: In some matters we shall obey you. Allah has full knowledge of their secret parleys.

# 4572

But how will they fare when angels will take their souls at death and will carry them, striking their faces and backs?

# 4573

That is because they have followed a way that angered Allah, and have been averse to His good pleasure. So He reduced all their works to nought.

# 4574

Or do they, in whose hearts there is a sickness, believe that Allah will not bring their failings to light?

# 4575

If We were to so will, We could have shown them to you so that you would recognise them by their faces, and you would certainly know them by the manner of their speech. Allah knows all your deeds.

# 4576

We shall certainly test you until We know those of you who truly strive and remain steadfast, and will ascertain about you.

# 4577

Those who disbelieved and barred others from Allah's Way and opposed the Messenger after the True Guidance had become manifest to them, they shall not be able to cause Allah the least harm; rather, Allah will reduce all their works to nought.

# 4578

Believers, obey Allah and obey the Messenger and do not cause your works to be nullified.

# 4579

Verily Allah shall not forgive those who disbelieved and barred others from Allah's Way and clung to their unbelief until their death.

# 4580

So, be not faint-hearted and do not cry for peace. You shall prevail. Allah is with you and will not bring your works to nought.

# 4581

The life of this world is but sport and amusement. If you believe and are God-fearing, He will grant you your reward, and will not ask you for your possessions.

# 4582

If He were to ask you for your possessions and press you (in that regard), you would have grown niggardly, and Allah would have brought your failings to light.

# 4583

Behold, you are those who are called upon to spend in Allah's Way, but some of you are niggardly. Whoever is niggardly is in fact niggardly to himself. For Allah is All-Sufficient, whereas it is you who are in need of Him. If you turn away, He will replace you by a people other than you, and they will not be like you.

# 4584

(O Prophet), surely We have granted you a clear victory

# 4585

so that Allah may forgive you your shortcomings, whether earlier or later, and may complete His favours upon you and guide you to the Straight Way,

# 4586

and that Allah may bestow upon you a mighty help.

# 4587

He it is Who bestowed inner peace on the hearts of the believers so that they may grow yet more firm in their faith. To Allah belong the legions of the heavens and the earth; Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.

# 4588

(He did this) to admit the believers, both men and women, to Gardens beneath which rivers flow, wherein they shall abide, and to efface their evil deeds from them. That, in Allah's sight, is the supreme triumph.

# 4589

(He also did this) to chastise the hypocrites, both men and women, and those who associate others in His Divinity, both men and women, and who harbour evil thoughts about Allah. They shall be afflicted with misfortune, Allah is wroth with them. He has laid His curse upon them and has prepared for them Hell. What an evil end!

# 4590

To Allah belong the legions of the heavens and the earth. Allah is Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 4591

(O Prophet), We have sent you forth as a witness, as a bearer of good news, and as a warner

# 4592

so that (all of) you may all believe in Allah and His Messenger, and support him, and revere him, and celebrate Allah's glory, morning and evening.

# 4593

Those who swore fealty to you, (O Prophet), in fact swore fealty to Allah. The Hand of Allah is above their hands. So whoever breaks his covenant breaks it to his own hurt; and whoever fulfils the covenant that he made with Allah, He will bestow on him a great reward.

# 4594

(O Prophet), the bedouins who were left behind say to you: We were occupied with our goods and families. So ask forgiveness for us. They say with their tongues what is not in their hearts. Say to them: Who can be of any avail to you against Allah if He should intend to cause you any harm or confer upon you any benefit? Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 4595

(But the truth is not what you say.) You had imagined that the Messenger and the believers would never return to their families, and this notion was embellished in your hearts. You harboured an evil thought, and you are an immensely evil people.

# 4596

As for those who do not believe in Allah and His Messenger, for such unbelievers We have prepared a Blazing Fire.

# 4597

To Allah belongs the kingdom of the heavens and the earth. He forgives whom He pleases and chastises whom He pleases. He is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 4598

When you press forth for the spoils, those who were left behind will say: Let us accompany you. They want to change the command of Allah. Say to them (in clear words): You shall not accompany us. Thus has Allah already said. Then they will say: Nay; but you are jealous of us. The truth is that they understand little.

# 4599

Say to the bedouins who were left behind: You will be called against those who possess great might and be asked to fight against them unless they surrender. If you obey (the command to fight), Allah will bestow upon you a goodly reward. But if you turn away, as you turned away before, He shall inflict upon you a grievous chastisement.

# 4600

There is no blame on the blind, nor on the lame, nor on the sick (if they do not go forth to fight). Allah will admit those who obey Allah and His Messenger to the Gardens beneath which rivers flow and will inflict a grievous chastisement on those who turn away.

# 4601

Allah was much pleased with the believers when they swore fealty to you under the tree. He knew what was in their hearts. So He bestowed inner peace upon them and rewarded them with a victory near at hand

# 4602

and with abundant spoils which they shall acquire. Allah is Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 4603

Allah has promised you abundant spoils which you shall acquire. He has instantly granted you this (victory) and has restrained the hands of people from you that it may be a Sign for the believers and He may guide you to a Straight Way.

# 4604

He also promises you other spoils which you have not yet taken, but Allah has encompassed them. Allah has power over everything.

# 4605

Had the unbelievers fought against you at that time, they would have turned their backs (in flight), and would have found none to protect or help them.

# 4606

Such is Allah's Way that has come down from the past. Never shall you find any change in the Way of Allah.

# 4607

He it is Who restrained their hands from you, and your hands from them in the valley of Makkah, even though He had made you victorious against them. Allah was watching all that you did.

# 4608

They are the ones who disbelieved and barred you from the Inviolable Mosque and prevented the animals you had designated for sacrifice from reaching the place of their offering. If it had not been for the believing men and believing women (who lived in Makkah and) whom you did not know, and had there not been the fear that you might trample on them and unwittingly incur blame on their account, (then fighting would not have been put to a stop. It was stopped so that) Allah may admit to His Mercy whomsoever He pleases. Had those believers been separated from the rest, We would certainly have inflicted a grievous chastise-ment on those of them \[i.e. the Makkans) who disbelieved.

# 4609

(This is why) when the unbelievers set in their hearts a fierce bigotry -- the bigotry of ignorance -- Allah bestowed inner peace upon His Messenger and upon the believers and made the word of piety binding on them. They were more deserving and worthier thereof. Allah has knowledge of everything.

# 4610

Allah indeed showed His Messenger the true vision, one fully in accord with reality. If Allah so wills you shall certainly enter the Inviolable Mosque, in full security, you will shave your heads and cut your hair short, and do so without any fear. He knew what you did not know, and He granted you a victory near at hand even before (the fulfilment of the vision).

# 4611

He it is Who sent His Messenger with the True Guidance and the Religion of Truth that He may make it prevail over every religion. Sufficient is Allah as a witness (to this).

# 4612

Muhammad is Allah's Messenger, and those who are with him are firm with the unbelievers but compassionate with one another. You see them occupied in bowing and prostrating and in seeking Allah's bounty and good pleasure. They are distinguished from others by the marks of prostration on their faces. Thus are they described in the Torah. And their parable in the Gospel is that of a tilth that puts forth its shoot, then strengthens it so that it becomes stout and stands firmly on its stem. This is a sight pleasing to the sowers and one by which the unbelievers will be enraged. As for those who believe and do righteous deeds, Allah has promised them forgiveness and a great reward.

# 4613

Believers, do not advance before Allah and His Messenger, and fear Allah. Verily Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing.

# 4614

Believers, do not raise your voices above the voice of the Prophet and when speaking to him do not speak aloud as you speak aloud to one another, lest all your deeds are reduced to nothing without your even realising it.

# 4615

The ones who lower their voices in the presence of the Messenger of Allah are those whose hearts Allah has tested for God-fearing. Theirs shall be forgiveness and a great reward.

# 4616

Surely most of those who call out to you, (O Prophet), from behind the apartments, are devoid of understanding.

# 4617

If they were patient until you went out to them, that would have been better for them. Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Merciful.

# 4618

Believers, when an ungodly person brings to you a piece of news, carefully ascertain its truth, lest you should hurt a people unwittingly and thereafter repent at what you did.

# 4619

Know that Allah's Messenger is among you. Were he to follow you in many an affair, you yourselves would suffer. But Allah has endeared faith to you and has embellished it in your hearts, and has made unbelief and evil-doing and disobedience abhorrent to you. Such are those who are rightly guided,

# 4620

by Allah's favour and bounty. Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise.

# 4621

If two parties of the believers happen to fight, make peace between them. But then, if one of them transgresses against the other, fight the one that transgresses until it reverts to Allah's command. And if it does revert, make peace between them with justice, and be equitable for Allah loves the equitable.

# 4622

Surely the believers are none but brothers unto one another, so set things right between your brothers, and have fear of Allah that you may be shown mercy.

# 4623

Believers, let not a group (of men) scoff at another group, it may well be that the latter (at whom they scoff) are better than they; nor let a group of women scoff at another group, it may well be that the latter are better than they. And do not taunt one another, nor revile one another by nicknames. It is an evil thing to gain notoriety for ungodliness after belief. Those who do not repent are indeed the wrong-doers.

# 4624

Believers, avoid being excessively suspicious, for some suspicion is a sin. Do not spy, nor backbite one another. Would any of you like to eat the flesh of his dead brother? You would surely detest it. Have fear of Allah. Surely Allah is much prone to accept repentance, is Most Compassionate.

# 4625

Human beings, We created you all from a male and a female, and made you into nations and tribes so that you may know one another. Verily the noblest of you in the sight of Allah is the most God-fearing of you. Surely Allah is All-Knowing, All-Aware.

# 4626

The Bedouins say: We believe. (O Prophet), say to them: You do not believe; you should rather say: 'We have submitted'; for belief has not yet entered your hearts. If you obey Allah and His Messenger, He will not diminish anything from the reward of any of your deeds. Surely Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 4627

Indeed the ones possessed of true faith are those who believed in Allah and His Messenger and then they did not entertain any doubt and strove hard in the Way of Allah with their lives and their possessions. These are the truthful ones.

# 4628

Say, (O Prophet), (to these pretenders to faith): Are you apprising Allah of your faith? Allah knows all that is in the heavens and the earth. Allah has full knowledge of everything.

# 4629

They count it as a favour to you that they accepted Islam. Say: Do not regard your (accepting) Islam as a favour to me; rather, Allah has bestowed a favour on you by guiding you to faith, if you are truthful (in your claim to be believers).

# 4630

Surely Allah knows every hidden thing of the heavens and the earth. Allah sees all that you do.

# 4631

Qaf. By the glorious Qur'an.

# 4632

Nay; they wondered that a warner should have come to them from among themselves. The unbelievers said: This indeed is a strange thing.

# 4633

What! When we are dead and reduced to mere dust, (shall we be raised to life)? Such a return is far-fetched.

# 4634

(Thus do they imagine, although) We know well what the earth takes away from them. With Us is a Record that preserves everything.

# 4635

They gave the lie to the Truth when it came to them. So they are now in a state of great perplexity.

# 4636

Did they never observe the sky above them: how We built it and beautified it; and it has no cracks;

# 4637

and We have spread out the earth, and have set upon it firm mountains, and have caused it to bring out plants of all beauteous kinds?

# 4638

All these are to serve as eye openers and as a lesson to every being who is prone to turn (to the Truth).

# 4639

We also sent down blessed water from the heaven, wherewith We caused gardens and harvest-grain to grow,

# 4640

and tall palm-trees with their thickly-clustered spathes;

# 4641

all this as sustenance for Our servants. And thus We do bring the dead land back to life with water. Such shall be the coming forth (of human beings from the earth).

# 4642

In the past Noah's people, and the people of Rass and Thamud gave the lie (to Messengers),

# 4643

and so did 'Ad, and Pharaoh and Lot's brethren,

# 4644

and the people of Aykah, and the people of Tubba'. They all gave the lie to the Messengers. Thereafter My threat of chastisement against them was fulfilled.

# 4645

Did We, then, become worn out by the first creation? Not at all; but they are in doubt about a fresh creation.

# 4646

Surely We have created man, and We know the promptings of his heart, and We are nearer to him than even his jugular vein.

# 4647

Moreover, there are two scribes, one each sitting on the right and the left, recording everything.

# 4648

He utters not a word, but there is a vigilant watcher at hand.

# 4649

Lo, the agony of death has indeed come with the Truth. That is what you had sought to avoid.

# 4650

And then the Trumpet was blown. This is the day of the promised chastisement.

# 4651

Everyone has come, each attended by one who will drive him on, and another who will bear witness.

# 4652

You were heedless of this. Now We have removed your veil and so your vision today is sharp.

# 4653

His companion said: Here is he who was in my charge.

# 4654

The command was given: Cast into Hell every hardened, stubborn unbeliever,

# 4655

who hinders good, exceeds the limits, is immersed in doubts,

# 4656

and has set up another deity with Allah. Hurl him into the grievous torment.

# 4657

His companion said: I did not incite him to rebel; he was far gone into error of his own accord.

# 4658

(It was said): Do not remonstrate in My presence. I had warned you.

# 4659

My Word is not changed; and never do I inflict the least wrong upon My servants.

# 4660

On that Day We shall ask Hell: Are you full? And it will reply: Are there any more?

# 4661

And when Paradise shall be brought close to the God-fearing, and will no longer be far away,

# 4662

it will be said: This is what you were promised, a promise made to everyone who turned much (to Allah) and was watchful of his conduct,

# 4663

to everyone who feared the Merciful One though He is beyond the reach of perception, to everyone who has come with a heart ever wont to turn (to Him).

# 4664

Enter this Paradise in peace. That will be the Day of Eternity.

# 4665

Therein they shall get whatever they desire; and with Us there is even more.

# 4666

How many a nation did We destroy before them that were stronger in prowess than these. They searched about the lands of the world. But could they find a refuge?

# 4667

Verily there is a lesson in this for everyone who has a (sound) heart and who listens with an attentive mind.

# 4668

We created the heavens and the earth and all that is between them in six days, and weariness did not even touch Us.

# 4669

Hence bear with patience whatever they say, and celebrate your Lord's glory before the rising of the sun and before its setting;

# 4670

and in the night, too, celebrate His glory, in the wake of prostration.

# 4671

Hearken on the Day when the caller will call from a place nearby,

# 4672

the Day when they shall hear the Blast in truth. That will be the Day (for the dead) to come forth.

# 4673

Surely it is We Who give life and cause death, and to Us shall all return

# 4674

on the Day when the earth will be rent asunder and people, rising from it, will hasten forth. To assemble them all will be easy for Us.

# 4675

(O Prophet), We are well aware of what they say; and you are not required to force things on them. So exhort with the Qur'an all those who fear My warning.

# 4676

By the winds which scatter dust,

# 4677

which carry clouds laden with water,

# 4678

which then smoothly speed along,

# 4679

and execute the great task of apportioning (rainfall):

# 4680

surely what you are being warned against is true,

# 4681

and the Judgement shall doubtlessly take place.

# 4682

By the heaven with its numerous forms:

# 4683

surely you are at variance (about the Hereafter);

# 4684

though only those who are averse to the Truth will turn away from (believing in it).

# 4685

Doomed are the conjecturers

# 4686

who are steeped in ignorance and heedlessness.

# 4687

They ask: When will the Day of Judgement be?

# 4688

It will be the Day when they shall be scourged by the Fire

# 4689

(and be told): Taste your ordeal! This is what you were seeking to hasten.

# 4690

As for the God-fearing, they shall be in the midst of gardens and fountains,

# 4691

joyously receiving what their Lord will have granted them. Verily they did good works before (the coming of this Day):

# 4692

they used to sleep but little by night,

# 4693

and would ask for forgiveness at dawn,

# 4694

and in their wealth there was a rightful share for him who would ask and for the destitute.

# 4695

There are many Signs on earth for those of sure faith,

# 4696

and also in your own selves. Do you not see?

# 4697

And in heaven is your provision and also what you are being promised.

# 4698

So, by the Lord of the heaven and the earth, this is certainly true, as true as the fact of your speaking.

# 4699

(O Prophet), did the story of Abraham's honoured guests reach you?

# 4700

When they came to him, they said: Peace; he said: Peace also be to you; (you seem to be) a group of strangers.

# 4701

Then he went back to his family and brought a fat roasted calf

# 4702

and laid it before them, saying: Will you not eat?

# 4703

Then he became afraid of them. They said: Fear not, and announced to him the good news of (the birth of) a boy endowed with knowledge.

# 4704

So hearing his wife went forth shouting. She struck her face and exclaimed: A barren old woman am I.

# 4705

They said: So has your Lord said (that you shall have a boy). Surely He is Most Wise, All-Knowing.

# 4706

Abraham said: Envoys (of Allah), what is your errand?

# 4707

They replied: Behold, we have been sent to a wicked people

# 4708

that we may unleash a shower of clay-stones

# 4709

marked by your Lord upon those who go beyond the limits.

# 4710

Then We evacuated there from all the believers

# 4711

 and We did not find there any, apart from a single house of Muslims 

# 4712

and We left therein a Sign for those who fear the grievous chastisement.

# 4713

There is also a Sign for you in the story of Moses when We sent him with a clear authority to Pharaoh.

# 4714

But Pharaoh turned away, showing arrogance on account of his power, and said (about Moses): He is either a sorcerer or a madman.

# 4715

So We seized him and his hosts, and cast them into the sea. He became an object of much blame.

# 4716

There is also a Sign for you in (the story of) Ad, when We let loose upon them an ominous wind

# 4717

that left nothing that it came upon without reducing it to rubble.

# 4718

There is also a Sign for you in (the story of) Thamud. They were told: Enjoy yourselves for a while.

# 4719

But they brazenly disobeyed their Lord's command, and then a sudden chastisement overtook them while they looked on.

# 4720

They were unable even to stand up or protect themselves.

# 4721

Before all these We destroyed the people of Noah: they were a wicked people.

# 4722

And heaven  We made it with Our Own Power and We have the Power to do so.

# 4723

And the earth  We spread it out, and how well have We smoothed it!

# 4724

And of everything We have created pairs; perhaps you will take heed.

# 4725

Flee, therefore, to Allah. Surely I am a clear warner to you from Him;

# 4726

and do not set up any deity with Allah. Surely I am a clear warner to you from Him.

# 4727

Thus has it been (in the past): never did a Messenger come to the nations that preceded them but they said: (He is) a sorcerer, or a mad-man.

# 4728

Have they arrived at a common understanding concerning this? No; but they are a people given to transgression.

# 4729

So turn your attention away from them; you shall incur no blame.

# 4730

Do, however, keep exhorting them; for exhortation benefits those endowed with faith.

# 4731

I created the jinn and humans for nothing else but that they may serve Me;

# 4732

I desire from them no provision, nor do I want them to feed Me.

# 4733

Surely Allah is the Bestower of all provision, the Lord of all power, the Strong.

# 4734

The wrong-doers shall receive a portion of the chastisements as their fellows (of yore). So let them not rush Me.

# 4735

Woe, then, betide those who disbelieved in that Day of theirs which they are being asked to hold in dread.

# 4736

By the Mount,

# 4737

and the Book inscribed

# 4738

on fine parchment;

# 4739

by the much-frequented House,

# 4740

by the elevated canopy;

# 4741

and by the swelling sea:

# 4742

verily your Lord's chastisement shall come to pass,

# 4743

none can avert that.

# 4744

(It shall come to pass) on the Day when the heaven will convulse in a great convulsion,

# 4745

and the mountains shall violently fly about.

# 4746

Woe, then, on that Day to those who give the lie (to this Message)

# 4747

and amuse themselves with vain argumentation.

# 4748

On the Day when they shall be thrust into Hell with a violent thrust (and shall be told):

# 4749

This is the Hell which you used to give the lie to.

# 4750

Is this, then, any feat of magic or are you unable to see?

# 4751

Go now and burn in it. It is all the same whether you bear it patiently or do not bear it with patience. You are only being recompensed for your deeds.

# 4752

Surely the God-fearing shall be in Gardens and bliss,

# 4753

enjoying what Allah will have endowed them with; and their Lord will have saved them from the torment of the Blazing Fire.

# 4754

(They will be told): Eat and drink to your hearts' content as a reward for your deeds.

# 4755

The God-fearing shall be reclining on couches facing each other, and We shall wed them to maidens with large, beautiful eyes.

# 4756

We shall unite the believers with those descendants of theirs who followed them in their faith, and shall not deny them any part of the reward for their good deeds. Every person is pledged to what he did.

# 4757

We shall provide them in abundance with all kinds of fruit and meat, whatever they may desire.

# 4758

They shall pass on to one another a cup that will incite neither levity nor sin.

# 4759

Youths as fair as hidden pearls will be set apart to wait upon them; they will be running to and fro to serve them.

# 4760

They will turn to one another and ask (regarding the past events).

# 4761

They will say: When we were living before among our kinsfolk we lived in constant fear (of Allah's displeasure).

# 4762

Then Allah graced us with His favour and saved us from the chastisement of the scorching wind.

# 4763

Formerly we had always prayed to Him. Surely He is Most Benign, Most Compassionate.

# 4764

So exhort (them, O Prophet), for by your Lord's Grace, you are neither a soothsayer nor a madman.

# 4765

Or do they say: He is a poet for whom we await an adverse turn of fortune.

# 4766

Tell them: Wait; I too am waiting with you.

# 4767

Do their minds prompt them to say such things, or are they a people immersed in transgression?

# 4768

Do they say: He has himself fabricated the Qur'an? No; the truth is that they are altogether averse to believing.

# 4769

(If they are truthful in this), then let them produce a discourse of similar splendour.

# 4770

Did they come into being without any creator? Or were they their own creators?

# 4771

Or is it they who created the heavens and the earth? No; the truth is that they lack sure faith.

# 4772

Or do they have your Lord's treasures in their keeping? Or have absolute authority over them?

# 4773

Or do they have a ladder whereon they can climb and attempt to listen (to what is transpiring in the Higher Realm)? Then, let any of them who has listened to it produce a clear proof of it.

# 4774

Or does Allah have daughters whereas you have sons?

# 4775

Or is it that you ask of them any recompense so that they should fear to be weighed down under the burden of debt?

# 4776

Or is it that they have access to (the Truths in) the realm beyond sense-perception which they are writing down?

# 4777

Or are they contriving a stratagem against you? If so, that stratagem will rebound against the unbelievers.

# 4778

Do they have any god other than Allah? Exalted be Allah above whatever they associate (with Him in His Divinity).

# 4779

(So obstinate are they that) even if they were to see some fragments of the sky falling down they would still say: It is only a mass of cloud.

# 4780

So leave them alone until they encounter that Day of theirs when they shall be struck down,

# 4781

when their stratagem shall be of no avail to them, nor shall they be succoured.

# 4782

Surely a chastisement awaits the wrong-doers even before the coming of that Day; but most of them do not know.

# 4783

Be patient, then, (O Prophet), until the judgement of your Lord comes. For surely you are before Our eyes. And celebrate the praise of your Lord when you rise,

# 4784

and also celebrate His praise at night, and at the retreat of the stars.

# 4785

By the star when it sets:

# 4786

your companion has neither strayed nor is he deluded;

# 4787

nor does he speak out of his desire.

# 4788

This is nothing but a revelation that is conveyed to him,

# 4789

something that a very powerful one has imparted to him,

# 4790

one endowed with immense wisdom. He came forth and stood poised,

# 4791

being on the higher horizon.

# 4792

Then he drew near and hung above suspended,

# 4793

until he was two bows' length away, or nearer.

# 4794

Then he revealed to Allah's servant whatever he had to reveal.

# 4795

His heart added no untruth to what he saw.

# 4796

Are you, then, going to contend with him regarding what he sees with his eyes?

# 4797

Indeed he saw him a second time,

# 4798

by the lote-tree at the farthest boundary,

# 4799

near which is the Garden of Abode.

# 4800

(This was) when the lote-tree was covered with that which covered it.

# 4801

His eye did not waver, nor did it stray,

# 4802

and he certainly saw some of the greatest Signs of His Lord.

# 4803

Have you ever thought about al-Lat and al-Uzza,

# 4804

and about the third deity, al-Manat?

# 4805

Shall you have the male issues, and He the female issues?

# 4806

That is indeed an unfair division!

# 4807

These are nothing but names that you and your forefathers have invented, for which Allah has sent down no authority. They are merely following their conjectures and their carnal desires although guidance has come to them from their Lord.

# 4808

Does man imagine that whatever he wishes for is right for him?

# 4809

To Allah belong both the Next World and the present.

# 4810

Numerous are the angels in the heavens; yet their intercession shall be of no avail, except in regard to those whom He grants the leave of intercession and whose plea He is pleased to accept.

# 4811

Those who do not believe in the Hereafter give angels the names of females,

# 4812

although they have no knowledge regarding that. They only follow their conjecture and conjecture can never take the place of the Truth.

# 4813

So leave alone those who turn away from the remembrance of Us and who seek nothing but the life of the world 

# 4814

that being the utmost of their knowledge. Surely your Lord fully knows those who have strayed away from His Path and He also fully knows those who are rightly guided.

# 4815

To Allah alone belongs whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth. He will requite the evil-doers for their deeds and bestow a goodly reward on those who have done good,

# 4816

on those who avoid grave sins and shameful deeds, even if they may sometimes stumble into lesser offences. Surely your Lord is abounding in His Forgiveness. Very well is He aware of you since He produced you from the earth, and while you were still in your mothers' wombs and not yet born. So do not boastfully claim yourselves to be purified. He fully knows those that are truly Godfearing.

# 4817

(O Prophet), did you see him who turned away (from the Path of Allah),

# 4818

who gave a little, and then stopped?

# 4819

Does he have any knowledge of the world beyond the ken of sense-perception, and therefore, clearly sees (the Truth)?

# 4820

Has he not been informed of what is in the Scrolls of Moses,

# 4821

and of Abraham, who lived up to the trust?

# 4822

That no bearer of a burden shall bear the burden of another,

# 4823

and that man shall have nothing but what he has striven for,

# 4824

and that (the result of) his striving shall soon be seen,

# 4825

and that he shall then be fully recompensed,

# 4826

and that the final end is with your Lord,

# 4827

and that He it is Who causes people to laugh and to cry,

# 4828

and that He it is Who causes death and grants life,

# 4829

and He it is Who created the two kinds, the male and the female,

# 4830

from a drop of sperm when it was emitted,

# 4831

and that it is for Him to grant the second life,

# 4832

that He it is Who bestowed wealth and riches,

# 4833

that He is the Lord of Sirius,

# 4834

that He it is Who destroyed the ancient 'Ad,

# 4835

and Thamud, leaving no trace of them,

# 4836

and that He it is Who destroyed the people of Noah before for they were much given to iniquity and transgression.

# 4837

And He brought perdition upon the subverted cities

# 4838

and caused them to be covered with that which He covered them with.

# 4839

So, which of your Lord's bounties will you doubt?

# 4840

This is a warning among the warnings of yore.

# 4841

The imminent Hour has drawn near,

# 4842

and none but Allah can avert it.

# 4843

Will you, then, wonder at this?

# 4844

Will you laugh at it rather than weep?

# 4845

Will you occupy yourselves simply in merriment?

# 4846

Prostrate yourselves before Allah, and serve Him.

# 4847

The Hour of Resurrection drew near and the moon split asunder.

# 4848

(Regardless of any Signs these people see), they turn away and say: This is an ongoing sorcery.

# 4849

They also gave the lie to (the splitting asunder of the moon) and only followed their desires. Yet everything is destined to reach an end.

# 4850

Surely there came to them narratives (of the ancient nations) that should suffice to deter (them from transgression),

# 4851

narratives that are full of consummate wisdom. But warnings do not avail them.

# 4852

So turn away from them, (O Prophet). On the Day when a caller shall call them to a thing most terrible,

# 4853

with down-cast eyes they shall go forth from their graves, as though they were scattered locusts.

# 4854

They shall be hurrying forth towards the caller, and the unbelievers (who had once denied this Day), will say: This is a woeful Day.

# 4855

Before them Noah's people also gave the lie (to his Message). They rejected Our servant as a liar, saying: He is a madman; and he was rebuffed.

# 4856

Then he called upon His Lord: Verily I am vanquished; so come You to my aid.

# 4857

Thereupon We opened the gates of the sky for water to pour down,

# 4858

and We made the earth burst forth with springs, and all this water converged to fulfil that which had been decreed.

# 4859

And We bore Noah on the vessel built of planks and nails,

# 4860

which sailed on under Our supervision: a reward for him who had been shown ingratitude.

# 4861

And We left the Ark as a Sign. Is there, then, any who will take heed?

# 4862

So how awesome were My chastisement and My warnings!

# 4863

We have made this Qur'an easy as a reminder. Is there, then, any who will take heed?

# 4864

'Ad also gave the lie (to Hud). So how awesome were My chastisement and My warnings!

# 4865

We sent a tumultuous wind against them on a day of unremitting misfortune,

# 4866

which tore people away and hurled them as though they were trunks of uprooted palm-trees.

# 4867

So how awesome were My chastisement and My warnings!

# 4868

We have made the Qur'an easy to derive lessons from. Is there, then, any who will take heed?

# 4869

Thamud gave the lie to the warnings,

# 4870

saying: Are we to follow a single mortal, one from among ourselves? If we do that, we shall surely be in error and folly.

# 4871

Was there none but he to whom the Reminder could be vouchsafed excluding all others? Nay; he is an insolent liar.

# 4872

(We told Our Messenger): Tomorrow they shall know who is the insolent liar.

# 4873

We shall send the she-camel as a trial for them; so watch their end with patience.

# 4874

Let them know that the water should be divided between them and the she-camel, each availing their turn.

# 4875

Eventually, they summoned their companion, and he undertook the (outrageous) task and hamstrung the she-camel.

# 4876

So how awesome were My chastisement and My warnings!

# 4877

Behold, We sent a single Blast against them, and they became like the trampled twigs of a sheep pen-builder.

# 4878

Surely We have made this Qur'an easy as a reminder. Is there, then, any who will take heed?

# 4879

Lot's people also gave the lie to the warnings,

# 4880

and behold, We let loose upon them a tempest which rained stones upon them, except upon Lot's household whom We rescued in the last hours of the night

# 4881

as a favour from Us. Thus do We reward those who give thanks.

# 4882

Surely Lot warned his people that We shall seize them (with Our chastisement), but they doubted the warnings.

# 4883

Then they even solicited his guests from him, whereupon We blotted out their eyes, (telling them): Now have a taste of My chastisement and My warnings.

# 4884

Indeed an abiding chastisement came upon them in the morning.

# 4885

So have a taste of My chastisement and My warnings.

# 4886

Surely We have made this Qur'an easy as a reminder. Is there, then, any who will take heed?

# 4887

Warnings also came to the Pharaonites,

# 4888

but they gave the lie to Our Signs, to all of them. Thereupon We seized them with the seizing of the Most Mighty, the Most Powerful.

# 4889

Are your unbelievers (of Makkah) any better than they? Or have you been granted any immunity in the Scriptures?

# 4890

Or do they say: We are a strong legion, strong enough for victory?

# 4891

Soon shall this legion be routed and shall turn their backs and flee.

# 4892

Nay; the Hour of Doom is their appointed time, and the Hour shall be more calamitous and bitter.

# 4893

The evil-doers are victims of error and madness.

# 4894

There shall come a Day when they will be dragged on their faces into the Fire and will be told: Now taste the flame of Hell.

# 4895

We have created everything in a determined measure.

# 4896

Our command consists of only one Word which is carried out in the twinkling of an eye.

# 4897

We did indeed destroy many like you. Is there, then, any who will heed?

# 4898

All their deeds are recorded in the Scrolls;

# 4899

everything large or small, is duly inscribed.

# 4900

Surely those who shun disobedience will dwell amidst Gardens and running streams

# 4901

where they will be honourably seated in the presence of a King, Mighty in Power.

# 4902

The Merciful One

# 4903

has taught the Qur'an,

# 4904

has created man,

# 4905

and has taught him articulate speech.

# 4906

The sun and the moon follow a reckoning,

# 4907

and the stars and the trees all prostrate themselves,

# 4908

and He has raised up the heaven and has set a balance

# 4909

that you may not transgress in the balance,

# 4910

but weigh things equitably and skimp not in the balance.

# 4911

And He has set up the earth for all beings.

# 4912

Therein are fruit and palm-trees with their dates in sheaths,

# 4913

and a variety of corn with both husk and grain.

# 4914

Which of the bounties of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4915

He has created man from dry, rotten clay like the potter's,

# 4916

and has created the jinn from the flame of fire.

# 4917

Which of the wonders of your Lord's power will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4918

Lord of the two easts and of the two wests is He.

# 4919

Which of the powers of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4920

He unleashed the two seas so that they merge together,

# 4921

and yet there is a barrier between them which they may not overstep.

# 4922

Which of the wonders of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4923

From these seas come forth pearls and coral.

# 4924

Which of the wonders of your Lord's power will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4925

His are the ships, towering on the sea like mountains.

# 4926

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4927

All that is on earth will perish,

# 4928

only the Person of your Lord, full of majesty and splendour, will endure.

# 4929

So which of the wonders of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4930

All in the heavens and the earth entreat Him for their needs; a new, mighty task engages Him each day.

# 4931

Which of your Lord's laudable attributes will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4932

O you twain, who are a burden (on the earth), We shall attend to you and call you to account.

# 4933

(We shall then see), which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4934

O company of jinn and men, if you have the power to go beyond the bounds of the heavens and the earth, go beyond them! Yet you will be unable to go beyond them for that requires infinite power.

# 4935

Which of your Lord's powers will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4936

(If you so venture) a flame of fire and smoke shall be lashed at you, which you shall be unable to withstand.

# 4937

Which of your Lord's powers will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4938

(What will happen) when the heaven will be split asunder and will become crimson like leather?

# 4939

Which of your Lord's powers will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4940

On that Day there will be no need to ask either men or jinn about their sins.

# 4941

(We shall see) which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4942

The culprits shall be known by their marks, and shall be seized by their forelocks and their feet.

# 4943

Which of the powers of your Lord, will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4944

(It will be said): This is the Hell that the culprits had cried lies to.

# 4945

They will keep circling around between Hell and boiling water.

# 4946

Which of your Lord's powers will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4947

For any who fears to stand before his Lord are two Gardens.

# 4948

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4949

These Gardens will abound in green, blooming branches.

# 4950

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4951

In each of the two Gardens are two flowing springs.

# 4952

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4953

In both these is a pair of every fruit.

# 4954

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4955

They shall recline on couches lined with brocade, and within reach shall hang the fruits of the two Gardens.

# 4956

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4957

In the midst of these shall be maidens with modest, restrained glances; maidens whom no man or jinn has ever touched before.

# 4958

Which of your Lord's favours will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4959

Lovely as rubies and pearls.

# 4960

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4961

Can the reward of goodness be any other than goodness?

# 4962

Which of the laudable attributes of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4963

And besides these two there shall be two other Gardens.

# 4964

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4965

Two Gardens, dark green and fresh.

# 4966

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4967

In them will be two gushing springs.

# 4968

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4969

Therein will be fruits and dates and pomegranates.

# 4970

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4971

In the midst of these will be maidens, good and comely.

# 4972

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4973

There shall be maidens sheltered in tents.

# 4974

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4975

No man or jinn ever touched them before.

# 4976

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4977

They shall be reclining on green cushions and splendid carpets.

# 4978

Which of the favours of your Lord will you twain  you men and jinn  then deny?

# 4979

Blessed be the name of your Lord, the Lord of Majesty and Glory.

# 4980

When the Event will come to pass

# 4981

 and then there will be no one to deny its occurrence 

# 4982

(a calamitous Event) that shall turn things upside down:

# 4983

when the earth will suddenly shake with a terrible shaking,

# 4984

and the mountains will crumble

# 4985

and will scatter abroad into fine dust.

# 4986

You shall then become three groups.

# 4987

The People on the Right: and how fortunate will be the People on the Right!

# 4988

And the People on the Left: and how miserable will be the People on the Left!

# 4989

As for the Foremost, they will be the foremost!

# 4990

They shall be near-stationed (to their Lord),

# 4991

in the Gardens of Bliss.

# 4992

A throng of the ancients,

# 4993

and a few from later times.

# 4994

They (will be seated) on gold-encrusted couches,

# 4995

reclining on them, arrayed face to face;

# 4996

immortal youths shall go about them

# 4997

with goblets and ewers and a cup filled with a drink drawn from a running spring,

# 4998

a drink by which their minds will not be clouded nor will it cause drunkenness;

# 4999

they will also go about them with the fruits of which they may choose,

# 5000

and with the flesh of any fowl that they may desire to eat;

# 5001

and there shall be wide-eyed maidens,

# 5002

beautiful as pearls hidden in their shells.

# 5003

All this shall be theirs as a reward for their deeds.

# 5004

There they shall hear no idle talk nor any sinful speech.

# 5005

All talk will be sound and upright.

# 5006

As for the People on the Right, how fortunate shall be the people on the Right!

# 5007

They shall be in the midst of thornless lote trees,

# 5008

and flower-clad acacias,

# 5009

and extended shade,

# 5010

and gushing water,

# 5011

and abundant fruit,

# 5012

never-ending and unforbidden.

# 5013

They shall be on upraised couches,

# 5014

and their spouses We shall have brought them into being afresh,

# 5015

and shall have made them virgins,

# 5016

intensely loving and of matching age.

# 5017

All this will be for the People on the Right;

# 5018

a large throng from the ancients,

# 5019

and also a large throng from those of later times.

# 5020

As for the People on the Left: how miserable will be the People on the Left!

# 5021

They will be in the midst of scorching wind and boiling water,

# 5022

and a shade of thick, pitch-black smoke,

# 5023

which will neither be cool nor soothing.

# 5024

Surely they had lived before in luxury,

# 5025

and had persisted in the Great Sin.

# 5026

They used to say: What! Once we are dead and are reduced to dust and bones, shall we still be raised to a new life from the dead?

# 5027

(We) and our fore-fathers of yore?

# 5028

Tell them, (O Prophet): The earlier ones and the later ones

# 5029

shall all be brought together on an appointed Day.

# 5030

Then you, the erring ones and those that gave the lie to the Truth,

# 5031

shall all eat from the Tree of al-Zaqqum,

# 5032

filling your bellies with it;

# 5033

and thereupon you shall drink boiling water,

# 5034

drinking it as thirsty camels do.

# 5035

Thus shall they be entertained on the Day of Recompense.

# 5036

We have created you, then why would you not confirm it?

# 5037

Did you ever consider the sperm that you emit?

# 5038

Do you create a child out of it, or are We its creators?

# 5039

It is We Who ordained death upon you and We are not to be frustrated.

# 5040

Had We so wished, nothing could have hindered Us from replacing you by others like yourselves, or transforming you into beings you know nothing about.

# 5041

You are well aware of the first creation; then, do you learn no lesson from it?

# 5042

Have you considered the seeds you till?

# 5043

Is it you or We Who make them grow?

# 5044

If We so wished, We could have reduced your harvest to rubble, and you would have been left wonder-struck to exclaim:

# 5045

We have been penalised;

# 5046

nay; we have been undone!

# 5047

Did you cast a good look at the water that you drink?

# 5048

Is it you who brought it down from the clouds or is it We Who brought it down?

# 5049

If We had so pleased, We could have made it bitter. So why would you not give thanks?

# 5050

Did you consider the fire which you kindle?

# 5051

Did you make its tree grow or was it We Who made it grow?

# 5052

We made it a reminder and a provision for the needy.

# 5053

Glorify, then, (O Prophet), the name of your Great Lord.

# 5054

No! I swear by the positions of the stars 

# 5055

and this is indeed a mighty oath, if only you knew 

# 5056

that this indeed is a noble Qur'an,

# 5057

inscribed in a well-guarded Book,

# 5058

which none but the pure may touch;

# 5059

a revelation from the Lord of the Universe.

# 5060

Do you, then, take this discourse in light esteem,

# 5061

and your portion in it is simply that you denounce it as false?

# 5062

Why, then, when the soul leaps up to the throat,

# 5063

the while you are helplessly watching that he is on the verge of death,

# 5064

 at that moment when We are closer to him than you, although you do not see (Us)

# 5065

if you are not subject to anyone's authority,

# 5066

why are you then not able to bring them back to life if you are truthful?

# 5067

So if he is one of those who are near-stationed (to Allah),

# 5068

then happiness and delight and Gardens of Bliss are his.

# 5069

And if he is one of the People on the Right,

# 5070

he will be welcomed by the words: Peace to you from the People on the Right.

# 5071

And if he is one of those who give the lie (to this Message) and go astray,

# 5072

then he will be served boiling water,

# 5073

and will be scorched by the Fire.

# 5074

That indeed is the absolute truth.

# 5075

So glorify the name of your Great Lord.

# 5076

All that is in the heavens and the earth extols the glory of Allah. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5077

His is the dominion of the heavens and the earth. He gives life and causes death, and He has power over everything.

# 5078

He is the First and the Last, and the Manifest and the Hidden, and He has knowledge of everything.

# 5079

He it is Who created the heavens and the earth in six days and then established Himself on the Throne. He knows all that enters the earth and all that comes forth from it, and all that comes down from the heaven and all that goes up to it. He is with you wherever you are. Allah sees all that you do.

# 5080

His is the dominion of the heavens and the earth, and to Him are all matters referred (for judgement).

# 5081

He causes the night to pass into the day, and causes the day to pass into the night, and He fully knows all that is hidden in the breasts of people.

# 5082

Believe in Allah and in His Messenger and expend of what He has entrusted to you. A great reward awaits those of you who believe and spend their wealth.

# 5083

How is it that you do not believe in Allah when the Messenger calls you to believe in your Lord and although he has taken a covenant from you, if indeed you are believers?

# 5084

He it is Who sends down Clear Signs to His servant so as to bring you out from darkness into light. Surely Allah is Most Kind and Most Compassionate to you.

# 5085

How is it that you do not expend in the Way of Allah when to Allah belongs the inheritance of the heavens and the earth? Those who spent their wealth and took part in fighting before the Victory cannot be equated (with those who spent their wealth and took part in fighting afterwards). They are higher in rank than those who spent and fought afterwards. But to each Allah has promised a good reward. Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 5086

Who is it that will give Allah a beautiful loan? A loan that Allah will repay after increasing it many times and grant him a generous reward.

# 5087

On that Day you will see believing men and women that their light will be running before them and on their right hands. (They will be told): A good tiding to you today. There shall be Gardens beneath which rivers flow; therein they shall abide. That indeed is the great triumph.

# 5088

On that Day the hypocrites, both men and women, shall say to the believers: Look at us that we may extract some light from your light. They will be told: Go back and seek light for yourselves elsewhere. Then a wall shall be erected between them with a door in it. On the inside of it there will be mercy, and on the outside of it there will be chastisement.

# 5089

The hypocrites will call out to the believers: Were we not with you? The believers will reply: Yes; but you allowed yourselves to succumb to temptations, and you wavered and you remained in doubt and false expectations deluded you until Allah's command came to pass, and the Deluder deluded you concerning Allah.

# 5090

So no ransom shall be accepted from you today, nor from those who disbelieved. You are destined for the Fire. That will be your guardian. And that indeed is a grievous destination.

# 5091

Is the time not come that the hearts of the believers should be humbled to Allah's remembrance and to the Truth that He has revealed, and that they should not be like those who were vouchsafed the Book and then a long time elapsed so that their hearts were hardened? A great many of them are now evil-doers.

# 5092

Know well that Allah revives the earth after it becomes lifeless. We have clearly shown Our Signs to you, perchance you will use your reason.

# 5093

Verily those who give alms -- be they men or women, -- and give Allah a beautiful loan shall be repaid after increasing it many times; and theirs shall be a generous reward.

# 5094

In Allah's sight only those who truly believe in Allah and His Messengers are utterly truthful and true bearers of witness (for the sake of Allah). For them is their reward and their light. As for those who gave the lie to Our Signs, they are the people of Hell.

# 5095

Know well that the life of this world is merely sport and diversion and adornment and an object of your boasting with one another, and a rivalry in the multiplication of riches and children. Its likeness is that of rain: when it produces vegetation it delights the tillers. But then it withers and you see it turn yellow, and then it crumbles away. In the Hereafter there is (either) grievous chastisement (or) forgiveness from Allah and (His) good pleasure. The life of this world is nothing but delusion.

# 5096

So vie with one another in seeking to attain your Lord's forgiveness and a Garden whose width is as the width of the heaven and the earth, one which has been prepared for those who believe in Allah and His Messengers. That is Allah's bounty which He bestows upon those whom He pleases. Allah is the Lord of abounding bounty.

# 5097

No misfortune ever befalls on earth, nor on yourselves but We have inscribed it in the Book before We make it manifest. Surely that is easy for Allah.

# 5098

(We do so) that you may not grieve over the loss you suffer, nor exult over what He gave you. Allah does not love the vainglorious, the boastful,

# 5099

those who are niggardly and bid others to be niggardly. And he who turns away, (should know that) Allah is Self-Sufficient, Immensely Praiseworthy.

# 5100

Indeed We sent Our Messengers with Clear Signs, and sent down with them the Book and the Balance that people may uphold justice. And We sent down iron, wherein there is awesome power and many benefits for people, so that Allah may know who, without even having seen Him, helps Him and His Messengers. Surely Allah is Most Strong, Most Mighty.

# 5101

Indeed We sent forth Noah and Abraham and established in their line Prophecy and the Book. Then some of them embraced the guidance and many of them are wicked.

# 5102

In their wake, We sent a succession of Our Messengers, and raised Jesus, son of Mary, after all of them, and bestowed upon him the Evangel, and We set tenderness and mercy in the hearts of those that followed him. As for monasticism, it is they who invented it; We did not prescribe it for them. They themselves invented it in pursuit of Allah's good pleasure, and then they did not observe it as it ought to have been observed. So We gave their reward to those of them that believed. But many of them are wicked.

# 5103

Believers, have fear of Allah and believe in His Messenger, and He will grant you a two-fold portion of His Mercy, and will appoint for you a light whereby you shall walk; and He will forgive you. Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5104

(You should do this) so that the People of the Book know that they have no control over Allah's Bounty, and that all bounty is in Allah's Hand; He bestows it on whomsoever He pleases. Allah is the Lord of abounding bounty.

# 5105

Allah has surely heard the words of her who contends with you concerning her husband and complains to Allah. Allah hears what both of you say. Verily Allah is All- Hearing, All-Seeing.

# 5106

Those among you who divorce their wives by declaring them to be their mothers, such are not their mothers; none are their mothers except those who gave birth to them. Indeed what they say is highly contemptible and false. Verily Allah is Most Pardoning, Most Forgiving.

# 5107

Those who declare their wives to be their mothers and thereafter go back on what they have said shall free a slave before they may touch each other. That is what you are exhorted to do. Allah is fully aware of all your deeds.

# 5108

And he who does not find a slave (to free), shall fast for two months consecutively before they may touch each other; and he who is unable to do so shall feed sixty needy people. All this is in order that you may truly believe in Allah and His Messenger. These are the bounds set by Allah; and a grievous chastisement awaits the unbelievers.

# 5109

Verily those who oppose Allah and His Messenger shall be brought low even as those before them were brought low. Surely We have sent down Clear Signs; and a humiliating chastisement awaits the unbelievers;

# 5110

a chastisement that shall come upon them on the Day when Allah will raise them all to a new life and will inform them of their deeds. Allah has recorded it all while they have forgotten it. Allah is a witness over everything.

# 5111

Are you not aware that Allah knows whatever is in the heavens and whatever is in the earth? Never is there any whispering among three but He is their fourth; nor among five but He is their sixth; nor fewer nor more but He is with them wherever they may be. And then He will tell them on the Day of Judgement all that they have done. Surely Allah knows everything.

# 5112

Have you not seen those who were forbidden to whisper and yet they engaged in what they had been forbidden? They secretly converse among themselves concerning sin and transgression and disobedience to the Messenger. And when they come to you, they greet you in a manner that Allah does not greet you, and say to themselves: Why does Allah not chastise us for these utterances of ours? Hell it is that shall suffice them, and in it will they burn. How woeful is their destination!

# 5113

Believers, when you converse in secrecy, let that not be concerning sin and transgression and disobedience to the Messenger; rather, converse concerning virtue and piety. And fear Allah to Whom all of you shall be mustered.

# 5114

Whispering is an act of Satan, one that aims at causing grief to the believers; yet without Allah's leave no harm can be caused to them. So in Allah should the believers put all their trust.

# 5115

Believers, when you are told: Make room for one another in your assemblies, then make room; Allah will bestow amplitude on you. And when it is said: Rise up, then rise up; Allah will raise to high ranks those of you who believe and are endowed with knowledge. Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 5116

Believers, when you come to the Messenger for private consultation, offer some charity before your consultation with him. That is better for you and more conducive to purity. But if you find nothing to offer in charity, then know that Allah is Most Merciful, Most Compassionate.

# 5117

Are you afraid that you will have to offer charity when you hold private conversation with the Prophet? But if you are unable to do so and Allah pardons you, then establish Prayer and pay Zakah, and obey Allah and His Messenger. Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 5118

Do you not see those who took for friends a people whom Allah is wroth with? They neither belong to you nor you to them. They swear to a falsehood, and they do so knowingly.

# 5119

Allah has prepared for them a grievous chastisement. Indeed, evil are the acts in which they are engaged.

# 5120

They have taken their oaths as a shield by means of which they hinder people from the Way of Allah. Theirs shall be a humiliating chastisement.

# 5121

Neither their possessions nor their offspring will be of any avail to them against Allah. They are the people of the Fire; therein they shall abide.

# 5122

On the Day when Allah will raise them all from the dead they will swear before Him as they swear before you today, thinking that this will avail them. Behold, they are utter liars.

# 5123

Satan has gained mastery over them and has made them neglect remembering Allah. They are the party of Satan. Behold, the party of Satan will be the losers.

# 5124

Verily those who oppose Allah and His Messenger will be among the most abject beings.

# 5125

Allah has written: Surely I will prevail; I and My Messengers. Verily Allah is Most Strong, Most Mighty.

# 5126

You shall not find a people who believe in Allah and the Last Day befriending those who oppose Allah and His Messenger even though they be their fathers or their sons or their brothers or their kindred. He has inscribed faith in their hearts and has strengthened them with a spirit from Him, and He shall make them enter Gardens beneath which rivers flow. Therein they shall abide. Allah is well-pleased with them, and they are well-pleased with Him. They belong to Allah's party. Verily Allah's party shall prosper.

# 5127

All that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth extols Allah's Glory: He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5128

He it is Who in the first assault drove forth the People of the Book that disbelieved from their homes at the first gathering of forces. You did not believe that they would leave; while they too thought that their fortresses would defend them against Allah. Then Allah came upon them from whence they did not even imagine, casting such terror into their hearts that they destroyed their homes by their own hands and their destruction was also caused by the hands of the believers. So learn a lesson from this, O you who have perceptive eyes!

# 5129

If Allah had not decreed banishment for them, He would certainly have chastised them in this world. As for the Hereafter, the chastisement of the Fire awaits them.

# 5130

That is because they set themselves against Allah and His Messenger; and whoever sets himself against Allah should know that Allah is surely Most Stern in retribution.

# 5131

The palm-trees that you cut down or those that you left standing on their roots, it was by Allah's leave that you did so. (Allah granted you this leave) in order that He might humiliate the evil-doers.

# 5132

Whatever Allah has taken away from them and bestowed (as spoils) on His Messenger for which you spurred neither horses nor camels; but Allah grants authority to His Messengers over whomsoever He pleases. Allah has power over everything.

# 5133

Whatever (from the possessions of the towns people) Allah has bestowed on His Messenger belongs to Allah, and to the Messenger, and to his kinsfolk, and to the orphans, and to the needy, and to the wayfarer so that it may not merely circulate between the rich among you. So accept whatever the Messenger gives you, and refrain from whatever he forbids you. And fear Allah: verily Allah is Most Stern in retribution.

# 5134

It also belongs to the poor Emigrants who have been driven out of their homes and their possessions, those who seek Allah's favour and good pleasure and help Allah and His Messenger. Such are the truthful ones.

# 5135

It also belongs to those who were already settled in this abode (of Hijrah) having come to faith before the (arrival of the) Muhajirun (Emigrants). They love those who have migrated to them and do not covet what has been given them; they even prefer them above themselves though poverty be their own lot. And whosoever are preserved from their own greed, such are the ones that will prosper.

# 5136

(And it also belongs to) those who came after them, and who pray: Lord, forgive us and our brethren who have preceded us in faith, and do not put in our hearts any rancour towards those who believe. Lord, You are the Most Tender, the Most Compassionate.

# 5137

Did you not see the hypocrites say to their brethren, the unbelievers among the People of the Book: If you are banished we too will go with you and will not listen to anyone concerning you; and if war is waged against you, we will come to your aid. But Allah bears witness that they are liars.

# 5138

To be sure, if they are banished, they will not go with them and if war is waged against them, they will not aid them; and even if they provide any aid to them, they will still turn their backs, and thereafter no aid will be forthcoming to them.

# 5139

Surely they have greater dread for you in their hearts than for Allah. That is because they are a people who are devoid of understanding.

# 5140

They will never fight against you as a body (in an open battlefield); and if they fight against you they will fight only in fortified townships or from behind walls. Intense is their hostility to one another. You reckon them united while their hearts are divided. That is because they are a people devoid of reason.

# 5141

They are like those who tasted the evil consequences of their deeds a short while before. A grievous chastisement awaits them.

# 5142

Their parable is that of Satan when he says to man: Disbelieve, but when he disbelieves, he says: I am quit of you. Verily I fear Allah, the Lord of the Universe.

# 5143

In the end both will be in the Fire, and will abide in it. That is the recompense of the wrong-doers.

# 5144

Believers, fear Allah and let every person look to what he sends forward for the morrow. Fear Allah; Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 5145

And be not like those who forgot Allah and so He made them oblivious of themselves. They are the wicked ones.

# 5146

Those destined for the Fire and those destined for Paradise cannot be alike. Verily it is those destined for Paradise who shall triumph.

# 5147

Had We sent down this Qur'an upon a mountain you would indeed have seen it humbling itself and breaking asunder out of fear of Allah. We propound such parables to people that they may reflect.

# 5148

He is Allah: there is no god but He; the Knower of the unseen and the manifest, He is the Most Merciful, the Most Compassionate.

# 5149

He is Allah: there is no god but He: the King, the Holy, the All-Peace, the Giver of security, the Overseer, the Most Mighty, the Overpowering, the All-Great. Exalted be He from whatever they associate with Him.

# 5150

He is Allah, the Planner, Executer and Fashioner of creation. His are the names most beautiful. Whatever is in the heavens and the earth extols His Glory. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5151

Believers, if you have left (your homes and) have come forth to struggle in My Way and to seek My good pleasure, do not make friends with My enemies and your enemies. You befriend them whereas they have spurned the Truth that has come to you; and (such is their enmity that) they expel the Messenger and yourselves for no other reason than that you believe in Allah, your Lord. You send to them messages of friendship in secrecy, although I know well whatever you do, be it secretly or publicly. And whosoever of you does so has indeed strayed far away from the Straight Path.

# 5152

If they could overcome you, they would act as your foes and would hurt you by their hands and tongues, and would love to see you become unbelievers.

# 5153

On the Day of Resurrection neither your blood-kindred nor your own offspring will avail you. (On that Day) He will separate you. Allah sees all that you do.

# 5154

You have a good example in Abraham and his companions: they said to their people: We totally dissociate ourselves from you, and from the deities that you worship instead of Allah. We renounce you and there has come to be enmity and hatred between us and you until you believe in Allah, the One True God. (But you may not emulate) Abraham's saying to his father: Certainly I will ask pardon for you, although I have no power over Allah to obtain anything on your behalf. (And Abraham and his companions prayed): Our Lord, in You have we put our trust, and to You have we turned, and to You is our ultimate return.

# 5155

Our Lord, do not make us a test for the unbelievers, and forgive us, our Lord. Surely You are Most Mighty, Most Wise.

# 5156

Indeed there is a good example for you in them; a good example for anyone who looks forward to Allah and the Last Day. As for him who turns away, Allah is All-Sufficient, Immensely Praiseworthy.

# 5157

It may well be that Allah will implant love between you and those with whom you have had enmity. Allah is Most Powerful; and Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5158

Allah does not forbid that you be kind and just to those who did not fight against you on account of religion, nor drove you out of your homes. Surely Allah loves those who are equitable.

# 5159

Allah only forbids you to be friends with those who have fought against you on account of religion and who have driven you out of your homes and have abetted in your expulsion. And any who make friends with them, they are the wrong-doers.

# 5160

Believers, when believing women come to you as Emigrants (in the cause of faith), examine them. Allah fully knows (the truth) concerning their faith. And when you have ascertained them to be believing women, do not send them back to the unbelievers. Those women are no longer lawful to the unbelievers, nor are those unbelievers lawful to those (believing) women. Give their unbelieving husbands whatever they have spent (as bridal-dues); and there is no offence for you to marry those women if you give them their bridal-dues. Do not hold on to your marriages with unbelieving women: ask for the return of the bridal-due you gave to your unbelieving wives and the unbelievers may ask for the return of the bridal-due they had given to their believing wives. Such is Allah's command. He judges between you. Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.

# 5161
