And if you fail to receive from the unbelievers a part of the bridal-due of your disbelieving wives, and then your turn comes, pay to those who have been left on the other side an amount the like of the bridal-due that they have paid. And have fear of Allah in Whom you believe.

# 5162

O Prophet, when believing women come to you and pledge to you that they will not associate aught with Allah in His Divinity, that they will not steal, that they will not commit illicit sexual intercourse, that they will not kill their children, that they will not bring forth a calumny between their hands and feet, and that they will not disobey you in anything known to be good, then accept their allegiance and ask Allah to forgive them. Surely Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5163

Believers, do not make friends with those against whom Allah is wrathful and who are despaired of the Hereafter, as despaired as are the unbelievers lying in their graves.

# 5164

All that is in the heavens and all that is on earth extols Allah's glory. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5165

Believers, why do you profess that which you do not practise?

# 5166

It is most loathsome in the sight of Allah that you should profess what you do not practise.

# 5167

Allah indeed loves those who fight in His Way as though they are a solid wall cemented with molten lead.

# 5168

And call to mind when Moses said to his people: O my people, why do you torment me when you know well that I am Allah's Messenger to you? So when they deviated, Allah made their hearts deviant. Allah does not direct the evil-doers to the Right Way.

# 5169

And call to mind when Jesus, son of Mary, said: O Children of Israel, I am Allah's Messenger to you, I verify the Torah which has come before me, and I give you the glad tiding of a Messenger who shall come after me, his name being Ahmad. Yet when he came to them with Clear Signs they said: This is sheer trickery.

# 5170

Who would be more unjust than he who invents a lie about Allah the while he is being called to Islam? Allah does not direct such evildoing folk to the Right Way.

# 5171

They seek to extinguish Allah's light (by blowing) with their mouths, but Allah shall spread His light in all its fullness, howsoever the unbelievers may abhor this.

# 5172

He it is Who has sent forth the Messenger with the Guidance and the True Religion that He may make it prevail over all religion, however those that associate aught with Allah in His Divinity might dislike this.

# 5173

Believers, shall I direct you to a commerce that will deliver you from a grievous chastisement?

# 5174

Have faith in Allah and His Messenger and strive in the Way of Allah with your possessions and your lives. That is better for you if you only knew.

# 5175

He will forgive you your sins and will admit you to Gardens beneath which rivers flow. He will lodge you in excellent mansions in the Gardens of eternity. That is the supreme triumph.

# 5176

He will also grant you the other favour that you desire: help from Allah and a victory that will come soon. Give glad tidings of this to the believers.

# 5177

Believers, become Allah's helpers, as Jesus, son of Mary, said to the disciples: Who is my helper in (calling people) to Allah? The disciples had responded by saying: We are Allah's helpers. Then a section of the Children of Israel believed and a section rejected the call. Thereafter We aided the believers against their enemies, and they prevailed.

# 5178

All that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth extols the glory of Allah, the Sovereign, the Holy, the All- Mighty, the All-Wise.

# 5179

He it is Who has sent to the gentiles a Messenger from among themselves, one who rehearses to them His verses, purifies their lives, and imparts to them the Book and the Wisdom although before that they were in utter error;

# 5180

and (He has also) sent him to those others who have not yet joined them. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5181

Such is Allah's favour: He bestows it on whomsoever He pleases. Allah is the Lord of abounding favour.

# 5182

The parable of those who were charged with the Torah and then they failed to live up to it is that of a donkey laden with books. Even more evil is the parable of the people who gave the lie to the Signs of Allah. Allah does not direct such wrong-doers to the Right Way.

# 5183

Tell them: O you who have become Judaised, if you arrogantly fancy that you are Allah's favourites to the exclusion of all people, then wish for death, if you are truthful in your claim.

# 5184

But they shall never wish for death because of the (evil) deeds they have committed. Allah is well aware of these evil-doers.

# 5185

Tell them: The death from which you flee will certainly overtake you. Then you will be returned to Him Who fully knows what is hidden and what is manifest. Thereupon He will let you know all that you used to do.

# 5186

Believers, when the call for Prayer is made on Friday, hasten to the remembrance of Allah and give up all trading. That is better for you, if you only knew.

# 5187

But when the Prayer is ended, disperse in the land and seek Allah's Bounty, and remember Allah much so that you may prosper.

# 5188

Yet no sooner than they saw some trading or amusement, they flocked to it and left you standing by yourself. Tell them: That which is with Allah is far better than amusement and trading. Allah is the Best Provider of sustenance.

# 5189

(O Prophet), when the hypocrites come to you, they say: We bear witness that you are certainly Allah's Messenger. Allah certainly knows that you are His Messenger. But Allah also bears witness that the hypocrites are utter liars!

# 5190

They shelter behind their oath, and thus hinder their own selves and others from the Path of Allah. Evil indeed is what they do.

# 5191

All that is because they first believed and then disbelieved, and therefore a seal was set on their hearts; as a result they understand nothing.

# 5192

When you look at them, their persons are pleasing, and when they speak, you pay heed to what they say. But in truth they are (merely) beams of timber propped-up (against a wall). They consider every shout they hear to be directed against them. They are your utter enemies; guard against them. May Allah do away with them! How are they being turned away (from the Truth)?

# 5193

When it is said to them: Come, Allah's Messenger will seek forgiveness for you, they (contemptuously) shake their heads and you see them holding back in pride.

# 5194

It is all the same for them whether you ask forgiveness for them or not; for Allah shall never forgive them. Surely Allah does not direct the transgressing folk to the Right Way.

# 5195

It is they who say: Give nothing to those who are with the Messenger of Allah so that they may disperse. (They say so although) the treasures of the heavens and the earth belong to Allah. But the hypocrites do not understand.

# 5196

They say: When we return to Madinah, the honourable ones will drive out from it those that are abject. In truth, all honour belongs to Allah, and to His Messenger, and to the believers. But the hypocrites do not know.

# 5197

Believers, let your possessions and your offspring not make you negligent of Allah's remembrance. For whoso does that, they will be the losers.

# 5198

And spend of what Allah has granted you by way of sustenance before death should come to any of you and he should say: Lord, why did You not defer my return for a while so that I might give alms and be among the righteous?

# 5199

But when a person's term comes to an end, Allah never grants any respite. Allah is well aware of all that you do.

# 5200

All that is in the heavens and all that is in the earth extols Allah's glory. His is the sovereignty and to Him is all praise due; He has power over everything.

# 5201

He it is Who has created you: and among you are those that deny the Truth and among you are those that believe in it. Allah observes all that you do.

# 5202

He created the heavens and the earth with Truth and shaped you, giving you excellent shapes. And to Him is your ultimate return.

# 5203

He knows what is in the heavens and the earth, and knows what you conceal and what you disclose. Allah even knows what lies hidden in the breasts of people.

# 5204

Has the news of the unbelievers of the past not reached you? (They disbelieved) and then tasted its evil consequence. A grievous chastisement awaits them.

# 5205

This was because their Messengers would come to them with Clear Signs, but they would say: Shall mortals (like ourselves) guide us to the Right Way? They rejected the Truth and turned away. Thereupon Allah became unconcerned with them, for Allah is Self-Sufficient, Innately Praiseworthy.

# 5206

The unbelievers have vehemently contended that they shall not be raised to life. Say to them: Yes, by my Lord, you shall surely be raised to life, and you shall certainly be fully informed of all that you did. That is easy enough for Allah.

# 5207

So believe in Allah and in His Messenger and in the Light that We have sent down. Allah is fully aware of what you do.

# 5208

(You shall come to know that) when He will assemble you on the Day of Gathering. That shall be the Day (to determine) mutual gains and losses. Whoever believes in Allah and acts righteously, Allah will have his evil deeds expunged and will admit him to Gardens beneath which rivers flow. Therein they shall abide forever. That is the supreme triumph.

# 5209

As for those who disbelieved and gave the lie to Our Signs: they shall be the inmates of the Fire, and will abide in it. That is a woeful resort!

# 5210

No misfortune ever befalls unless it be by Allah's leave. And whosoever has faith in Allah, Allah directs his heart along the Right Path. Allah has knowledge of everything.

# 5211

Obey Allah and obey the Messenger. But if you turn away from obedience, (then know that) Our Messenger has no other duty than to clearly convey the Truth.

# 5212

Allah there is no god but He; in Allah should the believers put all their trust.

# 5213

Believers, there are enemies to you from among your spouses and your off-spring, so beware of them. But if you forgive and overlook their offences and pardon them, then surely Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5214

Your possessions and your offspring are nothing but a trial for you. And there awaits a great reward for you with Allah.

# 5215

So hold Allah in awe as much as you can, and listen and obey, and be charitable. This is for your own good. And whoever remains safe from his own greediness, it is such that will prosper.

# 5216

If you give Allah a goodly loan, He will increase it for you several fold and will forgive you. Allah is Most Appreciative, Most Forbearing.

# 5217

He knows that which is beyond the ken of perception as well as that which can be perceived. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Wise.

# 5218

O Prophet, when you divorce women, divorce them for their waiting-period, and compute the waiting period accurately, and hold Allah, your Lord, in awe. Do not turn them out of their homes (during the waiting period)  nor should they go away (from their homes)  unless they have committed a manifestly evil deed. Such are the bounds set by Allah; and he who transgresses the bounds set by Allah commits a wrong against himself. You do not know: maybe Allah will cause something to happen to pave the way (for reconciliation).

# 5219

And when they reach the end of their term (of waiting), then either honourably retain them (in the bond of wedlock) or honourably part with them, and call two persons of known probity as witnesses from among yourselves, and (let these witnesses) give upright testimony for the sake of Allah. That is to what all those that believe in Allah and the Last Day are exhorted. Allah will find a way out for him who fears Allah,

# 5220

and will provide him sustenance from whence he never even imagined. Whoever puts his trust in Allah, He shall suffice him. Surely Allah brings about what He decrees; Allah has set a measure for everything.

# 5221

The waiting period of those of your women who have lost all expectation of menstruation shall be three months in case you entertain any doubt; and the same shall apply to those who have not yet menstruated. As for pregnant women, their waiting period shall be until the delivery of their burden. Allah will create ease for him who fears Allah.

# 5222

This is the commandment of Allah that He has revealed to you. Whoever fears Allah, He will expunge his evil deeds and will richly reward him.

# 5223

(During the waiting period) lodge them according to your means wherever you dwell, and do not harass them to make them miserable. And if they are pregnant, provide for them maintenance until they have delivered their burden. And if they suckle your offspring whom they bore you, then give them due recompense, and graciously settle the question of compensation between yourselves by mutual understanding. But if you experience difficulty (in determining the compensation for suckling) then let another woman suckle the child.

# 5224

Whoever has abundant means, let him spend according to his means; and he whose means are straitened, let him spend out of what Allah has given him. Allah does not burden any human being beyond the means that He has bestowed upon him. Possibly Allah will grant ease after hardship.

# 5225

How many towns rebelled against the commandment of their Lord and His Messengers. Then We called them to a stern accounting, and subjected them to a harrowing chastisement.

# 5226

So they tasted the evil fruit of their deeds; and the fruit of their deeds was utter loss.

# 5227

Allah has laid in store for them a grievous chastisement. So fear Allah, O people of understanding who have attained to faith. Allah has sent down to you an Exhortation,

# 5228

a Messenger who rehearses to you Allah's verses that clearly expound the Guidance so that He may bring out those that believe and act righteously, from every kind of darkness into light. He will admit whosoever believes in Allah and acts righteously to Gardens beneath which rivers flow. They shall abide in them forever. For such has Allah made an excellent provision.

# 5229

Allah it is He Who created seven heavens, and, like them, the earth. His commandment descends among them. (All this is being stated so that you know) that Allah has power over everything, and that Allah encompasses all things in His knowledge.

# 5230

O Prophet, why do you forbid what Allah has made lawful for you? Is it to please your wives? Allah is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5231

Allah has prescribed for you a way for the absolution of your oaths. Allah is your Guardian. He is All-Knowing, Most Wise.

# 5232

The Prophet confided something to one of his wives and then she disclosed it (to another); so after Allah revealed to the Prophet (that she had disclosed that secret), he made a part of it known to her and passed over a part of it. And when he told her about this (i.e., that she had disclosed the secret entrusted to her), she asked: Who informed you of this? He said: I was told of it by He Who is All-Knowing, All-Aware.

# 5233

If the two of you turn in repentance to Allah (that is better for you), for the hearts of both of you have swerved from the Straight Path. But if you support one another against the Prophet, then surely Allah is his Protector; and after that Gabriel and all righteous believers and the angels are all his supporters.

# 5234

Maybe if he were to divorce you, your Lord might grant him in exchange wives better than you  those who truly submit to Allah, are full of faith, obedient, disposed to repentance, and given to worship and fasting  both previously wedded ones and virgins.

# 5235

Believers, guard yourselves and your kindred against a Fire whose fuel is human beings and stones, a Fire held in the charge of fierce and stern angels who never disobey what He has commanded them, and always do what they are bidden.

# 5236

(It will then be said): Unbelievers, make no excuses today. You are being recompensed for nothing else but your deeds.

# 5237

Believers, turn to Allah in sincere repentance; maybe your Lord will expunge your evil deeds and admit you to the Gardens beneath which rivers flow. This will be on the Day when Allah will not disgrace the Prophet and those who have embraced faith and are with him; their light will be running before them and on their right hands, and they will say: Our Lord, perfect for us our light and forgive us. Surely You have power over everything.

# 5238

O Prophet, strive against the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and be severe with them. Hell shall be their resort. What a grievous end!

# 5239

Allah has set forth for the unbelievers the parable of the wives of Noah and Lot. They were wedded to two of Our righteous servants, but each acted treacherously with her husband, and their husbands could be of no avail to them against Allah. The two of them were told: Enter the Fire with all the others who enter it.

# 5240

Allah has set forth for the believers the parable of Pharaoh's wife. She prayed: My Lord, build for me a house with You in Paradise and deliver me from Pharaoh and his misdeeds; and deliver me from the iniquitous people.

# 5241

Allah has also set forth the parable of Mary, the daughter of Imran, who guarded her chastity, and into whom We breathed of Our Spirit, and who testified to the words of her Lord and His Books. She was among the obedient.

# 5242

Blessed is He in Whose Hand is the dominion of the Universe, and Who has power over everything;

# 5243

Who created death and life that He might try you as to which of you is better in deed. He is the Most Mighty, the Most Forgiving;

# 5244

Who created the seven heavens one upon another. You will see no incongruity in the Merciful One's creation. Turn your vision again, can you see any flaw?

# 5245

Then turn your vision again, and then again; in the end your vision will come back to you, worn out and frustrated.

# 5246

We have adorned the lower heaven with lamps, and have made them a means to drive away the satans. We have prepared for them the chastisement of the Blazing Fire.

# 5247

The chastisement of Hell awaits those who disbelieve in their Lord. What a wretched destination!

# 5248

When they will be cast into it, they will hear it roar as it boils,

# 5249

as though it will burst with rage. Every time a multitude is cast into it, its keepers will ask them: Did no warner come to you?

# 5250

They will say: Yes, a warner came to us, but we gave the lie to him and said: 'Allah has revealed nothing. You are surely in huge error.'

# 5251

They will say: 'If we had only listened and understood, we would not be among the inmates of the Blazing Fire.'

# 5252

Thus will they confess their sins. Damned are these inmates of the Blazing Fire.

# 5253

Surely forgiveness and a mighty reward await those who fear Allah without seeing Him.

# 5254

Whether you speak in secrecy or aloud, (it is all the same to Allah). He even knows the secrets that lie hidden in the breasts of people.

# 5255

Would He not know, He Who has created, when He is All-Subtle, All-Aware?

# 5256

He it is Who made the earth subservient to you. So traverse in its tracks and partake of the sustenance He has provided. To Him will you be resurrected.

# 5257

Do you feel secure that He Who is in the heaven will not cause the earth to cave in with you, and then suddenly it will begin to rock violently?

# 5258

Do you feel secure that He Who is in the heaven will not let loose upon you a storm of stones? Then shall you know what My warning is like!

# 5259

Those who came before them also gave the lie (to the Messengers): then how awesome was My chastisement!

# 5260

Have they not seen birds above them spreading and closing their wings, with none holding them except the Merciful One? He oversees everything.

# 5261

Which is your army that will come to your aid against the Merciful Lord? But the unbelievers are in utter delusion.

# 5262

Who shall provide for you if He withholds His sustenance? Nay; but they persist in rebellion and aversion.

# 5263

Who is better guided: he who walks grovelling on his face, or he who walks upright on a Straight Path?

# 5264

Say: He it is Who has brought you into being, and has given you hearing and sight, and has given you hearts to think and understand. How seldom do you give thanks!

# 5265

Say: Allah it is Who multiplied you in the earth and to Him you will be mustered.

# 5266

They say: If you are truthful, tell us when will this promise (of the Hereafter) be fulfilled?

# 5267

Say: Allah alone knows about that; and I am no more than a plain warner.

# 5268

When they will see it near at hand, the faces of all those who had denied it will be distraught, and then they will be told: This is the doom which you used to ask for.

# 5269

Say to them: Did you ever consider: whether Allah destroys me and those that are with me, or shows mercy to us, who can protect the unbelievers from a grievous chastisement?

# 5270

Say to them: He is Merciful, and it is in Him that we believe, and it is in Him that we put all our trust. Soon will you know who is in manifest error.

# 5271

Say to them: Did you even consider: if all the water that you have (in the wells) were to sink down into the depths of the earth, who will produce for you clear, flowing water?

# 5272

Nun. By the pen and what the scribes write.

# 5273

By your Lord's Grace, you are not afflicted with madness,

# 5274

and surely yours shall be a never-ending reward,

# 5275

and you are certainly on the most exalted standard of moral excellence.

# 5276

So you will soon see, and they too will see,

# 5277

which of you is afflicted with madness.

# 5278

Surely your Lord knows well those who have strayed from His Way just as He knows well those who are on the Right Way.

# 5279

Do not, then, yield to those who reject the Truth, decrying it as false;

# 5280

they would wish you to be pliant so that they too may be pliant.

# 5281

And do not yield to any contemptible swearer,

# 5282

the fault-finder who goes around slandering,

# 5283

the hinderer of good, the transgressor, the sinful;

# 5284

the coarse-grained, and above all mean and ignoble;

# 5285

(who so acts) simply because he has wealth and sons,

# 5286

and whenever Our verses are rehearsed to him, he says: These are fairy- tales of times gone by.

# 5287

Soon shall We brand him on his snout.

# 5288

We have put them \[i.e., the Makkans\] to test even as We put to test the owners of the orchard when they vowed that they would gather the fruit of their orchard in the morning,

# 5289

without making any allowance (for the will of Allah).

# 5290

Thereupon a calamity from your Lord passed over it while they were asleep,

# 5291

and so by morning the orchard lay as though it had been fully harvested.

# 5292

At daybreak they called out to one another:

# 5293

Hurry to your orchard if you would gather its fruit.

# 5294

So off they went, whispering to one another:

# 5295

No destitute person shall enter it today.

# 5296

They went forth early, believing that they had the power (to gather the fruit).

# 5297

But as soon as they beheld the orchard, (they cried out): We have certainly lost the way;

# 5298

rather, we are utterly ruined.

# 5299

The best among them said: Did I not say to you: why do you not give glory to (your Lord)?

# 5300

They cried out: Glory be to our Lord! Certainly we were sinners.

# 5301

Then they began to reproach one another.

# 5302

They said: Woe to us! We had indeed transgressed.

# 5303

Maybe our Lord will give us a better orchard in its place; to our Lord do we penitently turn.

# 5304

Such is the chastisement; and the chastisement of the Hereafter is assuredly even greater, if only they knew.

# 5305

Surely the God-fearing shall have Gardens of bliss with their Lord.

# 5306

What! Shall We treat those who have submitted (to Our command) like those who have acted as criminals?

# 5307

What is the matter with you? How ill do you judge!

# 5308

Or do you have a Book wherein you read

# 5309

that (in the Hereafter) you shall have all that you choose for yourselves?

# 5310

Or have We sworn a covenant with you which We are bound to keep till the Day of Resurrection, (a covenant requiring that whatever you ordain for yourselves shall be yours)?

# 5311

Ask them: Which of them can guarantee that?

# 5312

Or has something been guaranteed by any of those whom they associate with Allah in His Divinity? If so, let them bring forth their associates, if they are truthful.

# 5313

On the Day when the dreadful calamity will unfold, when people will be summoned to prostrate themselves, and yet they will not be able to prostrate.

# 5314

Their eyes shall be downcast and ignominy shall overwhelm them. For when they were safe and sound, they were summoned to prostrate themselves, (and they refused).

# 5315

So leave Me, (O Prophet), to deal with him who gives the lie to this Discourse. We shall draw them little by little (to their undoing) in a way that they will not know.

# 5316

I am giving them a respite. Great is My scheme!

# 5317

Or are you asking them for some compensation so that they feel burdened with debt?

# 5318

Or do they have any knowledge of the Unseen which they are now writing down?

# 5319

So bear with patience until the Judgement of your Lord comes, and do not belike the man in the fish (i.e., Jonah) who called out, choking with grief:

# 5320

had his Lord not bestowed His favour upon him, he would have been cast upon that barren shore (and would have remained there) in disgrace.

# 5321

But his Lord exalted him, and included him among His righteous servants.

# 5322

When the unbelievers hear this Exhortation, they look at you as though they would knock you off your feet with their (hostile) glances. They say: Surely he is afflicted with madness;

# 5323

although this is nothing but an Exhortation (to goodness) for everyone in the world.

# 5324

The indubitable event!

# 5325

And what is that indubitable event?

# 5326

And what do you know what that indubitable event is?

# 5327

The Thamud and the Ad denied the (possibility of a) sudden calamity, calling it false.

# 5328

Then the Thamud were destroyed by an awesome upheaval;

# 5329

and the Ad were destroyed by a furiously raging wind-storm

# 5330

which He let loose upon them for seven nights and eight days in succession; so that (if you had been there) you might have seen people lying prostrate, as though they were uprooted trunks of hollowed palm trees.

# 5331

Do you now see any trace of them?

# 5332

Pharaoh and those before him and the people of the overturned habitations all engaged in the same great sin.

# 5333

They did not follow the Messenger of their Lord, and so He seized them with a severe grip.

# 5334

Verily when the water rose to great heights, We bore you upon a floating vessel (i.e. the Ark)

# 5335

so that We might make it an instructive event for you, and retentive ears might preserve its memory.

# 5336

So when the Trumpet is blown with a single blast

# 5337

and the earth and the mountains are carried aloft and are crushed to bits at one stroke,

# 5338

on that Day shall that indubitable event come to pass;

# 5339

when the sky will be rent asunder, the grip holding it together having loosened on that Day,

# 5340

and the angels will stand on the sides, with eight of them bearing aloft the Throne of your Lord on that Day.

# 5341

That will be the Day when you shall be brought forth (before Allah) and no secret of yours shall remain hidden.

# 5342

On that Day, he whose Record is given to him in his right hand will say: Lo! Read my Record!

# 5343

Verily I was sure that I would be handed over my account.

# 5344

Then he shall find himself in a life of bliss;

# 5345

in a lofty Garden

# 5346

the clusters of whose fruit will be hanging low to be within reach (of the inmates of Paradise).

# 5347

(They will be told): Eat and drink with good cheer as a reward for the good deeds you did in the days that have passed by.

# 5348

As for him whose Record will be given to him in his left hand, he will exclaim: Would that I had never been given my Record,

# 5349

and had not known my account.

# 5350

Oh! Would that the death that came to me in the world had made an end of me!

# 5351

My riches have not availed me,

# 5352

and my authority has vanished.

# 5353

(A command will be issued): Seize him and shackle him,

# 5354

then cast him in the Fire,

# 5355

then fasten him with a chain, seventy cubits long.

# 5356

He would not believe in Allah, the Most Great;

# 5357

nor would he urge the feeding of the poor.

# 5358

Today he has been left here friendless;

# 5359

and has no food except the filth from the washing of wounds,

# 5360

which only the sinners will eat.

# 5361

But no; I swear by what you see,

# 5362

and by what you do not see,

# 5363

that this is the speech of an honourable Messenger,

# 5364

not the speech of a poet. Little do you believe!

# 5365

Nor is this the speech of a soothsayer. Little do you reflect!

# 5366

It has been revealed by the Lord of the Universe.

# 5367

And if he \[i.e., the Prophets\] had forged this Discourse and thereafter ascribed it to Us,

# 5368

We would surely have seized him by the right hand,

# 5369

and then severed his life vein;

# 5370

and not one of you would have been able to withhold Us from doing so.

# 5371

Surely it is a Good Counsel for the God-fearing.

# 5372

We certainly know that some among you will give the lie to it,

# 5373

and surely it will be a cause of regret for the unbelievers.

# 5374

Certainly it is a Truth of absolute certainty.

# 5375

So glorify the name of your Lord Most Great.

# 5376

A beseecher besought the visitation of chastisement,

# 5377

(a chastisement meant) for the unbelievers, one which none can avert;

# 5378

a chastisement from Allah, the Lord of the ascending steps,

# 5379

by which the angels and the Spirit ascend to Him in one Day the duration of which is fifty thousand years.

# 5380

So, (O Prophet), persevere with gracious perseverance.

# 5381

Verily they think that the chastisement is far off,

# 5382

while We think that it is near at hand.

# 5383

It shall befall on a Day whereon the sky will become like molten brass,

# 5384

and the mountains will become like dyed tufts of wool,

# 5385

and no bosom friend will enquire about any of his bosom friends

# 5386

although they shall be within sight of one another. The guilty one would fain ransom himself from the torment of that Day by offering his children,

# 5387

and his spouse and his brother,

# 5388

and his kinsfolk who had stood by him,

# 5389

and all persons of the earth, if only he could thus save himself.

# 5390

By no means! It will be the fierce flame

# 5391

that will strip off the scalp.

# 5392

It shall insistently summon him who turned his back and retreated,

# 5393

and amassed wealth and covetously hoarded it.

# 5394

Verily man is impatient by nature:

# 5395

bewailing when evil befalls him,

# 5396

and tight-fisted when good fortune visits him,

# 5397

except those that pray,

# 5398

and are constant in their Prayer;

# 5399

and those in whose wealth there is a known right

# 5400

for those that ask and those that are dispossessed,

# 5401

those who firmly believe in the Day of Recompense,

# 5402

and fear the chastisement of their Lord 

# 5403

surely the chastisement of their Lord is a thing none can feel secure from 

# 5404

and those who guard their private parts,

# 5405

except in regard to their spouses and those whom their right hands possess, for in regard to them they are not reproachable,

# 5406

but any who seeks to go beyond that, it is indeed they who are the transgressors,

# 5407

and those who fulfil their trusts and their covenants,

# 5408

and those who are upright in their testimonies;

# 5409

and who take due care of their Prayer:

# 5410

all these shall live honourably in the Gardens.

# 5411

But what is the matter with the unbelievers who are hurrying towards you

# 5412

in crowds, both on the right and on the left?

# 5413

Does everyone of them wish to enter the Garden of Bliss?

# 5414

By no means! They know that which We have created them from.

# 5415

I swear by the Lord of the easts and the wests that We have the power

# 5416

to replace them by others who would be better than they; and We shall certainly not be overpowered.

# 5417

So leave them to engage in vain talk and to amuse themselves until they come face to face with the Day which they are promised,

# 5418

the Day on which they will hastily come forth from their graves, as though they were hurrying on to the altars of their deities.

# 5419

Their eyes will be downcast and disgrace will overwhelm them. Such is the Day that they were promised.

# 5420

We sent Noah to his people (and directed him): Warn your people before a grievous chastisement comes upon them.

# 5421

Noah said: My people, I have certainly been sent as a clear warner to you,

# 5422

that you serve Allah and fear Him, and follow me;

# 5423

He will forgive your sins and will grant you respite until an appointed term. Indeed when Allah's appointed term comes, it cannot be deferred; if you only knew!

# 5424

He said: My Lord, I called my people by night and by day,

# 5425

but the more I called, the farther they fled.

# 5426

And every time I called them so that You might forgive them, they thrust their fingers into their ears and wrapped up their faces with their garments and obstinately clung to their attitude, and waxed very proud.

# 5427

Then I summoned them openly,

# 5428

and preached to them in public, and also addressed them in secret.

# 5429

I said to them: Ask forgiveness from your Lord; surely He is Most Forgiving.

# 5430

He will shower upon you torrents from heaven,

# 5431

and will provide you with wealth and children, and will bestow upon you gardens and rivers.

# 5432

What is amiss with you that you do not look forward to the majesty of Allah

# 5433

when He has created you in stages?

# 5434

Do you not see how Allah has created seven heavens, one upon the other,

# 5435

and has placed the moon in them as a light, and the sun as a radiant lamp?

# 5436

And Allah has caused you to grow out of the earth so wondrously,

# 5437

and He will later cause you to return to it and will then again bring you out of it.

# 5438

Allah has made the earth a wide expanse for you

# 5439

so that you may tread its spacious paths.

# 5440

Noah said: My Lord, they did not pay heed to what I said, and followed those (nobles) whose possession of wealth and children has led them to an even greater loss.

# 5441

They contrived a plot of great magnitude.

# 5442

They said: Do not abandon your deities; do not abandon Wadd, nor Suwa, nor Yaghuth, nor Yauq, nor Nasr.

# 5443

They have misled many. So do not enable these evildoers to increase in anything except straying (from the Right Way).

# 5444

And so they were drowned on account of their sins, and then cast into the Fire, and did not find any other than Allah, to come forth to their help.

# 5445

Noah said: My Lord, do not leave out of these unbelievers even a single dweller on earth,

# 5446

for certainly if You should leave them (alive), they will mislead Your servants, and will beget none but sinners and utter unbelievers.

# 5447

My Lord, forgive me and my parents, and whoever enters my house as a believer, and forgive all believers, both men and women, and do not increase the wrong-doers in anything except perdition.

# 5448

Say, (O Prophet), it was revealed to me that a band of jinn attentively listened to (the recitation of the Qur'an) and then (went back to their people) and said:

# 5449

We have indeed heard a wonderful Qur'an which guides to the Right Way; so we have come to believe in it, and we will not associate aught with Our Lord in His Divinity;

# 5450

and that He  exalted be His Majesty  has not taken to Himself either a wife or a son;

# 5451

and that the foolish among us have been wont to say outrageous things about Allah;

# 5452

and that we had thought that men and jinn would never speak a lie about Allah,

# 5453

and that some from among the humans used to seek protection of some among the jinn, and thus they increased the arrogance of the jinn;

# 5454

and that they thought, even as you thought, that Allah would never raise anyone (as a Messenger);

# 5455

and that we tried to pry (the secrets of) the heaven, but we found it full of terrible guards and shooting meteors;

# 5456

and that we would take up stations in the heaven to try to hear but anyone who now attempts to listen finds a shooting meteor in wait for him;

# 5457

and that we do not know whether evil is intended for those on the earth, or whether their Lord intends to direct them to the Right Way;

# 5458

and that some of us are upright and some of us are otherwise for we follow widely divergent paths;

# 5459

and that we thought that we will neither be able to frustrate Allah on earth, nor frustrate Him by flight;

# 5460

and that when we heard the teaching of the Right Way we came to believe in it; he who believes in His Lord shall have no fear of suffering loss or being subjected to any injustice;

# 5461

and that among us some are Muslims (Those who have submitted to Allah), and some of us are deviant. So those who became Muslims found the Right Course;

# 5462

but those who deviated from the Truth, will be the fuel for Hell.

# 5463

If people were to keep firmly to the Right Way, We would have vouchsafed them abundant rain

# 5464

so that We might try them through this bounty. Whoso turns away from the remembrance of his Lord, He will cause him to suffer a grievous chastisement;

# 5465

and that mosques belong to Allah, so do not invoke anyone with Him;

# 5466

and when Allah's servant stood up to call on Him, they well-nigh swarmed him.

# 5467

Say, (O Prophet): I call on my Lord alone, and I do not associate aught with Him in His Divinity.

# 5468

Say: Surely neither it is in my power to hurt you nor to bring you to the Right Way.

# 5469

Say: None can protect me from Allah, nor can I find a refuge apart from Him.

# 5470

(My task is no more than) to deliver Allah's proclamation and His messages. And whoever disobeys Allah and His Messenger, surely the Fire of Hell awaits him; therein he will abide in perpetuity.

# 5471

(They shall not change their ways) until they see that against which they had been warned, and then they will know whose helpers are weaker and whose supporters are fewer in number.

# 5472

Say: I know not whether what you are promised is near or whether my Lord will prolong its term.

# 5473

He is the Knower of the Unseen, and He does not disclose His Unseen to anyone

# 5474

other than to a Messenger whom He chooses (for the bestowal of any part of the knowledge of the Unseen), whereafter He appoints guards who go before him and behind him,

# 5475

so that He may know that they have delivered the messages of their Lord. He encompasses in His knowledge their surroundings and keeps a count of all things.

# 5476

O you the (sleeping) enwrapped one!

# 5477

Stand up in Prayer by night, all but a small part of it;

# 5478

half of it, or reduce it a little;

# 5479

or add to it a little; and recite the Qur'an slowly and distinctly.

# 5480

Behold, We shall cast upon you a Weighty Word.

# 5481

Surely getting up at night is the best means of subduing the self and is more suitable for uprightness in speech.

# 5482

You are indeed much occupied during the day with the affairs of the world.

# 5483

So remember the name of your Lord and devote yourself to Him with exclusive devotion.

# 5484

He is the Lord of the East and the West; there is no god but He. So take Him alone for your Guardian,

# 5485

And bear patiently the vain things they utter, and gracefully forsake them.

# 5486

Leave it to Me to deal with the affluent ones who give the lie (to the Truth), and bear with them for a while.

# 5487

We have heavy fetters and a blazing Fire in store for them;

# 5488

and a food that chokes, and a grievous chastisement.

# 5489

(They will come across all this) on the Day when the earth and the mountains shall tremble violently and the mountains shall crumble into heaps of scattered sand.

# 5490

Surely We have sent to you a Messenger as a witness over you, just as We had sent a Messenger to Pharaoh.

# 5491

But Pharaoh disobeyed Our Messenger, so We seized him with a terrible seizing.

# 5492

If you persist in disbelieving, how will you guard yourself against the (woe of the) Day that will turn children grey-haired,

# 5493

the Day whose severity shall cause the heaven to split asunder? Allah's promise is ever bound to be fulfilled.

# 5494

Indeed this is nothing but a Good Counsel; so let him who will take a way leading to his Lord.

# 5495

(O Prophet), your Lord knows that you sometimes stand up in Prayer nearly two-thirds of the night, and sometimes half or one-third of it, and so does a party of those with you; Allah measures the night and the day. He knows that you cannot keep an accurate count of it, so He has shown mercy to you. So now recite as much of the Qur'an as you can. He knows that there are among you those who are sick and others who are journeying in the land in quest of Allah's bounty, and still others who are fighting in the cause of Allah. So recite as much of the Qur'an as you easily can, and establish Prayer, and pay Zakah, and give Allah a goodly loan. Whatever good you send forth for yourselves, you shall find it with Allah. That is better and its reward is greater. And ask for Allah's forgiveness; surely He is Most Forgiving, Most Compassionate.

# 5496

O you enveloped in your cloak!

# 5497

Arise, and warn,

# 5498

and magnify the glory of your Lord,

# 5499

and purify your robes,

# 5500

and shun uncleanness,

# 5501

and bestow not favour in order to seek from others a greater return,

# 5502

and persevere for your Lord's sake.

# 5503

When the Trumpet shall be sounded,

# 5504

that will surely be a hard day,

# 5505

not an easy day for the unbelievers.

# 5506

Leave Me with him whom I alone have created,

# 5507

whom I have endowed with abundant riches,

# 5508

and sons ever present with him,

# 5509

and for whom I have smoothed the way (to power and riches),

# 5510

and who still greedily desires that I should bestow upon him more.

# 5511

By no means; he is stubbornly opposed to Our Signs.

# 5512

I shall soon constrain him to a hard ascent.

# 5513

He reflected and then hatched a scheme.

# 5514

Ruin seize him, how did he hatch a scheme?

# 5515

Again, ruin seize him, how did he hatch a scheme?

# 5516

He looked (at others);

# 5517

then frowned and scowled;

# 5518

then he retreated and waxed proud,

# 5519

and said: This (Qur'an) is merely a sorcery of yore;

# 5520

this is nothing but the word of a mere mortal!

# 5521

Him shall I soon roast in Hell.

# 5522

And what do you know what Hell is?

# 5523

It spares nothing; it leaves nothing intact;

# 5524

it scorches (even) the skin.

# 5525

Over it are nineteen keepers.

# 5526

We have appointed none but angels as the keepers of the Fire, and We have not made their number but as a trial for the unbelievers so that those who have been endowed with the Book will be convinced and the believers' faith will increase, and neither those who have been endowed with the Book nor the believers will fall into any doubt. As for those in whose hearts there is a sickness as well as the unbelievers, they will say: What did Allah aim at by this strange parable? Thus does Allah let whomsoever He pleases to go astray, and directs whomsoever He pleases to the Right Way. And none knows the hosts of your Lord but He. (And Hell has only been mentioned here) that people may take heed.

# 5527

Nay, by the moon,

# 5528

and by the night when it recedes,

# 5529

and by the day when it dawns (with its radiance),

# 5530

surely (Hell) is one of the greatest Signs,

# 5531

a warning to humankind,

# 5532

a warning to everyone of you whether he would like to come forward or lag behind.

# 5533

Each one is a hostage to one's deeds,

# 5534

save the People of the Right Hand

# 5535

who shall be in the Gardens, and shall ask

# 5536

about the guilty ones:

# 5537

What drove you to Hell?

# 5538

They will answer: We were not among those who observed Prayer,

# 5539

and we did not feed the poor,

# 5540

and we indulged in vain talk with those who indulged in vain talk,

# 5541

and we gave the lie to the Day of Judgement

# 5542

until the inevitable event overtook us.

# 5543

The intercession of the intercessors shall then be of no avail to them.

# 5544

What is the matter with people that they are turning away from this Exhortation,

# 5545

as though they were frightened wild asses,

# 5546

fleeing from a lion?

# 5547

No indeed; each one of them desires that open letters be sent to each of them.

# 5548

No indeed; the truth is that they have no fear of the Hereafter.

# 5549

Nay; this is an Exhortation.

# 5550

So, whoever wills may benefit from it.

# 5551

But they will not benefit from it unless Allah Himself so wills. He is worthy to be feared; and He is worthy to forgive (those that fear Him).

# 5552

Nay, I swear by the Day of Resurrection;

# 5553

and nay, I swear by the self-reproaching soul!

# 5554

Does man imagine that We will not be able to bring his bones together again?

# 5555

Yes indeed; We have the power to remould even his finger-tips.

# 5556

But man desires to persist in his evil ways.

# 5557

He asks: When will the Day of Resurrection be?

# 5558

When the sight is dazed,

# 5559

and the moon is eclipsed,

# 5560

and the sun and the moon are joined together,

# 5561

on that Day will man say: Whither the refuge?

# 5562

No, there is no refuge.

# 5563

With your Lord alone will be the retreat that Day.

# 5564

On that Day will man be apprised of his deeds, both the earlier and the later.

# 5565

But lo, man is well aware of himself,

# 5566

even though he might make up excuses.

# 5567

(O Prophet), do not stir your tongue hastily (to commit the Revelation to memory).

# 5568

Surely it is for Us to have you commit it to memory and to recite it.

# 5569

And so when We recite it, follow its recitation attentively;

# 5570

then it will be for Us to explain it.

# 5571

Nay; the truth is that you love ardently (the good of this world) that can be obtained hastily,

# 5572

and are oblivious of the Hereafter.

# 5573

Some faces on that Day will be fresh and resplendent,

# 5574

and will be looking towards their Lord;

# 5575

and some faces on that Day will be gloomy,

# 5576

believing that a crushing calamity is about to strike them.

# 5577

Nay; when a man's soul reaches up to the throat,

# 5578

and it is said: Is there any enchanter who can step forward and help (by his chanting)?

# 5579

and he realises that the hour of parting is come,

# 5580

and calf is inter-twined with calf.

# 5581

On that Day you will be driven to your Lord.

# 5582

But he did not verify the Truth, nor did he observe Prayer;

# 5583

on the contrary, he gave the lie to the Truth and turned his back upon it,

# 5584

then he went back to his kinsfolk, elated with pride.

# 5585

This (attitude) is worthy of you, altogether worthy;

# 5586

again, it is worthy of you, altogether worthy.

# 5587

Does man think that he will be left alone, unquestioned?

# 5588

Was he not a drop of ejaculated semen,

# 5589

then he became a clot, and then Allah made it into a living body and proportioned its parts,

# 5590

and then He made of him a pair, male and female?

# 5591

Does He, then, not have the power to bring back the dead to life?

# 5592

Was there a period of time when man was not even worthy of a mention?

# 5593

Verily We created man out of a drop of intermingled sperm so that We might try him, and We therefore endowed him with hearing and sight.

# 5594

Surely We showed him the Right Path, regardless of whether he chooses to be thankful or unthankful (to his Lord).

# 5595

For the unbelievers, We have kept ready chains and fetters and a Blazing Fire.

# 5596

The virtuous shall drink from a cup tempered with camphor water.

# 5597

This will be a gushing spring wherefrom Allah's servants shall drink wine, a spring from which they will take out channels wherever they wish.

# 5598

These will be the ones who fulfil their vows and dread the Day whose woe shall be spread far and wide;

# 5599

those who, for the love of Him, feed the needy, and the orphan, and the captive,

# 5600

(saying): We feed you only for Allah's sake; we do not seek of you any recompense or thanks,

# 5601

we fear from our Lord a Day that shall be long and distressful.

# 5602

So Allah shall guard them against the woe of that Day, and will procure them freshness and joy,

# 5603

and will reward them for their steadfastness with Paradise and robes of silk.

# 5604

There they will recline on elevated couches and will be subjected neither to the burning heat of the sun nor to bitter cold.

# 5605

The shades of Paradise will bend over them, and its fruits will be brought within their easy reach;

# 5606

and there shall be passed around them vessels of silver and goblets of crystal,

# 5607

goblets bright as crystal but made of silver, filled to exact measure.

# 5608

Therein they shall be served a cup flavoured with ginger,

# 5609

drawn from a spring (in Paradise) called Salsabil.

# 5610

There boys of everlasting youth shall go about attending them: when you see them, you would think that they are scattered pearls.

# 5611

Whitherto you look around, you will see an abundance of bliss and the glories of a great kingdom.

# 5612

They \[i.e., the virtuous\] shall be attired in garments of fine green silk and rich brocade and will be adorned with bracelets of silver. Their Lord will give them a pure wine to drink.

# 5613

Behold, this is your recompense and your endeavour has been appreciated.

# 5614

(O Prophet), indeed We have revealed the Qur'an to you in portions.

# 5615

So persevere with the command of your Lord and do not pay any heed to the wicked and the unbelieving,

# 5616

and remember the name of your Lord, morning and evening;

# 5617

and prostrate yourself before Him at night, and extol His Glory during the long watches of the night.

# 5618

Verily they love (the good of this world) that is hastily obtainable and are oblivious of the burdensome Day ahead of them.

# 5619

We created them and strengthened their joints; and whenever We wish, We can change their faces entirely.

# 5620

Verily this is an Exhortation; so let him who so will take a way to his Lord.

# 5621

But your willing shall be of no avail until Allah Himself so wills. Surely Allah is All-Knowing, Most Wise.

# 5622

He admits to His Mercy whomsoever He pleases. As for the wrong-doers, He has prepared for them a grievous chastisement.

# 5623

By the (winds) sent forth in quick succession,

# 5624

which then blow tempestuously

# 5625

and raise (clouds) and scatter them around,

# 5626

then winnow them thoroughly,

# 5627

and then cast (Allah's) remembrance (in people's hearts),

# 5628

to serve as an excuse or a warning.

# 5629

Surely what you are promised shall come to pass.

# 5630

So when the stars are extinguished,

# 5631

and the sky is rent asunder,

# 5632

and the mountains are blown away,

# 5633

and the appointed time to bring the Messengers together arrives, (then shall the promised event come to pass).

# 5634

To which Day has this task been deferred?

# 5635

To the Day of Judgement.

# 5636

What do you know what the Day of Judgement is?

# 5637

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5638

Did We not destroy many a nation of the earlier times?

# 5639

And We shall cause those of later times to follow them.

# 5640

Thus do We deal with the guilty.

# 5641

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5642

Did We not create you of a mean fluid,

# 5643

which We then placed in a secure repository

# 5644

until an appointed time?

# 5645

See that We had the power to do so. Great indeed is Our power to do what We will.

# 5646

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5647

Did We not make the earth a receptacle,

# 5648

for the living and the dead,

# 5649

and did We not firmly fix towering mountains on it and give you sweet water to drink?

# 5650

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5651

Proceed now towards that which you were wont to deny as false;

# 5652

proceed towards the three-pronged shadow,

# 5653

which neither provides (cooling) shade nor protection against the flames;

# 5654

it indeed throws up sparks like castles,

# 5655

which seem as though they are yellow-coloured camels.

# 5656

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5657

That will be the Day on which they will not (be able to) utter a word,

# 5658

nor will they be allowed to proffer excuses.

# 5659

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5660

That is the Day of Judgement on which We have assembled you as well as all those who went before you.

# 5661

So if you have any ploy, try it against Me!

# 5662

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5663

Behold, today the God-fearing will be amidst shades and springs,

# 5664

and the fruits that they desire (will be ready at hand).

# 5665

Eat and drink and may every joy attend you as a reward for your deeds.

# 5666

Thus do We reward those that do good.

# 5667

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5668

Eat and enjoy yourselves for a while. Surely you are evil-doers.

# 5669

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5670

When it is said to them: Bow down (before Allah), they do not bow down.

# 5671

Woe on that Day to those that give the lie to the Truth!

# 5672

In what discourse after this (Qur'an) will they, then, believe?

# 5673

About what are they asking one another?

# 5674

Is it about the awesome tiding

# 5675

that they are in utter disagreement?

# 5676

No indeed; soon will they come to know;

# 5677

again, no indeed; soon will they come to know.

# 5678

Have We not spread the earth like a bed,

# 5679

and fixed the mountains like pegs,

# 5680

and created you in pairs (as men and women),

# 5681

and made your sleep a means of repose,

# 5682

and made the night a covering,

# 5683

and made the day to seek livelihood,

# 5684

and built above you seven strong firmaments,

# 5685

and placed therein a hot, shining lamp,

# 5686

and sent down abundant water from the clouds

# 5687

so that We may thereby bring forth grain and vegetation,

# 5688

and gardens dense with foliage?

# 5689

Surely the Day of Judgement has an appointed time;

# 5690

the Day when the Trumpet shall be blown, and you will come forth in multitudes;

# 5691

and when the sky shall be opened up and will become all doors;

# 5692

and the mountains will be set in motion and become a mirage.

# 5693

Surely the Hell is an ambush,

# 5694

a resort for the rebellious;

# 5695

therein they shall abide for ages,

# 5696

they shall taste in it no coolness, nor any pleasant drink

# 5697

save boiling water and wash of the wounds;

# 5698

a befitting recompense for their deeds.

# 5699

For indeed they did not look forward to any reckoning,

# 5700

and roundly denied Our Signs as false.

# 5701

And everything have We recorded in a Book.

# 5702

So taste (the fruit of your deeds). We shall only increase your torment.

# 5703

Surely the state of triumph awaits the God-fearing:

# 5704

gardens and vineyards,

# 5705

and youthful maidens of like age,

# 5706

and an overflowing cup.

# 5707

Therein they shall hear no idle talk, nor any falsehood;

# 5708

a recompense from your Lord and an ample reward

# 5709

from the Lord of the heavens and the earth and of that which is between them; the Most Merciful Lord before Whom none dare utter a word.

# 5710

The Day when the Spirit and the angels are ranged row on row. None shall speak save he whom the Merciful Lord will permit; and he too will speak what is right.

# 5711

That Day is sure to come. So let him who will seek a resort with his Lord.

# 5712

Lo! We warn you of a chastisement near at hand; the Day when a man will look on what his own hands have sent forth, and the unbelievers shall say: Oh would that I were utter dust.

# 5713

By those (angels) that pluck out the soul from depths,

# 5714

and gently take it away;

# 5715

and by those that speedily glide along (the cosmos),

# 5716

and vie with the others (in carrying out their Lord's behests);

# 5717

and then manage the affairs of the Universe (according to their Lord's commands).

# 5718

The Day when the quaking will cause a violent convulsion,

# 5719

and will be followed by another quaking.

# 5720

On that Day some hearts shall tremble (with fright),

# 5721

and their eyes shall be downcast with dread.

# 5722

They say: Shall we indeed be restored to life,

# 5723

even after we have been reduced to bones, hollow and rotten?

# 5724

They say: That will then be a return with a great loss!

# 5725

Surely they will need no more than a single stern blast,

# 5726

and lo, they will all be in the open plain.

# 5727

Has Moses' story reached you?

# 5728

When his Lord called him in the sacred valley of Tuwa,

# 5729

and directed him: Go to Pharaoh, he has rebelled,

# 5730

and say to him: 'Are you willing to be purified,

# 5731

that I may direct you to your Lord and then you hold Him in awe?'

# 5732

Then Moses (went to Pharaoh and) showed him the Great Sign;

# 5733

but he denied it as false and disobeyed,

# 5734

and then he turned back to have recourse to his craftiness,

# 5735

and gathered his people and declared:

# 5736

I am the supreme lord of you all.

# 5737

Thereupon Allah seized him for the chastisement of the World to Come as well as of the present.

# 5738

Surely there is a great lesson in it for whoever would fear (Allah).

# 5739

Is it harder to create you or the heaven? But Allah built it,

# 5740

and raised its vault high and proportioned it;

# 5741

and covered its night with darkness and brought forth from it its day;

# 5742

and thereafter spread out the earth,

# 5743

and brought out of it its water and its pasture,

# 5744

and firmly fixed in it mountains;

# 5745

all this as provision for you and your cattle.

# 5746

But when the great calamity will come about

# 5747

on the Day when man will recall all his strivings,

# 5748

and Hell will be brought in sight for anyone to see:

# 5749

then he who transgressed

# 5750

and preferred the life of this world,

# 5751

most surely his abode shall be Hell.

# 5752

But he who feared to stand before his Lord, and restrained himself from evil desires,

# 5753

most surely his abode shall be Paradise.

# 5754

They ask you about the Hour: When will it be?

# 5755

What concern do you have to speak about that?

# 5756

Its knowledge rests with your Lord.

# 5757

You are only a warner to him who has a fear of it.

# 5758

On the Day they see it, they will feel as though they had stayed (in the grave) no more than one evening or one morning.

# 5759

He frowned and turned away

# 5760

that the blind man came to him.

# 5761

How could you know? Perhaps he would cleanse himself,

# 5762

or he might be mindful and good counsel might avail him.

# 5763

Now he who waxes indifferent,

# 5764

you attend to him,

# 5765

though you are not to blame if he would not cleanse himself.

# 5766

But he who comes to you running,

# 5767

and fears (Allah),

# 5768

you pay no heed to him.

# 5769

No indeed; this is only a Reminder.

# 5770

So whoso wills may give heed to it.

# 5771

It is contained in scrolls highly honoured,

# 5772

most exalted and purified,

# 5773

borne by the hands of scribes,

# 5774

noble and purified.

# 5775

Accursed be man! How stubbornly he denies the Truth.

# 5776

Out of what did Allah create him?

# 5777

Out of a sperm-drop did He create him and then determined a measure for him,

# 5778

and then made the course of life easy for him,

# 5779

then He caused him to die and brought him to the grave,

# 5780

and then, whenever He wishes, He will raise him back to life.

# 5781

Nay, but man did not fulfil what Allah had enjoined upon him.

# 5782

So let man just consider his food:

# 5783

We poured water, pouring it in great abundance,

# 5784

and cleaved the earth, cleaving it asunder;

# 5785

then caused the grain to grow out of it,

# 5786

together with grapes and vegetables,

# 5787

and olives and palms,

# 5788

and dense orchards,

# 5789

and fruits and pastures 

# 5790

all this as a provision for you and your cattle.

# 5791

But when the deafening cry shall be sounded

# 5792

on the Day when each man shall flee from his brother,

# 5793

and his mother and his father;

# 5794

and his consort and his children;

# 5795

on that Day each will be occupied with his own business, making him oblivious of all save himself.

# 5796

Some faces on that Day shall be beaming with happiness,

# 5797

and be cheerful and joyous.

# 5798

Some faces on that Day shall be dust-ridden,

# 5799

enveloped by darkness.

# 5800

These will be the unbelievers, the wicked.

# 5801

When the sun shall be folded up,

# 5802

when the stars shall scatter away,

# 5803

when the mountains shall be set in motion,

# 5804

when the ten-months pregnant camels shall be abandoned,

# 5805

when the savage beasts shall be brought together,

# 5806

when the seas shall be set boiling,

# 5807

when the souls shall be rejoined (with their bodies),

# 5808

and when the girl-child buried alive shall be asked:

# 5809

for what offence was she killed?

# 5810

and when the scrolls of (men's) deeds shall be unfolded,

# 5811

and when Heaven is laid bare;

# 5812

and Hell is stoked,

# 5813

and Paradise brought nigh:

# 5814

then shall each person know what he has brought along.

# 5815

No indeed; I swear by the alternating stars

# 5816

that hide,

# 5817

and by the night as it recedes,

# 5818

and the morn as it breathes.

# 5819

Verily this is the word of a noble message-bearer;

# 5820

one mighty and held in honour with the Lord of the Throne;

# 5821

there he is obeyed and held trustworthy.

# 5822

(O people of Makkah), your companion is not mad;

# 5823

he indeed saw the message-bearer on the clear horizon;

# 5824

nor does he grudge (conveying this knowledge about) the Unseen;

# 5825

nor is it a word of an accursed Satan.

# 5826

Where to are you then heading?

# 5827

It is nothing but Good Counsel for everyone in the world,

# 5828

for everyone of you who wishes to follow the Straight Way;

# 5829

but your wishing will not avail unless Allah, the Lord of the Universe, so wishes.

# 5830

When the heaven is split asunder,

# 5831

when the stars are scattered,

# 5832

when the seas are made to burst forth,

# 5833

and when graves are laid open,

# 5834

everyone shall know all his deeds, both the earlier and the later.

# 5835

O man! What has deceived you about your generous Lord

# 5836

Who created you, shaped you, and made you well-proportioned,

# 5837

and set you in whatever form He pleased?

# 5838

No indeed; (the fact is that) you deny the Reckoning, declaring it a lie;

# 5839

you do so the while there are watchers over you;

# 5840

noble scribes,

# 5841

who know what you do.

# 5842

Surely the virtuous shall be in Bliss,

# 5843

and the wicked shall be in the Blazing Fire.

# 5844

They shall enter it on the Day of Recompense

# 5845

and then shall never come out of it.

# 5846

What do you know what the Day of Recompense is?

# 5847

Again, what do you know what the Day of Recompense is?

# 5848

It is the Day when no one shall have the power to do anything for another, and all command shall be Allah's.

# 5849

Woe to the stinters;

# 5850

those who, when they take from others by measure, take their full share;

# 5851

but who, when they measure or weigh for others, give less than their due.

# 5852

Do they not realise that they will be raised to life

# 5853

on a Great Day,

# 5854

a Day when mankind will stand before the Lord of the Universe?

# 5855

No indeed! Verily the deeds of the wicked are in the Record locked up in the prison-house!

# 5856

And how would you know what the Record of the prison-house is?

# 5857

It is a Book inscribed.

# 5858

Woe, then, to those that give the lie,

# 5859

those that give the lie to the Day of Recompense.

# 5860

Yet none gives the lie to it except the transgressor immersed in sin;

# 5861

who, when Our verses are recited to him, says: Mere tales of olden times!

# 5862

No indeed! The truth is that their hearts have become rusted on account of their evil deeds.

# 5863

No indeed! On that Day they will be screened off from seeing their Lord,

# 5864

and then they shall enter Hell,

# 5865

whereafter they will be told: This is what you used to give the lie to.

# 5866

No indeed! Verily, the deeds of the virtuous shall be in the record of the exalted ones.

# 5867

And what do you know what the Record of the exalted ones is?

# 5868

It is a Book inscribed,

# 5869

which the angels placed near Allah to safeguard.

# 5870

Verily the virtuous shall be in Bliss;

# 5871

resting on couches, looking around.

# 5872

You shall see upon their faces the glow of bliss.

# 5873

They will be served a drink of the finest sealed wine,

# 5874

whose seal is musk  so let all aspirants aspire after that 

# 5875

a wine whose mixture is Tasnim,

# 5876

a fountain at which the chosen ones shall drink.

# 5877

Behold, the wicked were wont to laugh at the believers:

# 5878

when they passed by them they winked,

# 5879

and when they went back to their families, they went back jesting,

# 5880

and when they saw the believers, they said: Lo! These are the erring ones;

# 5881

(they said so although) they had not been appointed watchers over them.

# 5882

But today the believers are laughing at the unbelievers;

# 5883

seated upon their couches, they are looking around.

# 5884

Have the unbelievers been duly rewarded for their deeds?

# 5885

When the sky is rent asunder

# 5886

and hearkens to the command of its Lord, doing what it should;

# 5887

and when the earth is stretched out

# 5888

and casts out what is within it and is emptied,

# 5889

and hearkens to the command of its Lord, doing what it should.

# 5890

O man, you are striving unto your Lord and you will meet Him.

# 5891

Whoever is given the Record in his right hand

# 5892

shall be called to an easy accounting,

# 5893

and shall return to his people joyfully.

# 5894

But he who is given the Record behind his back,

# 5895

shall cry for perdition,

# 5896

and will enter the Blazing Fire.

# 5897

He used to live joyfully among his people,

# 5898

thinking he would never revert (to Us).

# 5899

But no; (how would he not revert)? His Lord was ever watching him.

# 5900

Nay; I swear by the twilight;

# 5901

and by the night and what it enfolds,

# 5902

and by the moon, when it reaches its fullness:

# 5903

you shall proceed onwards from stage to stage.

# 5904

So, what is the matter with them that they do not believe,

# 5905

and when the Qur'an is recited to them, they do not prostrate themselves?

# 5906

Instead, the unbelievers reject it, calling it a lie.

# 5907

Allah knows best what they are accumulating (in their Record).

# 5908

So give them the good news of a painful chastisement,

# 5909

except for those who believe and do good deeds. Theirs shall be an unending reward.

# 5910

By the heaven with its impregnable castles;

# 5911

by the Promised Day,

# 5912

and by the witness and what is witnessed:

# 5913

the people of the pit were destroyed

# 5914

with fire abounding in fuel,

# 5915

while they sat around it,

# 5916

and were witnessing what they did to the believers.

# 5917

Against these they had no grudge except that they believed in Allah, the Most Mighty, the Most Praiseworthy,

# 5918

to Whom belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth. Allah witnesses everything.

# 5919

Surely those who tormented the believing men and the believing women and then did not repent, theirs shall be the chastisement of Hell, and theirs shall be the chastisement of burning.

# 5920

As for those who believed and acted righteously, theirs shall be Gardens beneath which rivers flow. That is the great triumph.

# 5921

Stern indeed is your Lord's punishment.

# 5922

He it is Who creates for the first time and He it is Who will create again,

# 5923

and He is the Ever Forgiving, the Most Loving

# 5924

 the Lord of the Glorious Throne,

# 5925

the Executor of what He wills.

# 5926

Has the story of the armies reached you,

# 5927

the armies of Pharaoh and Thamud?

# 5928

The unbelievers are indeed engaged in denying it, calling it a lie,

# 5929

although Allah surrounds them.

# 5930

Nay; but this is a glorious Qur'an,

# 5931

inscribed on a well-guarded Tablet.

# 5932

By the heaven, and the night-visitor,

# 5933

what do you know what the night-visitor is?

# 5934

It is the piercing star.

# 5935

There is no living being but there is a protector over it.

# 5936

So let man consider of what he was created.

# 5937

He was created of a gushing fluid,

# 5938

emanating from between the loins and the ribs.

# 5939

Surely He (the Creator) has the power to bring him back (to life).

# 5940

On the Day when man's deepest secrets shall be put to the test

# 5941

he shall have no power, and no helper.

# 5942

By the heaven with its recurring cycle of rain,

# 5943

and by the earth ever bursting with verdure,

# 5944

this (Qur'an) is surely a decisive Word,

# 5945

not a flippant jest.

# 5946

They are devising a guile,

# 5947

and I too am devising a guile.

# 5948

So leave the unbelievers to themselves; respite them awhile.

# 5949

Glorify the name of your Lord, the Most High,

# 5950

Who created all things and fashioned them in good proportion;

# 5951

Who determined and guided them,

# 5952

Who brought forth the pasture,

# 5953

and then made it into a blackish straw.

# 5954

We shall make you recite and then you will not forget,

# 5955

except what Allah should wish. He knows all that is manifest and all that is hidden.

# 5956

We shall ease you to follow the way of Ease.

# 5957

So render good counsel if good counsel will avail.

# 5958

He who fears (Allah) shall heed it,

# 5959

but the wretched will turn away from it.

# 5960

He will be cast into the Great Fire.

# 5961

Then he will neither die in it, nor live.

# 5962

He who purified himself shall prosper,

# 5963

remembering his Lord's name and praying.

# 5964

No; but you prefer the present life,

# 5965

whereas the Hereafter is better and more enduring.

# 5966

This, indeed, was in the ancient Scrolls,

# 5967

the Scrolls of Abraham and Moses.

# 5968

Has the news of the overwhelming event reached you?

# 5969

Some faces that Day shall be downcast with fear,

# 5970

be toiling and worn-out;

# 5971

they shall burn in a Scorching Fire;

# 5972

their drink shall be from a boiling spring.

# 5973

They shall have no food except bitter dry thorns

# 5974

that will neither nourish nor satisfy their hunger.

# 5975

On that very Day some faces shall be radiant with joy,

# 5976

well-pleased with their striving.

# 5977

They will be in a lofty Garden

# 5978

wherein they shall hear no vain talk.

# 5979

In it there shall be a flowing spring,

# 5980

and couches raised high,

# 5981

and goblets laid out,

# 5982

and cushions arrayed in rows,

# 5983

and rich carpets levelled out.

# 5984

Do (these unbelievers) not observe the camels: how they were created?

# 5985

And the sky: how it was raised high?

# 5986

And the mountains: how they were fixed?

# 5987

And the earth: how it was spread out?

# 5988

So render good counsel, for you are simply required to counsel,

# 5989

and are not invested with the authority to compel them.

# 5990

But whoever will turn away (from the Truth),

# 5991

Allah will chastise him with the most terrible chastisement.

# 5992

Surely to Us is their return;

# 5993

and then it is for Us to call them to account.

# 5994

By the dawn,

# 5995

and the ten nights,

# 5996

and the even and the odd,

# 5997

and by the night when it departs.

# 5998

Is there in this an oath for one endowed with understanding?

# 5999

Have you not seen how your Lord dealt with Ad

# 6000

of Iram, known for their lofty columns,

# 6001

the like of whom no nation was ever created in the lands of the world?

# 6002

And how did He deal with Thamud who hewed out rocks in the valley?

# 6003

And with Pharaoh of the tent pegs

# 6004

who transgressed in the countries of the world

# 6005

spreading in them much corruption?

# 6006

Then their Lord unloosed upon them the lash of chastisement.

# 6007

Truly your Lord is ever watchful.

# 6008

As for man, when his Lord tests him by exalting him and bestowing His bounties upon him, he says: My Lord has exalted me.

# 6009

But when He tests him by straitening his sustenance, he says: My Lord has humiliated me.

# 6010

But no; you do not treat the orphan honourably,

# 6011

and do not urge one another to feed the poor,

# 6012

and greedily devour the entire inheritance,

# 6013

and love the riches, loving them ardently.

# 6014

But no; when the earth is ground to powder,

# 6015

and when your Lord appears with rows upon rows of angels,

# 6016

and when Hell is brought near that Day. On that Day will man understand, but of what avail will that understanding be?

# 6017

He will say: Would that I had sent ahead what would be of avail for this life of mine!

# 6018

Then on that Day Allah will chastise as none other can chastise;

# 6019

and Allah will bind as none other can bind.

# 6020

(On the other hand it will be said): O serene soul!

# 6021

Return to your Lord well-pleased (with your blissful destination), well-pleasing (to your Lord).

# 6022

So enter among My (righteous) servants

# 6023

and enter My Paradise.

# 6024

Nay! I swear by this city

# 6025

 this city wherein you have been rendered violable

# 6026

and I swear by the parent and his offspring:

# 6027

Verily We have created man into toil and hardship.

# 6028

Does he think that no one can overpower him?

# 6029

He says: I have squandered enormous wealth.

# 6030

Does he believe that none has seen him?

# 6031

Did We not grant him two eyes,

# 6032

and a tongue and two lips?

# 6033

And did We not show him the two highroads (of good and evil)?

# 6034

But he did not venture to scale the difficult steep.

# 6035

And what do you know what that difficult steep is?

# 6036

It is freeing someone's neck from slavery;

# 6037

or giving food on a day of hunger

# 6038

to an orphan near of kin;

# 6039

or to a destitute lying in dust;

# 6040

and, then besides this, he be one of those who believed, and enjoined upon one another steadfastness and enjoined upon one another compassion.

# 6041

These are the People of the Right Hand.

# 6042

As for those who rejected Our Signs, they are the People of the Left Hand.

# 6043

Upon them shall be a Fire that will hem them in.

# 6044

By the sun and its heat and brightness,

# 6045

and by the moon as it follows it;

# 6046

and by the day as it displays the sun's glory,

# 6047

and by the night as it envelopes the sun;

# 6048

and by the sky and by Him Who made it;

# 6049

and by the earth and by Him Who stretched it out;

# 6050

and by the soul and by Him Who perfectly proportioned it,

# 6051

and imbued it with (the consciousness of) its evil and its piety:

# 6052

He who purifies it will prosper,

# 6053

and he who suppresses it will be ruined.

# 6054

In their presumptuous insolence the Thamud called the Truth a lie

# 6055

when their arch-criminal rose up in rage.

# 6056

Then Allah's Messenger warned them: Hands off the she-camel and her drink!

# 6057

But they rejected his statement as a lie and hamstrung the she-camel. For that crime their Lord rumbled down upon them, utterly razing them to the ground.

# 6058

He has no fear of its sequel.

# 6059

By the night when it enshrouds,

# 6060

and by the day when it breaks in its glory,

# 6061

and by Him Who created the male and the female:

# 6062

surely your strivings are divergent.

# 6063

As for him who gave out his wealth (for Allah's sake) and abstained (from disobeying Him),

# 6064

and affirmed the Truth of goodness:

# 6065

We shall facilitate for him the Way to Bliss.

# 6066

As for him who was a miser and behaved with aversion (to Allah),

# 6067

and denied the Truth of goodness:

# 6068

We shall facilitate for him the way to Hardship,

# 6069

and his wealth shall be of no avail to him when he perishes.

# 6070

Surely it is for Us to show the Right Way,

# 6071

and to Us belong the Next Life and the present.

# 6072

I have now warned you of a Blazing Fire,

# 6073

where none shall burn except the most wicked,

# 6074

who rejected the Truth, calling it falsehood and turned his back on it.

# 6075

But the God-fearing shall be kept away from it,

# 6076

the Godfearing who spends his wealth to purify himself;

# 6077

not as payment for any favours that he received,

# 6078

but only to seek the good pleasure of his Lord Most High.

# 6079

He will surely be well-pleased (with him).

# 6080

By the bright forenoon,

# 6081

and by the night when it covers the world with peace:

# 6082

(O Prophet), your Lord has neither forsaken you, nor is He displeased.

# 6083

Indeed what is to come will be better for you than what has gone by.

# 6084

Verily your Lord will soon give you so amply that you will be well-pleased.

# 6085

Did He not find you an orphan and then gave you shelter?

# 6086

Did He not find you unaware of the Right Way, and then directed you to it?

# 6087

And did He not find you in want, and then enriched you?

# 6088

Therefore, be not harsh with the orphan;

# 6089

and chide not him who asks,

# 6090

and proclaim the bounty of your Lord.

# 6091

(O Prophet), Did We not lay open your breast

# 6092

and relieve you of the burden

# 6093

that had well-nigh broken your back?

# 6094

And did We not exalt your fame?

# 6095

Indeed, there is ease with hardship.

# 6096

Most certainly, there is ease with hardship.

# 6097

So, whenever you are free, strive in devotion,

# 6098

and turn to your Lord with longing.

# 6099

By the fig and the olive;

# 6100

and by the Mount Sinai,

# 6101

and by this city (of Makkah), a haven of peace:

# 6102

surely We created man in the best mould;

# 6103

then We reverted him to the lowest of the low,

# 6104

except those who have faith and do righteous deeds. Theirs is a never ending reward.

# 6105

Who, then, can give the lie to you, (O Prophet), about the Reward and the Punishment?

# 6106

Is not Allah the Greatest of all sovereigns?

# 6107

Recite in the name of your Lord Who created,

# 6108

created man from a clot of congealed blood.

# 6109
